## Overview

Bjorlam in his carriage outside Whiterun

**Bjorlam** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H"), and the [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") [carriage](/wiki/Skyrim:Carriage "Skyrim:Carriage") driver. He can be found near the [Whiterun Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Stables "Skyrim:Whiterun Stables"), and will take you to any of the [hold capitals](/wiki/Skyrim:Cities "Skyrim:Cities") on his carriage, for a fee.

Bjorlam wears a set of farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#000261c0 "Skyrim:Clothes"), a pair of [gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Gloves#000261c1 "Skyrim:Gloves"), and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000261bd "Skyrim:Boots"). He is equipped with an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe").

## Related Quests

- **[Prophet (Dawnguard)](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Prophet (Dawnguard)")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Find and rescue [a Moth Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus") from the [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan").
- **[Prophet (Vampire)](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Vampire) "Skyrim:Prophet (Vampire)")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): The time of prophecy has arrived! Locate [a Moth Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus") for the [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan").

## Dialogue

You can ask him what he knows about Whiterun, to which he'll reply:

:   **What do you know about Whiterun?**
:   *"Well, I know the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") make their home here. Their mead hall, [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr"), is the oldest building in the city. Oh, and there's a nasty feud between two families called the [Gray-Manes](/wiki/Skyrim:Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Gray-Mane") and [Battle-Borns](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle-Born "Skyrim:Battle-Born"). You'll want to be careful there. The rest you can find out by asking the townsfolk. I'd start with the barkeep at [the Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare"), or the castle steward."*

Apart from this, he shares his dialogue with other carriage drivers.

# Skyrim:Bjormund Wind-Strider

## Overview

Bjormund Wind-Strider's corpse

Bjormund Wind-Strider is a dead [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") and former [Crimson Dirk](/wiki/Skyrim:Crimson_Dirks "Skyrim:Crimson Dirks") who is encountered during the quest [Bones for a Crow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bones_for_a_Crow "Skyrim:Bones for a Crow"). His body is found at the very top of the tower at [Arcwind Point](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcwind_Point "Skyrim:Arcwind Point"), at the bottom of the stairs which lead to the book [Withershins](/wiki/Skyrim:Withershins "Skyrim:Withershins"), after the player has battled past the enemies that occupy the tower. When he chased the same bounty as you, [Crowstooth](/wiki/Skyrim:Crowstooth "Skyrim:Crowstooth") killed him. As part of the reward for the quest (any spoils of Crowstooth's), you may take his unique armor.

Bjormund wears the [Dragonbone Mail](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonbone_Mail "Skyrim:Dragonbone Mail"), [Dragonplate Insulated Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonplate_Insulated_Boots "Skyrim:Dragonplate Insulated Boots"), [Dragonplate Insulated Gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonplate_Insulated_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Dragonplate Insulated Gauntlets") and a [Dragonplate Insulated Helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonplate_Insulated_Helmet "Skyrim:Dragonplate Insulated Helmet"), and carries [Nord Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), an [Amulet of Akatosh](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Akatosh "Skyrim:Amulet of Akatosh"), and a random selection of loot.

## Related Quests

- **[Bones for a Crow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bones_for_a_Crow "Skyrim:Bones for a Crow")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Dragon_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Dragon Plate"): Hunt down the Forsworn Crowstooth.

## Bugs

- Bjormund's body may not appear.
- Can appear in High Hrothgar.

Bjornolfr

**Bjornolfr** is a dead [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") found in a hidden Dwemer room at the back of [Hrodulf](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrodulf "Skyrim:Hrodulf")'s [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrodulf%27s_House "Skyrim:Hrodulf's House"). When entering the house, you may hear some [reavers](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver "Skyrim:Reaver") laughing about a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Letter (Dragonborn)") which Bjornolfr wrote to Hrodulf before his death. This letter reveals that Bjornolfr was concerned for his lover, that he wished Hrodulf would return to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), and that he intended to come to Solstheim if that didn't happen. When you find Bjornolfr's body, he carries a [bloodstained letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodstained_Letter "Skyrim:Bloodstained Letter") from Hrodulf warning him not to come there.

Bjornolfr wears [novice robes of Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Novice_Robes_of_Conjuration "Skyrim:Novice Robes of Conjuration"), a [novice hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Novice_Hood "Skyrim:Novice Hood"), and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0006b46c "Skyrim:Boots"). His body is surrounded by a few coins and a [Nordic dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Dagger "Skyrim:Nordic Dagger").

## Related Quests

- **[Hrodulf's Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrodulf%27s_Madness "Skyrim:Hrodulf's Madness")**: Uncover the secret of [Hrodulf's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrodulf%27s_House "Skyrim:Hrodulf's House").

The Black Book in the excavated Kolbjorn Barrow

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read the Black Book *[Filament and Filigree](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Filament_and_Filigree_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Filament and Filigree (book)")* in [Kolbjorn Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolbjorn_Barrow "Skyrim:Kolbjorn Barrow").
2. Make your way through [Apocrypha‎](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha_(Filament_and_Filigree) "Skyrim:Apocrypha (Filament and Filigree)").
3. Learn the Black Book's hidden knowledge and choose your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Dangerous Darkness

You can find the Black Book *[Filament and Filigree](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Filament_and_Filigree_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Filament and Filigree (book)")* in [Kolbjorn Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolbjorn_Barrow "Skyrim:Kolbjorn Barrow"). Defeat [Ahzidal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal_(creature) "Skyrim:Ahzidal (creature)") and enter the standing sarcophagus opposite the gate you entered through. At the end of a rough tunnel you will find the Black Book in a circular chamber. Read the Book to be drawn into Apocrypha.

This area of [Hermaeus Mora](/wiki/Lore:Hermaeus_Mora "Lore:Hermaeus Mora")'s realm consists of a long, straight, dark path with several hovering lights illuminating small patches. Use [Candlelight](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlelight "Skyrim:Candlelight") or a [torch](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch") to light your way, as the darkness will damage your health. Before proceeding, loot the [pod](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Pod "Skyrim:Containers") hidden behind the left-hand statue at the foot of the stairs, as well as the random [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") and the Sneak Skill Book 'Three Thieves' on the table to the right. Then climb the stairs, claim the contents of a second pod to the left of the doors and the [scroll of invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Invisibility "Skyrim:Scroll of Invisibility") beside it. Activate the scrye and deal with two leveled [seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker "Skyrim:Seeker") and one leveled [lurker](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurker "Skyrim:Lurker"), avoiding the whipping tentacles in alternating pools along the path. At the far end of the path, you will climb another set of stairs to a platform, where another leveled lurker will emerge from a pool and attack. After defeating this final foe, climb the last set of stairs to find a [vessel](/wiki/Skyrim:Vessel "Skyrim:Vessel"), a few soul gems on another stone table, and the Black Book *Filament and Filigree*. Read the book to choose your reward, then read it again to return to Kolbjorn Barrow.

### Rewards

Your choice of one of three greater powers:

- [Secret of Strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Secret_of_Strength "Skyrim:Secret of Strength") — Power attacks cost no [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") for 30 seconds.
- [Secret of Arcana](/wiki/Skyrim:Secret_of_Arcana "Skyrim:Secret of Arcana") — Spells cost no [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") for 30 seconds.
- [Secret of Protection](/wiki/Skyrim:Secret_of_Protection "Skyrim:Secret of Protection") — You take half damage for 30 seconds.

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements#Dragonborn "Skyrim:Achievements") is related to this quest:

-  **Hidden Knowledge** (40 points/Bronze)

## Notes

- Other than using a light source, the damage caused by the darkness cannot be avoided by any means, including the [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") [Shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") and the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") command `tgm`.
- You can change the reward at any time by traveling to Solstheim and re-reading the book. This will transport you to Apocrypha near the reward location and you can select a different one.

## Bugs

- The burning sound effect that plays when you go into the darkness might not end.
  - Exiting to the main menu might solve this issue. If not, clearing the game cache should.
  - After you exit Apocrypha, load a different save then reload the auto-save that was just made and this will stop.
  - Your health might continue to deplete as if you're still in the shadows of Apocrypha.
  - Revisiting the Filament and Filigree and waiting to stop burning before leaving to Solstheim can fix this.
  - Transforming into a werewolf/vampire lord and back will cause the sound to stop.
  - Saving the game and loading that save may also fix the issue.

## Quest Stages

| Black Book: Filament and Filigree (DLC2BlackBook06Quest) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I read the Black Book called "Filament and Filigree", and found myself in Hermaeus Mora's realm of Apocrypha. I should uncover the knowledge hidden here, or read the book again to escape. *Objective 10:* Learn the Black Book's hidden knowledge |
| 20 | ☑ | I uncovered the hidden knowledge contained in the Black Book "Filament and Filigree". |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2BlackBook06Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2BlackBook06Quest`.

A Black Book

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Be approached by a [madman](/wiki/Skyrim:Madman "Skyrim:Madman") ranting about a black book.
2. Kill the madman when he turns hostile and find his [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Scribbles_of_a_Madman "Skyrim:Scribbles of a Madman") revealing the book's location.
3. Retrieve the black book from the dungeon.

## Detailed Walkthrough

In your travels across [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") you may come across a [madman](/wiki/Skyrim:Madman "Skyrim:Madman") shouting things related to some [mysterious books](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book (book)"). He has a chance to spawn at several specific spots all over the island of Solstheim as part of a [world interaction](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Black_Book "Skyrim:World Interactions"). After a short conversation your map will be updated with the location of a Black Book and the madman will attack you. After defeating the madman you will need to travel to the location on your map to retrieve the Black Book.

Possible locations you can be sent to include: [Benkongerike](/wiki/Skyrim:Benkongerike "Skyrim:Benkongerike"), [Kolbjorn Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolbjorn_Barrow "Skyrim:Kolbjorn Barrow"), [Raven Rock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine"),[*verification needed — see [talk page](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Black_Book_(quest))*] [Tel Mithryn Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)"), and [White Ridge Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Ridge_Barrow "Skyrim:White Ridge Barrow").

If the madman dies before he finishes the conversation, this quest will not be added unless you read the note on his body.

## Notes

- The madman will not approach you if you have already collected all of the [Black Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book (book)").
- If the book you are sent to collect is the one in [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)"), you will not be able to access it until you've done a number of quests for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth"), so this quest may remain open for a while.

## Bugs

- Reading the madman's note can cause a glitched journal entry sending you to retrieve a book you have already found, for example to Tel Mithryn.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.4, fixes this bug.
  -  Type `SetStage DLC2WE06 200`. This clears the quest and removes the entry.
- After completing or leaving [Filament and Filigree](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Filament_and_Filigree_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: Filament and Filigree (quest)") or [The Sallow Regent](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Sallow_Regent_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Sallow Regent (quest)") you may hear a hissing sound. **?**
  - Reentering the book should remove the sound
- Even if you have collected all of the Black Books, this quest may activate, as the two main quest books are not properly excluded from the list.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Black Book (DLC2WE06) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 50 |  | *Objective 1:* Find the Black Book in <Alias=Dungeon> |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 10, 20, 100, 200, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2WE06 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2WE06`.

# Skyrim:Black Book: The Hidden Twilight (quest)

## Overview

If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project"). Neloth's Black Book

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read the Black Book *[The Hidden Twilight](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Hidden_Twilight_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Hidden Twilight (book)")* in [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)").
2. Make your way through [Apocrypha‎](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha_(The_Hidden_Twilight) "Skyrim:Apocrypha (The Hidden Twilight)").
3. Learn the Black Book's hidden knowledge.
4. Choose your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

There are eight chapters/zones here, so be prepared for a trek. You'll materialize in a room with a platform and two fonts of magicka. A scrye is past the platform, straight ahead. Activate the scrye and the door behind it will open, revealing a book on a pedestal: the next chapter. Before going in, search behind and below the pedestal to find a pod containing loot.

Chapter II starts out as a corridor twisting past fonts of magicka built into the walls of books. When the path opens up, beware two [seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker "Skyrim:Seeker") wandering the room ahead. Dispose of them and grab the [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") on an altar, then head east where a ramp leads up. At the end of the ramp is another scrye. Upon activating the scrye, the bridge below you will curve upwards and peak before receding again and will repeat this cycle indefinitely. The goal is to sprint to the edge of the bridge as it reaches its peak before leaping to the next ledge before it begins its descent. The timing is delicate but if you fall you will land on a grated path that will lead you back up to where you were before. There are two such bridges before reaching the other side.

When you reach solid ground there will be two paths forward. The passage to the left leads to a dead end containing a Font of Stamina near a pod. Just beside there is an altar with at two soul gems. If your [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") skill is above 40 a [Conjure Seeker](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Seeker "Skyrim:Conjure Seeker") spell tome will be present as well. Head back to the top of the ramp and travel down the right hand passage to find the portal to Chapter III.

Chapter III begins at the base of a book pillar. You can go either way but by taking the left route you can temporarily evade the nearby Seeker. Hugging the left wall will bring you to a Font of Stamina along the southeast edge of the book barricade just before the opening into the main chamber. Turn left and round the corner to find a pod in an alcove with some minor loot. Exit the alcove and turn west. Do not try to head for the platform yet as the stairs have to be released by activating the scrye situated above where you stand presently. Face west and turn right. Just outside the entry arch there is a ramp. Climb the ramp until you reach the roof of the entryway where you will find the scrye at the edge of the lattice beneath a floating lantern. Activate it and descend the ramp back down towards the main path.

Dispatch the Seeker as you cross the abyssal waters. Take care as tentacles will lash at you as you cross. There are three soul gems on the platform along the way to the other side.

When you reach the end of the crossing you will find an enclosure with a set of stairs directly to the left of a font of stamina. Dispatch the [lurker](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurker "Skyrim:Lurker") and walk past the font of stamina and up the stairs through the arch facing directly south. From there you can climb a ramp that leads to the scyre which opens the gates to the enclosure. Before moving to the next area, take a right at the bottom of the stairs when you come back down the ramp. You should see two curved tendril-shaped lamps. Pass between them, take a sharp left and then turn south again. You should notice another font of stamina inside a book crevice. Walk towards it and you will find the gate to chapter IV. There is a seeker on the other side so be ready for a fight.

Chapter IV consists of only one small room with nothing but the seeker and a scrye. Activating it opens a gate in chapter V that provides access to a set of five [skill books](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books"), one for each school of [magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Magic "Skyrim:Magic").

Go back to Chapter III and retrace your steps to the gate you opened before entering Chapter IV. The next gate can be opened by a scrye up the ramp to the south-southwest. A seeker is in the maze-like section ahead, so kill it and go east. There is what looks like a dead end up ahead, but as you approach the rest of the corridor telescopically expands outward. There is a pod on the north side just before the newly-visible section of corridor. At the end are Chapter V and Chapter VI.

Choose your new power.

Entering chapter V lands you in front of another seeker. Defeat it and activate the scrye which opens a gate in the northwest corner of the chamber. There you will find *[A Hypothetical Treachery](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Hypothetical_Treachery "Skyrim:A Hypothetical Treachery")*, *[Racial Phylogeny](/wiki/Skyrim:Racial_Phylogeny "Skyrim:Racial Phylogeny")*, *[Breathing Water](/wiki/Skyrim:Breathing_Water "Skyrim:Breathing Water")*, *[Before the Ages of Man](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Ages_of_Man "Skyrim:Before the Ages of Man")*, and *[2920 Hearth Fire v9](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Hearth_Fire,_v9 "Skyrim:2920, Hearth Fire, v9")* resting on an altar next to a pod. Return to Chapter III, turn right, and enter Chapter VI. This area is very small, but leads to both Chapter VII and Chapter VIII. Enter Chapter VII, kill the seeker, and activate yet another scrye to raise a bridge in Chapter VIII. Return to Chapter VI, turn to your left, and enter Chapter VIII.

Upon arrival you will be ambushed by another seeker. Just before you reach the bridge, take a left to find another altar with a few soul gems. Loot the area and return to the crossing. Make preparations here as a lurker will burst from a pool on the left side of the platform opposite where you are standing as you cross the bridge. Depending on your current level, a second lurker may appear from the right pool as well.

Crossing one last bridge lands you at *The Hidden Twilight*, your final destination. Other loot is scattered around the same area, including a vessel, four soul gems (two black and two grand), and three scrolls (a [Scroll of Ebonyflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Ebonyflesh "Skyrim:Scroll of Ebonyflesh"), a [Scroll of Grand Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Grand_Healing "Skyrim:Scroll of Grand Healing"), and a [Scroll of Paralyze](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Paralyze "Skyrim:Scroll of Paralyze")). Upon opening the book, three green orbs will appear in front of you, one for each [reward](#Reward). Choose one, then activate the open book to travel back to Tel Mithryn.

If at a later time you want to change your reward, reread the book and you will be transported to this location again. You will not have to trek through the previous chapters.

### Reward

Your choice of one of three [greater powers](/wiki/Skyrim:Powers#Greater_Powers "Skyrim:Powers"):

- [Mora's Agony](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora%27s_Agony "Skyrim:Mora's Agony") — Summons a field of writhing tentacles that poisons foes.
- [Mora's Grasp](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora%27s_Grasp "Skyrim:Mora's Grasp") — Freezes the target between Oblivion and Tamriel for 30 seconds, making them immune to all damage.
- [Mora's Boon](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora%27s_Boon "Skyrim:Mora's Boon") — Fully restores your [health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health"), [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka"), and [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina").

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements#Dragonborn "Skyrim:Achievements") is related to this quest:

-  **Hidden Knowledge** (40 points/Bronze)

## Bugs

- Mora's Grasp is affected by the Vampirism+Necromage bug, which will permanently cause its duration to be increased by 50% if you take the ability as a vampire with [Necromage](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromage "Skyrim:Necromage"). See the [vampirism's](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampirism "Skyrim:Vampirism") bug list for more info on being a necromage vampire. **?**
  - If can take the perk as a necromage vampire and then later cure yourself of vampirism, you will still retain the 50% longer bonus as long as you never swap it out for one of the other 2 rewards.

| 20 | ☑ | I uncovered the hidden knowledge contained in the Black Book "The Hidden Twilight". |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2BlackBook07Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2BlackBook07Quest`.

# Skyrim:Black Book: The Sallow Regent (quest)

## Overview

The Sallow Regent

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read the Black Book *[The Sallow Regent](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Sallow_Regent_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Sallow Regent (book)")* in [White Ridge Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Ridge_Barrow "Skyrim:White Ridge Barrow").
2. Travel through [Apocrypha‎](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha_(The_Sallow_Regent) "Skyrim:Apocrypha (The Sallow Regent)").
3. Learn the Black Book's hidden knowledge.
4. Choose your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

The darkness inside

After reading The Sallow Regent you will enter a considerably darker region of Apocrypha than most others. Quickly light a torch or cast a spell of Candlelight as entering the darkness will quickly drain your health. Upon entering you will encounter a small poisoned pool with a pod next to it containing a few books, some gold, and possibly a spell tome. If you are low on potions or health after the long trek through the Barrow, it is wise to avoid this pod as the tentacle will inevitably strike you. It may be possible to access it without injury using the [Slow Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Slow_Time "Skyrim:Slow Time") shout.

Visibility is poor in this section of Apocrypha. Fog combined with abstruse darkness makes for a haunting environment. A hovering light which you can follow in the absence of a torch or light spell will mark the way forward. After passing under a curved lamp you will find a circular pool with an amorphous eye protruding from the depths, next to another pod. Watch for the tentacle here as well, though this one is easier to access safely than the first.

Following the hovering lamp you will make a right turn at the next curved lamp and ascend a hallway leading to an open area where you will encounter two or three seekers. The fog and absence of lighting makes it difficult to ascertain their location while they are still invisible (as normally they leave a faint, black aura where they float), so be prepared for a fight as soon as you climb the ramp. With the [Eagle Eye](/wiki/Skyrim:Eagle_Eye "Skyrim:Eagle Eye") and [Steady Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Steady_Hand "Skyrim:Steady Hand") Archery skills it is possible to snipe them through the fog through careful observation. The arena in front of you will be lit spontaneously by waves of light drifting through the black mist.

After dispatching the seekers return to the lamp that marks the entry way to this area. Turn to your left and move along the wall to encounter a pod containing some minor loot. Go back to the lamp and turn right, following the right hand wall until you find a two shelves set upon stone carved pillars. You will find there the speech skill book [2920, Second Seed, v5](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Second_Seed,_v5 "Skyrim:2920, Second Seed, v5") along with the alteration spell book [Detect Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Undead "Skyrim:Detect Undead"), among numerous ruined books. You may also find a few scrolls or a soul gem. Between the pillars sits another pod. Continue following the right hand wall until you come across a semi-spherical object with a large claw like formation extending forth from its top. Around the corner to the right you will find an altar containing the spell tome  [Conjure Seeker](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Seeker "Skyrim:Conjure Seeker") with several soul gems amid some ruined books.

Turn east and make way toward the light hovering around two curved street lamps, above which flies a green and yellow banner. There is a pod to the left of the portal containing a few books and possibly an Atronach Forge Recipe. Pass through the lamps and up a ramp until you reach a winding path with no boundaries. Be careful here as you can easily fall off either side. The pathways that connect each pillar expand and contract with the motion of the overhead lights, so be aware of their presence or you will fall to your death.

You will notice a Lurker shambling down the ramp one level higher, potentially coming your way. Casting a spell of Magelight towards any object in his vicinity will divert his attention. It is possible to cause the Lurker to fall off the platform by using Magelight repeatedly so that he follows the light up the ramp until he meets a pathway that is not lit. If you don't know Magelight then ranged attacks are your best bet here, as the pathways are narrow and you can easily be thrown off by the force of the Lurker's attacks. It may be possible to use [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") to shove the Lurker off the ramps as well.

Ascending the ramps you will encounter another altar with a spell tome and one or more soul crystals. Your final encounter may be with a Lurker Guardian, so be prepared for a fight when you reach the main platform just before ascending the stairs to the end of Apocrypha. After you have defeated it, you will find to the right of *[The Sallow Regent](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Sallow_Regent_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Sallow Regent (book)")* a scroll of Summon Storm Atronach and a [Flame Thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Thrall "Skyrim:Flame Thrall") spell tome. To the left another you will find another altar containing several soul gems. Read the book to exit Apocrypha and return to [White Ridge Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Ridge_Barrow "Skyrim:White Ridge Barrow"), thus finishing the quest.

### Rewards

Your choice of one of three abilities:

- [Seeker of Might](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker_of_Might "Skyrim:Seeker of Might") — [Combat](/wiki/Skyrim:Combat "Skyrim:Combat") skills are all 10% more effective.
- [Seeker of Sorcery](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker_of_Sorcery "Skyrim:Seeker of Sorcery") — All [spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Spells "Skyrim:Spells") cost 10% less [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka"). Enchantments are 10% more powerful.
- [Seeker of Shadows](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker_of_Shadows "Skyrim:Seeker of Shadows") — [Stealth](/wiki/Skyrim:Stealth "Skyrim:Stealth") skills are all 10% more effective.

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements#Dragonborn "Skyrim:Achievements") is related to this quest:

-  **Hidden Knowledge** (40 points/Bronze)

## Notes

- The section of Apocrypha‎ that you land in here is perhaps one of the more difficult areas. Besides the typical dangers encountered in this realm, the environment is badly lit (pitch black in areas), and the dark areas will quickly eat away at your health. Using spells such as [Candlelight](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlelight "Skyrim:Candlelight") or [Magelight](/wiki/Skyrim:Magelight "Skyrim:Magelight"), or carrying a [torch](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch") is an effective way to avoid health damage. Alternatively, you may attempt to remain in the illuminated area under the floating eye lamps, or simply sprint through the stage using potions as needed. If you enter this area already in need of healing, it would be prudent to heal yourself immediately before moving on. Damage is dealt even if you have 100% immunity to poison, 100% resistant to magic, or use the [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") shout.
- This section has a [Seeker](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker "Skyrim:Seeker"), a High Seeker, a [Lurker](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurker "Skyrim:Lurker"), and a Lurker Vindicator. Knowing the Candlelight spell and attacking from long range and/or using sneak attacks can be particularly effective.
- You can change the reward at any time by traveling to Solstheim and re-reading the book. This will transport you to Apocrypha near the reward location and you can select a different one.
- The quest rewards apply to all skills under their respective categories. Therefore Seeker of Might makes Smithing 10% more effective, and Seeker of Shadows makes created potions 10% more powerful.

## Bugs

- Upon returning to Solstheim, the sound effect of the health drain may continue to play indefinitely, or your health might continue to deplete as if you're still in the shadows of Apocrypha.
  - Exiting to the main menu might solve this issue. If not, clearing the game cache should.
  - After you exit Apocrypha, load a different save then reload the auto-save that was just made and this will stop.
  - Transforming into a werewolf or a vampire lord and back will cause the sound to stop.
  - This can be corrected by saving current progress in a new file, quitting to the Main Menu, then returning to the game without loss of progress.
  - Reading the book again and returning to Apocrypha, and then rereading it to return to Solstheim solved the problem as well.
  - Another way to fix this is leaving Apocrypha by committing suicide rather than using the books to escape as dying in Apocrypha teleports you back to Nirn.
- Upon returning to Solstheim, a second copy of The Sallow Regent may appear in your inventory and both copies become unreadable.

## Quest Stages

| Black Book: The Sallow Regent (DLC2BlackBook05Quest) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I read the Black Book called "The Sallow Regent", and found myself in Hermaeus Mora's realm of Apocrypha. I should uncover the knowledge hidden here, or read the book again to escape. *Objective 10:* Learn the Black Book's hidden knowledge |
| 20 | ☑ | I uncovered the hidden knowledge contained in the Black Book "The Sallow Regent". |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2BlackBook05Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2BlackBook05Quest`.

# Skyrim:Black Book: The Winds of Change (quest)

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Learn the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Winds_of_Change_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Winds of Change (book)")'s hidden knowledge.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | The Black Book *[The Winds of Change](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Winds_of_Change_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Winds of Change (book)")* |
| Location(s): | [Raven Rock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine"), [Apocrypha‎](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha_(The_Winds_of_Change) "Skyrim:Apocrypha (The Winds of Change)") |
| Reward: | [Companion's Insight](/wiki/Skyrim:Companion%27s_Insight "Skyrim:Companion's Insight"), [Lover's Insight](/wiki/Skyrim:Lover%27s_Insight "Skyrim:Lover's Insight"), or [Scholar's Insight](/wiki/Skyrim:Scholar%27s_Insight "Skyrim:Scholar's Insight") ability |
| ID: | DLC2BlackBook04Quest |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** Start [The Final Descent](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Final_Descent "Skyrim:The Final Descent") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | Start [The Final Descent](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Final_Descent "Skyrim:The Final Descent") | | |

The Black Book, located in the depths of Raven Rock Mine

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read the Black Book *[The Winds of Change](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Winds_of_Change_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Winds of Change (book)")* in [Raven Rock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine").
2. Make your way through [Apocrypha‎](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha_(The_Winds_of_Change) "Skyrim:Apocrypha (The Winds of Change)").
3. Learn the Black Book's hidden knowledge.
4. Choose your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

After reading the black book, you'll find yourself on a low path surrounded by water. Walk forward quickly to avoid the tentacles on either side. Up the stairs, you'll encounter a [Seeker](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker "Skyrim:Seeker"). If you take too long, or fight too far forward, you may attract the attention of another Seeker farther ahead. At the top of the stairs is a pool of poisonous water, which contains another tentacle, a Font of Stamina, and a Scrye. If your [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") skill is above 40, you will also find a spell tome for the [Conjure Seeker](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Seeker "Skyrim:Conjure Seeker") spell here.

Activating the Scrye will open a gate to your left, into a series of tunnels with fenced walls. Here there are two tables with soul gems, and a pod filled with loot. You will come to a second Scrye by one of these tables and a Font of Stamina. Activate it and a gate will open to the next chamber, which has a pool with a tentacle and another Seeker (if you did not have to fight it before). This small room contains a third Scrye, which opens up a larger room containing some green fog.

Entering the fog will cause a leveled [Lurker](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurker "Skyrim:Lurker") to emerge from a pool in the center of this room. Defeat it, then climb the ramp to find a table and two pedestals with soul gems, scrolls, and the two-handed skill book [Words and Philosophy](/wiki/Skyrim:Words_and_Philosophy "Skyrim:Words and Philosophy"), as well as the fourth Scrye. If you haven't read the skill book already, you may want to get Scholar's Insight before doing so. Activate the Scrye to open the final door, then return down the ramp and activate the final Scrye on your left, which will extend a staircase leading to the door you just opened.

Ascend the stairs to find a loot-filled vessel and the Black Book: Winds of Change. You may pick one reward, and after that, read the book again to return to Solstheim.

### Rewards

Your choice of one of three abilities:

- [Companion's Insight](/wiki/Skyrim:Companion%27s_Insight "Skyrim:Companion's Insight") — Your attacks, [shouts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"), and [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") spells do no damage to your [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") when in combat.
- [Lover's Insight](/wiki/Skyrim:Lover%27s_Insight "Skyrim:Lover's Insight") — Do 10% more damage *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* and get 10% better prices from people of the opposite sex.
- [Scholar's Insight](/wiki/Skyrim:Scholar%27s_Insight "Skyrim:Scholar's Insight") — Reading [skill books](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") gives you an extra skill point.

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements#Dragonborn "Skyrim:Achievements") is related to this quest:

-  **Hidden Knowledge** (40 points/Bronze)

## Notes

- You can change the reward at any time by traveling to Solstheim and re-reading the book. This will transport you to Apocrypha near the reward location and you can select a different one.
- Companion's Insight does not apply to your mount, summoned Atronachs, or vampire followers.
- Companion's Insight does not affect area effects like Fireball and Chain Lightning.

## Bugs

- You may be unable to go back to Solstheim using the activator at the end, instead receiving the message "You are unable to concentrate on what you're reading."
  - Step into the black water in Apocrypha. When you lose all your health in the game, you'll be transported out of the book.
  -  Use the `coc` command to another location, (e.g., `coc WindhelmDocksExterior01`).
  -  Any mods that interfere with fast travel have been known to trigger this. Disabling them may allow you to return.

| 20 | ☑ | I uncovered the hidden knowledge contained in the Black Book "The Winds of Change". |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2BlackBook04Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2BlackBook04Quest`.

# Skyrim:Black Book: Untold Legends (quest)

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by multiple users, *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [178.235.103.47](/wiki/Special:Contributions/178.235.103.47 "Special:Contributions/178.235.103.47"), *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Learn the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Untold_Legends_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Untold Legends (book)")'s hidden knowledge.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | The Black Book *[Untold Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Untold_Legends_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Untold Legends (book)")* |
| Location(s): | [Benkongerike Great Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Benkongerike_Great_Hall "Skyrim:Benkongerike Great Hall"), [Apocrypha‎](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha_(Untold_Legends) "Skyrim:Apocrypha (Untold Legends)") |
| Reward: | [Bardic Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Bardic_Knowledge "Skyrim:Bardic Knowledge"), [Black Market](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Market "Skyrim:Black Market"), or [Secret Servant](/wiki/Skyrim:Secret_Servant "Skyrim:Secret Servant") power |
| ID: | DLC2BlackBook03Quest |
| Suggested Level: | 25 |

The Black Book in Benkongerike

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read the Black Book *[Untold Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Untold_Legends_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Untold Legends (book)")* in [Benkongerike Great Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Benkongerike_Great_Hall "Skyrim:Benkongerike Great Hall").
2. Make your way through [Apocrypha‎](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha_(Untold_Legends) "Skyrim:Apocrypha (Untold Legends)").
3. Learn the Black Book's hidden knowledge.
4. Choose your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

There are five chapters: Chapter I is basically a corridor that leads to Chapter II, containing no enemies and only three [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") in the way of loot. These can be found at the very end of the chapter, at the final bend just before the book that leads to Chapter II.

Chapter II has exits to both Chapter III and Chapter IV, enabling you to bypass Chapter III if you wish. There is a leveled [lurker](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurker "Skyrim:Lurker") to battle before reaching either exit. The lurker is standing near a Font of Stamina and a Font of Magicka. There is another Font of Magicka by the exit to Chapter IV. The exit to Chapter IV can be found by taking the corridor south and then west; whereas the exit for Chapter III is taking the corridor north.

Chapter III contains a [seeker](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker "Skyrim:Seeker"), a [spell tome of Conjure Seeker](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Seeker "Skyrim:Conjure Seeker") if your Conjuration skill is at least 65, and a container of loot. These are all in the same enclosed starting area, so that the Seeker will attack you just as you enter the Chapter; the spell tome is in the beginning area as well. There is no direct path from Chapter III to Chapter IV, so you do have to return to Chapter II.

Chapter IV contains the most loot including four stealth based [skill books](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books"), two soul gems and four containers of loot as well as three seekers to battle. It starts off on an open platform with two Fonts of Stamina; walking down the corridor will take you past a well-lit Font of Magicka. You will head south into another open area; all the Seekers are here together. There are various landings here going in roughly the eight cardinal directions; the northeast one contains a locked treasure pod, a soul gem, and the four skill books. East is another locked pod and another Scrye which opens the middle. Southeast goes nowhere. South is initially unclimbable. Southwest contains another locked treasure pod. By the west gate is a Scrye which opens said gate. Inside is another Scrye which opens the east landing. There is a pod to the northwest. North returns you to the corridor to Chapter II. The middle Scrye opens out the southern stairs, allowing exit to Chapter V.

Chapter V contains a corridor that initially points towards the final reward, but may bend to the left or right whenever you move down the corridor. If it does, you'll be directed towards a room with a leveled lurker. Kill the lurker and a door will open behind it, allowing you to return to the central room. Once any side areas have been dealt with, the corridor should return to its original position, leading to the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book (book)"): *[Untold Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Untold_Legends_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Untold Legends (book)")*.

### Rewards

Your choice of one of three lesser powers:

- [Bardic Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Bardic_Knowledge "Skyrim:Bardic Knowledge") — Summons a spectral drum that plays for you, increasing [stamina regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Regenerate_Stamina "Skyrim:Regenerate Stamina") for you and nearby allies for 300 secs.
- [Black Market](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Market "Skyrim:Black Market") — Summons a [Dremora merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_Merchant "Skyrim:Dremora Merchant") to trade with you for 15 secs.
- [Secret Servant](/wiki/Skyrim:Secret_Servant "Skyrim:Secret Servant") — Summons a [Dremora butler](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_Butler "Skyrim:Dremora Butler") to carry your excess items for 15 secs. (Max carry weight 148)

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements#Dragonborn "Skyrim:Achievements") is related to this quest:

-  **Hidden Knowledge** (40 points/Bronze)

## Notes

- There is a table in Chapter IV that has the four skill books [The Gold Ribbon of Merit](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gold_Ribbon_of_Merit "Skyrim:The Gold Ribbon of Merit"), [Advances in Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Advances_in_Lockpicking "Skyrim:Advances in Lockpicking"), [Beggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Beggar_(book) "Skyrim:Beggar (book)"), and [The Rear Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rear_Guard "Skyrim:The Rear Guard"), which train archery, lockpicking, pickpocket and light armor, respectively.
- You can change the reward at any time by traveling to Solstheim and re-reading the book. This will transport you to Apocrypha near the reward location and you can select a different one.

## Bugs

- Sometimes after defeating one of the lurkers in Chapter V, the nearby door will open and then shut before you have a chance to pass through.
  -  Use the `tcl` console command to clip through the door.
- If you return to Chapter III, the hallway configuration may change, leaving any dropped items in the previous configuration permanently inaccessible. **?**
  -  Use the `tcl` console command to clip through the door(s) and regain your items.
- Although it appears that the corridor in Chapter V was always supposed to move to the left, right, or possibly each in sequence, it will often fail to do so.
- Sometimes after completing the book, you will have a false combat signature, preventing you from exiting. **?**
  - Reload the game.

- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.

# Skyrim:Black-Briar Lodge

## Overview

| # of [Stone Quarries](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") | 1 |

Black-Briar Lodge

**Black-Briar Lodge** is a large remote building east of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").

The lodge belongs to the wealthy Black-Briar family, and is inhabited by hostile [Black-Briar Mercenaries](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mercenary "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mercenary"). During the quest [Promises to Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Promises_to_Keep "Skyrim:Promises to Keep"), you will have to break into the house and steal the [identity papers](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost%27s_Identity_Papers "Skyrim:Frost's Identity Papers") for the horse [Frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost "Skyrim:Frost").

It consists of three zones. The first is *[Black-Briar Lodge](#Black-Briar_Lodge)*, which is divided into a *[ground floor](#Ground_Floor)*, a *[second floor](#Second_Floor)*, and a *[basement](#Basement)*. The other two are [exterior zones](#Exterior).

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Black-Briar Mercenaries](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mercenary "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mercenary") |

### Side Quests

- **[Promises to Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Promises_to_Keep "Skyrim:Promises to Keep")**: Help [Louis Letrush](/wiki/Skyrim:Louis_Letrush "Skyrim:Louis Letrush") get [Frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost "Skyrim:Frost") from [Sibbi Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Sibbi Black-Briar").

### Thieves Guild

- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.

### Exterior

| Plants | Animals | Other |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 [Blue Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower")  2 [Canis Root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root")  3 [Purple Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower")  2 [Red Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") | [Frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost "Skyrim:Frost") [†](#intnote_Note)  3 [Chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken") | 2 [Chickens' Nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") |

[†](#note_Note)Only appears during the quest [Promises to Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Promises_to_Keep "Skyrim:Promises to Keep")

### Black-Briar Lodge

Owned by one of the wealthiest families in Skyrim, the Black-Briar Lodge is huge and spacious, having three stories and as many entrances, all of them locked with locks of varying level. There are three hostile [Black-Briar mercenaries](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mercenary "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mercenary") guarding the exterior, and four inside the lodge. All of them carry the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Lodge_Key "Skyrim:Black-Briar Lodge Key") to the three entrances. Once the quest [Promises to Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Promises_to_Keep "Skyrim:Promises to Keep") has been initiated, [Frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost "Skyrim:Frost") the horse can be found outside the main northern entrance.

#### Ground Floor

The ground floor

Upon entering from the main entrance, a ladder to the right leads to the basement, while a table to the left holds a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). Across the hallway is an end table with clutter, with a sample of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") and a bottle of [Black-Briar Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead") on top. To the right of this table stands a wardrobe with clutter and upper-class clothes and an alcove with a food barrel. To the left is a hallway leading further into the house, past yet another wardrobe with clothes. Around the corner is a huge dining area with a doorway to the north leading further into the house and two ladders leading upstairs to the second floor. On a small table along the western wall are two bottles of wine and one of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). Underneath the two ladders is a total of four food sacks. The dining table seats six and is dressed with a huge variety of food on display, including four loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), three [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), three cloves of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), two [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), two slices of [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), two [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), two wedges of [eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), one [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"), one [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), one head of [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), one [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), one [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), one [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), and a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"). Additionally, the table holds beverages, including one bottle of alto wine, one of Black-Briar Mead, and one of [Black-Briar Reserve](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Reserve "Skyrim:Black-Briar Reserve"). Surrounding the dinner table are several shelves with valuable utensils and more drinks, five bottles of Black-Briar mead, two bottles of wine, and one bottle of alto wine.

Continuing past the dining area through the entrance to the north will place you in a small storage area, where another ladder leads downstairs, and two sacks and a barrel all hold food. A door to the east leads to a bedroom with a double bed and even more valuables. In the eastern corner is a dresser with a novice-locked chest containing random items on top. At the foot of the bed is an unlocked chest with random items, while the end table next to the bedhead contains only clutter. The wardrobe contains upper-class clothes, and a set of shelves holds two loaves of bread, an eidar cheese wheel, and a bottle of wine.

#### Second Floor

The second floor

On the second floor, you can choose between doors to the north and south. The southern door leads to a food barrel and, behind the corner, a huge bedroom. Along the northern wall is an end table with clutter, with the [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") skill book *[Legend of Krately House](/wiki/Skyrim:Legend_of_Krately_House "Skyrim:Legend of Krately House")* on top. Following the wall to the right, next to a small storage alcove, a chest holds some random items, while the wardrobe has some upper-class clothes and the chance of a book and some gold. Next to the bed, on an end table with clutter, is a [Stone of Barenziah](/wiki/Skyrim:Stone_of_Barenziah "Skyrim:Stone of Barenziah"). The end table at the foot of the bed has a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") on top. Lastly, the southwestern corner has an end table with more clutter, a wardrobe with clothes, and some shelves with two [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"). The northern door leads to another dining room, obviously rarely used, with an exit to Skyrim along the northern wall. A small table holds a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and at the other end of the room, a set of shelves holds two bottles of wine and two of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). A novice-locked chest on the shelves contains random items, while the nearby end table contains clutter. A door leads to a storage room with two food barrels, three food sacks, two wheels of [goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), and a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread").

#### Basement

The basement

When entering the basement from the main entrance on the ground floor, check behind the ladder for a locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") with a solid amount of gold. A set of shelves holds six gold coins, a bottle of alto wine, an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), and a [mammoth tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Tusk "Skyrim:Mammoth Tusk"). The next room has an apprentice-locked chest with random items, and if you have started the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Promises_to_Keep "Skyrim:Promises to Keep"), *[Frost's Identity Papers](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost%27s_Identity_Papers "Skyrim:Frost's Identity Papers")* on an end table. The door to the north leads to a huge room with an exit to Skyrim and a total of six food sacks scattered around. A [Black-Briar mead barrel](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Black-Briar_Mead_Barrel "Skyrim:Containers") with up to ten bottles of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead") stands against the northern wall, opposite a small table with a bottle of wine, a slice of [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), a loaf of bread, an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), an [cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), and some [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"). A wardrobe holds some common clothes, and two doors lead to two bedrooms with unowned beds. The bedroom on the right contains a medium coin purse, while the one on the left contains an end table containing some gold.

The last room features a set of stairs leading to the ground floor and a food barrel behind the door. The western part of the room contains a huge counter with a [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), some [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), and two bottles of Black-Briar mead. The northeastern corner holds a set of shelves with a huge amount of food crammed together, including eight [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), three [gourds](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), three loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), two [boiled creme treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"), two wedges of [goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), two wheels of [goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), two [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), two [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), an [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), and a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"). Behind all the food sits a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") and a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina").

## Notes

- This house has many [safe containers](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Safe_Containers "Skyrim:Containers"). Most, however, are owned, and thus will mark your items as stolen if you place them inside then remove them.
- The three door locks are leveled differently. The top floor is the easiest, and the bottom floor is the hardest.
- Black-Briar Lodge also [appears](/wiki/Online:Black-Briar_Lodge "Online:Black-Briar Lodge") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- The Black-Briar mercenaries may attack the chickens outside the building.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.
- The basement door is missing its key setting.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.8, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Black-Briar Manor

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Black-Briar Manor ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Black-Briar+Manor)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| RiftenBlackBriarManor | |
| Region | |
| [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | |
| Location | |
| [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Alchemy Labs](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") | 1 |
| [Shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") | [Protected](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Protected") Protected |

Black-Briar Manor

**Black-Briar Manor** is the Black-Briars' residence in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").

It is the home of [Maven Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar"), her son [Hemming Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hemming_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Hemming Black-Briar"), and her daughter [Ingun Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingun_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Ingun Black-Briar"). Maven's [housecarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl"), [Maul](/wiki/Skyrim:Maul "Skyrim:Maul"), resides here as well. Ingun spends most of her day in [Elgrim's Elixirs](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim%27s_Elixirs "Skyrim:Elgrim's Elixirs"), and returns at night to sleep. This is an easy target for thieves as it is likely to be unoccupied most of the day. It contains only one zone, the [interior](#Black-Briar_Manor).

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Hemming Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hemming_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Hemming Black-Briar") \*  [Ingun Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingun_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Ingun Black-Briar")  [Maul](/wiki/Skyrim:Maul "Skyrim:Maul") \*  [Maven Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar") \* |

\* These NPCs relocate to [Mistveil Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistveil_Keep "Skyrim:Mistveil Keep") if the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") takes over [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift").

## Related Quests

- **[Few and Far Between](/wiki/Skyrim:Few_and_Far_Between "Skyrim:Few and Far Between")**: Help [Ingun](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingun_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Ingun Black-Briar") restock [Elgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim "Skyrim:Elgrim")'s rare ingredients.

## Black-Briar Manor

Entering the manor brings you into an oddly shaped reception room with a chair to your left, a long end table against the northeast wall, with a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Regarding_Your_Loss "Skyrim:Regarding Your Loss") regarding the loss of a shipment of [Black-Briar Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead") to [Cyrodiil](/wiki/Lore:Cyrodiil "Lore:Cyrodiil") on top and a doorway to the right of it. Against the southeast wall is a tall wardrobe and another long end table that holds an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), with a doorway to the right of it. In the western corner is a small sitting area with two chairs and a low table between them. On the table is a bottle of Black-Briar Mead. To the southwest of the doorway is a cupboard against the southwest wall holding [plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate") and a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl"). There is a alcove containing several crates, sacks and a couple of [Black-Briar Mead barrels](/wiki/Skyrim:Barrel "Skyrim:Barrel").

To the northeast is another oddly shaped room with a cupboard holding two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and several [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"). Further around against a wall to the north is a set of shelves holding three bottles of Black-Briar Mead, a bowl and copies of *[Gods and Worship](/wiki/Skyrim:Gods_and_Worship "Skyrim:Gods and Worship")* and *[The Hope of the Redoran](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Hope_of_the_Redoran "Skyrim:The Hope of the Redoran")*, again further to the right is a set of shelves against the northeast wall with a [jug](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug "Skyrim:Jug") and a copy of *[The Amulet of Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Amulet_of_Kings "Skyrim:The Amulet of Kings")* with chairs on either side. Another set of shelves against the east wall holds a bunch of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"), a bowl, a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") and a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"). To the right of this is a flight of stairs down to the cellar, with a flight up to the second story behind it and a doorway to the right that enters a corridor that has a second entrance to the Manor and the stairs leading upstairs, to the left and another doorway ahead that enters a dining room, there are several sacks on a crate and a couple of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels in this corridor. The second entrance is from the rear garden of the manor which has a gate at the end, a couple of trees, a wooden bench, a lavender bush and three food barrels.

The dining room has a long wooden table down the middle and chairs on either side. On the table which is set for five with plates and goblets, are two [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), two [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), two portions of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), some [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), several pieces of cheese, an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"), a bottle of wine and two bottles of Black-Briar Mead. Against the northeast wall is a set of shelves holding several goblets, three bottles of Black-Briar Mead, a bottle of alto wine and a bottle of wine. Against the northeast wall is a long end table with a bunch of tundra cotton on top and to the southeast is a cupboard holding various bowls, jugs, goblets and plates, finally in the western corner is a chair between two small tables that hold a copy of *[Thief of Virtue](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_of_Virtue "Skyrim:Thief of Virtue")* and a bottle of wine and a goblet.

Climbing the stairs to the second floor leads to a large landing, again oddly shaped. In the northeastern corner is a set of shelves holding a bunch of tundra cotton and copies of *[Lost Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends")* and *[Ruins of Kemel-Ze](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Kemel-Ze "Skyrim:Ruins of Kemel-Ze")*, with wooden benches to the left and right, against the walls. To the south is another storage area with crates, sacks and a Black-Briar Mead barrel. To the west is a door that opens into Maven's large bedroom with a king-sized bed coming out from the southeast wall, with a long unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing random items at the foot of the bed, an end table with a goblet and bottle of alto wine on top and wardrobe containing [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") to the left and a long end table holding a [letter from Christophe](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Christophe "Skyrim:Letter from Christophe") and a [letter from Sabjorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Sabjorn "Skyrim:Letter from Sabjorn") and a couple of chairs to the right, with a small table holding a bottle of wine between them. Opposite the chairs is a fireplace with a piece of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") to the left. Against the northwest wall is a wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") with a door out onto a small balcony that looks out over the canal and marketplace to the right. Another wardrobe stands in a corner to the north. Opposite the internal door is a set of shelves holding a [statue of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Statue_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Statue of Dibella"), a [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"), a bunch of tundra cotton and copies of *[Alduin is Real](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin_is_Real "Skyrim:Alduin is Real")* and *[The Arcturian Heresy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcturian_Heresy "Skyrim:The Arcturian Heresy")* and a final wardrobe is to the right of these.

A corridor leads between this bedroom and the storage area to the southwest with two doors on the left and more storage at the end. The first door on the left consists of a single owned bed in the southern corner, with an end table beside it holding a goblet and bottle of alto wine. In the western corner is a wardrobe of fine clothes. Against the southeast wall is a long end table and against the northeast wall is a set of shelves holding a bunch of tundra cotton, an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), an [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield") and copies of *[Darkest Darkness](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkest_Darkness "Skyrim:Darkest Darkness")*, *[Biography of Barenziah, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:Biography_of_Barenziah,_v1 "Skyrim:Biography of Barenziah, v1")* and *[v2](/wiki/Skyrim:Biography_of_Barenziah,_v2 "Skyrim:Biography of Barenziah, v2")*. The second door enters another bedroom with a single owned bed coming out from the southwest wall, with an end table holding a bottle of alto wine and a goblet to the left and a set of shelves holding a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and three bottles of [Black-Briar Reserve](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Reserve "Skyrim:Black-Briar Reserve").

At the bottom of the stairs down to the cellar there is a room on the right containing several bales of straw and a couple of piles of wood, with three doors, one to the northeast and two to the northwest. The door to the northeast is [Ingun Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingun_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Ingun Black-Briar")'s bedroom and contains a wardrobe against the southwest wall, a single unowned bed in an alcove to the northwest (see [notes](#Notes)), an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") in the northern corner, a set of shelves against the northeast wall holding a [chicken's egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), a [pine thrush egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"), two [rock warbler eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"), a bowl of [ectoplasm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ectoplasm "Skyrim:Ectoplasm"), two [Falmer ears](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Ear "Skyrim:Falmer Ear"), three bowls of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), a sample of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), a sample of [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"), a [blue butterfly wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Butterfly_Wing "Skyrim:Blue Butterfly Wing"), a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), six [slaughterfish eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg"), a [skeever tail](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever_Tail "Skyrim:Skeever Tail"), a sample of [scaly pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota"), two [Nordic barnacles](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle"), a bunch of [jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes") and a bunch of [juniper berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries"). In an alcove to the southeast are a couple of Black-Briar Mead barrels, sacks and crates.

The first door to the northwest is master-locked and contains more Black-Briar Mead barrels, a crate, a sack and the remains of a [Black Sacrament](/wiki/Lore:Black_Sacrament "Lore:Black Sacrament") performed using a skeleton, a [human heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Human_Heart "Skyrim:Human Heart"), [human flesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Human_Flesh "Skyrim:Human Flesh"), a [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") flower and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") as explained in the book *[A Kiss, Sweet Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Kiss,_Sweet_Mother "Skyrim:A Kiss, Sweet Mother")*, a copy of which is present along with a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:To_the_Brotherhood "Skyrim:To the Brotherhood") to [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid") from Maven Black-Briar, complaining at the lack of action (see [notes](#Notes)). The second door to the northwest opens into another bedroom with a single owned bed against the southwest wall, an end table holding a bottle of wine beside it and a wardrobe further to the right of the northwest wall.

## Notes

- Ingun's bed in the cellar becomes available to use once you have completed her [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Few_and_Far_Between "Skyrim:Few and Far Between").
- The human flesh and human heart respawn.
- There are two  "Protected") Protected [shadowmarks](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") around the manor, one by the front entrance and one by a gate at the rear of the property. Maven Black-Briar has strong ties with the Thieves Guild.
- The letter to Astrid doesn't seem to get sent, as no action is taken, and no quest that is clearly for Maven is given to you to carry out.
- Aside from most barrels and sacks, all containers in the house are [non-respawning](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") and safe to store items in.
- During the quest [Dampened Spirits](/wiki/Skyrim:Dampened_Spirits "Skyrim:Dampened Spirits"), the door to Black-Briar Manor will lock if night falls while inside it. Unlocking the door will be considered a crime. Just wait until morning for the door to unlock itself.

# Skyrim:Black-Briar Meadery

## Overview
