| Special Features | |
| [Shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") | [Protected](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Protected") Protected |

The Black-Briar Meadery

**Black-Briar Meadery** is a bar and brewery in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). The meadery is owned by [Maven Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar"), who employs several people who actually run the business. There is only one zone, which is the [interior](#Black-Briar_Meadery).

## Related Quests

- **[The Lover's Requital](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lover%27s_Requital "Skyrim:The Lover's Requital")**: Help [Sibbi Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Sibbi Black-Briar") locate his former [fiancée](/wiki/Skyrim:Svidi "Skyrim:Svidi"), so he can kill her.
- **[Under the Table](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_the_Table "Skyrim:Under the Table")**: Deliver a smuggled Black-Briar Mead keg to the inn at [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead").

### Black-Briar Meadery

[Ungrien](/wiki/Skyrim:Ungrien "Skyrim:Ungrien") is the barkeeper, and therefore welcomes most visitors to the meadery. However, [Indaryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Indaryn "Skyrim:Indaryn") is the brew master, in charge of brewing the mead. [Romlyn Dreth](/wiki/Skyrim:Romlyn_Dreth "Skyrim:Romlyn Dreth"), [Niluva Hlaalu](/wiki/Skyrim:Niluva_Hlaalu "Skyrim:Niluva Hlaalu"), and [Asgeir Snow-Shod](/wiki/Skyrim:Asgeir_Snow-Shod "Skyrim:Asgeir Snow-Shod") are the remaining employees, and can be found doing various nondescript jobs around the meadery.

Entering leads directly into the shop/bar area, with the counter in the southwestern corner. On the counter is a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Attention_Employees! "Skyrim:Attention Employees!") from Indaryn regarding thefts from the meadery. There are three stools in front of the counter, and a couple [Black-Briar mead barrels](/wiki/Skyrim:Barrel "Skyrim:Barrel") in the southeastern corner. There are two small square wooden tables, one to the north and the other in the northwestern corner. These have three bottles of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), two [salt piles](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), and two notes, the first titled [All Employees Must Read Immedately!](/wiki/Skyrim:All_Employees_Must_Read! "Skyrim:All Employees Must Read!"), and the second titled [To Be Read Immedately!](/wiki/Skyrim:To_Be_Read_Immedately! "Skyrim:To Be Read Immedately!"). Both notes indicate that working conditions are terrible for the employees, and that Indaryn is a tyrant. Hanging above the counter is a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, two bunches of [Elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), and two bunches of [Frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). Under the counter is a leveled [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword") and three bottles of Black-Briar mead. On the south wall is a wall shelf holding all of the [displayed merchandise](#Displayed_Merchandise) (see [notes](#Notes)). There is a door behind the counter to the west.

Through the door is a corridor heading north to a T-junction, with a set of shelves in front, against the north wall, that holds three [boiled creme treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"), a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), a couple loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), several [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), and several pieces of cheese. There is a crate, a sack, a couple [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels, and a Black-Briar mead barrel in the corridor, with a second to the east of the junction over a flight of stairs leading down to the cellar. Heading west along a walkway with the lower lever visible below, there is a railing on your left side, with a wooden bench and a dresser against the east wall. At the end of the walkway is a storage area with several crates, sacks, and more Black-Briar mead barrels, with the door to Indaryn's bedroom to the left. Seen over the railing on a ledge in the southeast corner is a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"); to reach it, you must jump over the railing and land on the ledge before inching across and then dropping down to the floor below.

Indaryn's bedroom contains his owned double bed, a medium coin purse and two loose gold coins under the bed, a cupboard to the left holding four potions and a mammoth tusk, a dresser at the foot of the bed with a [note from Maven](/wiki/Skyrim:Note_From_Maven "Skyrim:Note From Maven") on top, an end table, and a wardrobe. Clutter, food, and alcohol are also found scattered about the furniture and on a wall shelf.

At the bottom of the stairs are more barrels containing Black-Briar mead, with a small chance of finding a bottle of [Black-Briar Reserve](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Reserve "Skyrim:Black-Briar Reserve"). Against the east wall is an unlocked chest containing nothing, with a set of shelves beside it. These hold a bottle of wine, an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), and copies of *[The City of Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_City_of_Stone "Skyrim:The City of Stone")*, *[Songs of the Return, Vol 19](/wiki/Skyrim:Songs_of_the_Return,_Vol_19 "Skyrim:Songs of the Return, Vol 19")*, *[The Code of Malacath](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Code_of_Malacath "Skyrim:The Code of Malacath")*, and *[Song of the Askelde Men](/wiki/Skyrim:Song_of_the_Askelde_Men "Skyrim:Song of the Askelde Men")*. In the southeast corner is a small round wooden table and two chairs. Against the north wall is a long wooden table holding a medium coin purse, three loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), a bottle of Black-Briar mead, a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a loaf of bread, and a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"). There is a doorway to the west that leads onto another walkway with a railing around the middle and a view down to the bottom level, where the storage and boiling vats are. The walkway heads both west and north. Following it north passes a couple wall shelves on the east wall holding three bottles of Black-Briar mead, a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and plenty of clutter, with a garlic braid, a bunch of elves ear, and two bunches of frost mirriam hanging above. At the end of the walkway is a small square wooden table set for three, with two [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), three portions of grilled leeks, and a bottle of Black-Briar mead. Heading west passes several more Black-Briar mead barrels, before turning to the north and passing a second exit leading out onto the docks. At the end is a flight of stairs down to the east leading to the lowest level.

At the bottom, in front of you is a chest that requires a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi%27s_Chest_Key "Skyrim:Sibbi's Chest Key") to open. The only way to get this key is by completing the relevant [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lover%27s_Requital "Skyrim:The Lover's Requital") for [Sibbi Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Sibbi Black-Briar"). There are two large boiling vats against the north wall, three large storage vats opposite against the south wall, and several piles of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") on the floor and under the stairs, where you can find two loose pieces. There are also a large number of Black-Briar mead barrels stacked in piles around the room, and a wall shelf in the middle of the east wall holding several food sacks.

## Displayed Merchandise

The following items are sitting out in the store, for example, on the store counters. They can be purchased from the merchant, or can be stolen. Other items may also be present in the store, but those other items are not available for purchase. These items [respawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Respawning "Skyrim:Dungeons") after ten days.

|  |
| --- |
| - **[Potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions")**: 1 [Philter of Pickpocketing](/wiki/Skyrim:Philter_of_Pickpocketing "Skyrim:Philter of Pickpocketing"), 1 [Potion of the Healer](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_the_Healer "Skyrim:Potion of the Healer") - **Food**: 3 Black-Briar Mead, 1 Black-Briar Reserve |

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in the meadery's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") or stolen. These items are restocked every two days.

| Count | Item |
| --- | --- |
| 12 | bottles of Black-Briar Mead |
| 3 | bottles of Black-Briar Reserve |

## Notes

- There is a  "Protected") Protected [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") by the entrance, due to Maven Black-Briar's strong ties with the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").
- The music that plays inside the shop is environmental music, rather than city music.
- Completing [Under the Table](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_the_Table "Skyrim:Under the Table") for [Wilhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Wilhelm "Skyrim:Wilhelm") or turning [Valindor](/wiki/Skyrim:Valindor "Skyrim:Valindor") into vampire during quest [New Allegiances](/wiki/Skyrim:New_Allegiances "Skyrim:New Allegiances") for Volkihar Clan, will makes low-level items in the meadery freely available, including the bottles of Black-Briar mead found in barrels, but not the bottles of Black-Briar reserve, nor the items on the shelf behind the counter, which are always tagged as owned.
- Aside from most barrels and sacks, all containers in the area are [non-respawning](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning"), and are safe to store items in.
- If you don't want to go through the main gate of Riften (and thus meet Maul on the other side, who will start the misc. quest to talk to Brynjolf about joining the Thieves Guild), you can go through the meadery's doors on the docks outside the city during the day and enter Riften this way, bypassing Maul. Brynjolf will seek you out as soon as you enter the market, but you can use the forge at the Scorched Hammer to avoid the misc. quest he gives to join the Guild.

A Black-Briar Mercenary inside the lodge

Four **Black-Briar Mercenaries** are present inside the [Black-Briar Lodge](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Lodge "Skyrim:Black-Briar Lodge"). They wear [steel plate armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate_Armor "Skyrim:Steel Plate Armor"), leveled [light boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor"), and have a 50% chance of wearing leveled [light bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Gauntlets "Skyrim:Armor"). These four carry 25-125 gold, a [torch](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch"), a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Lodge_Key "Skyrim:Black-Briar Lodge Key") to the lodge, and a leveled [weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons").

## Bugs

- The Black-Briar mercenaries may attack the chickens outside the building.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Blackblood Marauder

## Overview

The **Blackblood Marauders** are a group of bandits living in [Broken Oar Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Oar_Grotto "Skyrim:Broken Oar Grotto") who also appear at [the Wreck of the Icerunner](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_the_Icerunner "Skyrim:Wreck of the Icerunner") during [Lights Out!](/wiki/Skyrim:Lights_Out! "Skyrim:Lights Out!"). They are led by [Jaree-Ra](/wiki/Skyrim:Jaree-Ra "Skyrim:Jaree-Ra"), his sister [Deeja](/wiki/Skyrim:Deeja "Skyrim:Deeja"), and [Captain Hargar](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Hargar "Skyrim:Captain Hargar"). During the related quest, their leader, Jaree-Ra, arranged for the light in the [Solitude Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Solitude Lighthouse") to be extinguished by you, causing The Icerunner to run aground near the west shore. They then boarded the ship under command by Deeja, massacred the crew, and stole all the cargo, which they shipped to their base of operations at Broken Oar Grotto to keep the loot safe. They can be easily recognized by their signature black tattoos, mimicking the blood vessels, on the sides of their necks and faces.

Blackblood Marauder (Bandit Wizard)

These two Marauders are both [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [bandit wizards](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Wizard "Skyrim:Bandit Wizard"), differing only in their appearance. They wear a leveled set of [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes"), which will be enchanted to either fortify [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Alteration "Skyrim:Fortify Alteration"), [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Destruction "Skyrim:Fortify Destruction"), or  [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Restoration "Skyrim:Fortify Restoration") or to [regenerate magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Regenerate_Magicka "Skyrim:Regenerate Magicka"). They are armed with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and may also carry a small amount of gold. Each can cast a leveled set of spells from the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration"), [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction"), and [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") schools, including one [armor spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor_(spells) "Skyrim:Armor (spells)"), one [ward spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Ward "Skyrim:Ward"), one [healing spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Restore_Health "Skyrim:Restore Health") and one elemental damage spell.

Blackblood Marauder (Bandit)

This Marauder is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)"). He wears [leather armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Armor "Skyrim:Leather Armor") with matching [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") and defends himself with a random leveled [two-handed weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-Handed_Weapons "Skyrim:Two-Handed Weapons"), up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") in quality. He also may carry a small amount of gold.

Blackblood Marauder (Bandit)

This Marauder is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)"). He wears [leather armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Armor "Skyrim:Leather Armor") with matching [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") and [bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Bracers "Skyrim:Leather Bracers"). He defends himself with a leveled [one-handed weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:One-Handed_Weapons "Skyrim:One-Handed Weapons"), which can be up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") in quality; and a leveled [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"), which can be up to [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel "Skyrim:Steel") in quality. He also may carry a few [lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") or a small amount of gold.

Blackblood Marauder (Bandit Archer)

This Marauder is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [bandit archer](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Archer "Skyrim:Bandit Archer"). He wears [leather armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Armor "Skyrim:Leather Armor") with matching [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") and defends himself with a leveled [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") with twenty leveled [arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows"), both of which may be up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") in quality. The bow is also supplemented by a leveled [one-handed weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:One-Handed_Weapons "Skyrim:One-Handed Weapons"), which also may be up to elven in quality. Additionally, he may carry a few [lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") or a small amount of gold.

## Related Quests

- **[Lights Out!](/wiki/Skyrim:Lights_Out! "Skyrim:Lights Out!")**: Help run a [cargo ship](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Icerunner "Skyrim:The Icerunner") aground.
- **[Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader")**: Do a favor by slaying a bandit leader. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Notes

- The archer does not have a unique facial model, he instead uses the default male Nord face, albeit with a shaved head and the identifying face tattoo. He shares this quirk with numerous other NPCs, including [Erikur](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur "Skyrim:Erikur"), [Briehl](/wiki/Skyrim:Briehl "Skyrim:Briehl"), [Lynoit](/wiki/Skyrim:Lynoit "Skyrim:Lynoit"), [Barknar](/wiki/Skyrim:Barknar_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Barknar (Dawnguard)"), and many other generic NPCs.

# Skyrim:Blackbone Isle Grotto

## Overview

The entrance to Blackbone Isle Grotto

**Blackbone Isle Grotto** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") connected to the sea, situated on [Blackbone Isle](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackbone_Isle "Skyrim:Blackbone Isle"). The cave is initially filled with [undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Undead "Skyrim:Undead"). It houses a haunted ship named *[Dead Man's Dread](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread_(place) "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread (place)")*, which can be repurposed as a player home after completing the related quest.

## Related Quests

- **[The Restless](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Restless "Skyrim:The Restless")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread"): Search for an ancient pirate ship.

### Exterior

The entrance to this cave can be found directly next to the boat connecting Blackbone Isle to [Orphan's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Orphan's Tear"). For more information, see the [Blackbone Isle article](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackbone_Isle "Skyrim:Blackbone Isle").

### Blackbone Isle Grotto

Blackbone Isle Grotto

The skull

Blackbone Isle Grotto is a flooded cavern containing *Dead Man's Dread*, a famed ship which became trapped underground roughly six hundred years ago. Two undead enemies block your path when you first approach the ship, although they do not respawn. A giant skull has been hewn into the stone wall of the cavern. In the mouth of giant skull, behind and to the right of the fire is a treasure chest. To reach it you can use [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") from the ship's bowsprit and aim for the mouth.

*This [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim")-related article is a [stub](/wiki/UESPWiki:Stub "UESPWiki:Stub"). You can help by [expanding it](https://en.uesp.net/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Blackbone_Isle_Grotto&action=edit).*

# Skyrim:Blackbone Isle

## Overview

Blackbone Isle

**Blackbone Isle** is a haunted island in the [Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sea_of_Ghosts "Skyrim:Sea of Ghosts"). It can only be reached via the boat at [Orphan's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Orphan's Tear").

The island consists of a small strip of coastline as well as the entrance to a cave known as [Blackbone Isle Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackbone_Isle_Grotto "Skyrim:Blackbone Isle Grotto"). The Grotto houses a ship named *[Dead Man's Dread](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread_(place) "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread (place)")*, which can be repurposed as a [player house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") after completion of the related quest.

## Related Quests

- **[The Restless](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Restless "Skyrim:The Restless")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread"): Search for an ancient pirate ship.

## Blackbone Isle

You will arrive on Blackbone Isle just at the entrance to the Grotto, where you may immediately be attacked by an undead enemy (see below). You will need to enter the Grotto as part of the related quest, but a quick detour down the coast can offer additional loot. The island cannot actually be circumnavigated due to invisible barriers, and tall mountains block any progress into the interior. Your only option is therefore to head south, towards a shipwreck visible from the entrance.

The remainder of the coast is crawling with undead if you have either the [Bone Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Wolf "Skyrim:Bone Wolf") and [Plague of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Plague_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Plague of the Dead") [Creations](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed. There are a total of six undead enemy spawn points along the shore where you may encounter some of these new enemy types, including the one at the entrance. If you have neither Creation installed, the island will instead be inhabited by six harmless [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit "Skyrim:Rabbit"). Several chests can be found by exploring the island, as well as two [moonstone veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone "Skyrim:Moonstone"). There is also an [amethyst geode](/wiki/Skyrim:Amethyst_Geode "Skyrim:Amethyst Geode") due north of the boat you arrive in, hidden between two sets of rocks jutting out from the shore. There are three [pearl oysters](/wiki/Skyrim:Pearl_Oyster "Skyrim:Pearl Oyster") hidden just south of the same boat, which can be found by standing beneath the first tree along the shore heading south, while looking out west at the larger rock formation and then looking left and slightly down.

## Notes

- Blackbone Isle has a map marker and it can be fast traveled to from the mainland. However, although you can display the world map while you are on the island, there are no displayed place names and you are therefore compelled to return to the mainland using the boat on the beach outside the grotto entrance, as fast travel is impossible in the reverse direction. It is worth bearing in mind that you will probably be immediately attacked when you land at Orphan's Tear unless you have dealt with the three respawning resident bandits before you left for the island.

## Maps

Inside Blackreach

**Blackreach** is an immense, naturally lit [cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") inhabited by hordes of [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and containing the ruins of a [Dwemer](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer") [city](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins"). The cavern itself is reached by traversing any of three Dwemer ruins: [Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand "Skyrim:Alftand") (southwest of Winterhold), [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft") (southwest of Dawnstar), or [Raldbthar](/wiki/Skyrim:Raldbthar "Skyrim:Raldbthar") (west-southwest of Windhelm). In order to access the entrances to Blackreach from these ruins, the [Attunement Sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Attunement_Sphere "Skyrim:Attunement Sphere") is needed to reveal the stairs leading to each entrance. The Dwemer theme of the ruins continues within the cavern proper, featuring what appears to be a small city, which has long since been claimed by Falmer. The northernmost point of the cavern features a Dwemer observatory and a lift to the surface for easy access.

.jpg)

Geode Vein

The Silent City

Blackreach is the only place where [crimson nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Crimson_Nirnroot "Skyrim:Crimson Nirnroot") can be found, which was of great interest to the renowned botanical [alchemist](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy"), [Sinderion](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinderion "Skyrim:Sinderion"). The cavern also houses many geode veins, some of which can be [mined](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") for [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") using a pickaxe, as well as an assortment of other ore veins scattered around. There are 36 geode veins scattered throughout Blackreach in total: 34 in the cavern itself, and 2 in [Silent City Catacombs](/wiki/Skyrim:Silent_City_Catacombs "Skyrim:Silent City Catacombs"). 23 of these geode veins can be [mined](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") to yield level-dependent empty soul gems (grand soul gems and black soul gems start to appear at level 16 with a very low probability, which increases until level 30 (grand)/31 (black)). However, the other 13 geode veins are no different from standard corundum ore veins; these veins will always yield three [corundum ores](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore"), with a chance of also yielding one or more regular [gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems").

- With version 1.2.4 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), this is changed so that Geode Veins always yield soul gems. (It is unclear whether this has been achieved by making the 13 anomalous Geode Veins drop soul gems instead of corundum, or by converting them to standard Corundum Veins, or a mix of the two.)

## Zones

Blackreach is a huge cavern that can be difficult to navigate, especially since your in-game map will only ever allow you to see part of the cavern.

Most players will first enter Blackreach in the northeast corner, through the door leading to [Alftand Cathedral](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand#Alftand_Cathedral "Skyrim:Alftand"). The [Great Lift at Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Great_Lift_at_Alftand "Skyrim:Great Lift at Alftand") is found a short distance to the south-southeast; it is one of three [lifts](#Exit_Locations) that provide direct access to the surface. Directly across from the Alftand Cathedral entrance is the first of many buildings scattered throughout the cavern:

- **[Sinderion's Field Laboratory](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinderion%27s_Field_Laboratory "Skyrim:Sinderion's Field Laboratory")** — A small [Dwarven building](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") in Blackreach serving as [Sinderion's](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinderion "Skyrim:Sinderion") alchemical foothold in the cavern. This is the only building in Blackreach that contains an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs"), an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters"), a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot"), and a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench").

One distinctive section of the cavern is the ruined Dwemer city, found in the western part of the cavern. It contains several buildings:

- **[Debate Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Debate_Hall "Skyrim:Debate Hall")** — A small [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") in Blackreach occupied by [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and [their servants](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Servant "Skyrim:Falmer Servant").
- **[Hall of Rumination](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Rumination "Skyrim:Hall of Rumination")** — A small [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") in Blackreach occupied by [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and [their servants](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Servant "Skyrim:Falmer Servant").
- **[Pumping Station](/wiki/Skyrim:Pumping_Station "Skyrim:Pumping Station")** — A small [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") in Blackreach occupied by [Falmer servants](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Servant "Skyrim:Falmer Servant").
- **[Silent City Catacombs](/wiki/Skyrim:Silent_City_Catacombs "Skyrim:Silent City Catacombs")** — A small [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") in Blackreach occupied by [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer").

The entrances related to Mzinchaleft are north of the city, namely the door to [Mzinchaleft Gatehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft#Mzinchaleft_Gatehouse "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft") (in the northwestern corner of the cavern) and the [Great Lift at Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Great_Lift_at_Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Great Lift at Mzinchaleft"). Two other buildings are also found along the northern wall of the cavern:

- **[Reeking Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Reeking_Tower "Skyrim:Reeking Tower")** — A small [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") in Blackreach occupied by [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider").
- **[Silent Ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Silent_Ruin "Skyrim:Silent Ruin")** — A small [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") in Blackreach.

Entrance to Raldbthar Deep Market

The southern part of Blackreach is dominated by waterfalls plunging into a lake far below the rest of Blackreach. The entrances related to Raldbthar are to the southeast, namely the door to [Raldbthar Deep Market](/wiki/Skyrim:Raldbthar#Raldbthar_Deep_Market "Skyrim:Raldbthar") and the [Great Lift at Raldbthar](/wiki/Skyrim:Great_Lift_at_Raldbthar "Skyrim:Great Lift at Raldbthar"). The [Tower of Mzark](/wiki/Skyrim:Tower_of_Mzark "Skyrim:Tower of Mzark") is on a spire to the southwest. Three other buildings are scattered around the edges of the lake:

- **[Derelict Pumphouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Derelict_Pumphouse "Skyrim:Derelict Pumphouse")** — A small [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") in Blackreach occupied by a [Dwarven spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider").
- **[Farm Overseer's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Farm_Overseer%27s_House "Skyrim:Farm Overseer's House")** — A small [Dwarven building](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") in Blackreach.
- **[War Quarters](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Quarters "Skyrim:War Quarters")** — A small [Dwarven building](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") in Blackreach.

## Exit Locations

Overlooking the Silent City

Once you enter Blackreach, there are several different exits from Blackreach to Skyrim. The quickest way to the surface is by using any of the three "Great Lifts", elevator shafts leading to gatehouses on the surface. These lifts can only be accessed from Blackreach; however, once you open the gate at the top of the lift, it becomes a new access point for Blackreach, with a fast-travel marker on your map. One other exit, the [Tower of Mzark](/wiki/Skyrim:Tower_of_Mzark "Skyrim:Tower of Mzark"), must also be initially accessed from Blackreach.

Lift locations:

-  **[Great Lift at Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Great_Lift_at_Alftand "Skyrim:Great Lift at Alftand")** — A Dwarven lift to Blackreach located northeast of [Nightgate Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn") and southeast of [Wayward Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Wayward_Pass "Skyrim:Wayward Pass"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Great+Lift+at+Alftand)
-  **[Great Lift at Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Great_Lift_at_Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Great Lift at Mzinchaleft")** — A Dwarven lift to Blackreach located south of [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Great+Lift+at+Mzinchaleft)
-  **[Great Lift at Raldbthar](/wiki/Skyrim:Great_Lift_at_Raldbthar "Skyrim:Great Lift at Raldbthar")** — A Dwarven lift to Blackreach located west-southwest of [Anga's Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Anga%27s_Mill "Skyrim:Anga's Mill") and east of [Irkngthand](/wiki/Skyrim:Irkngthand "Skyrim:Irkngthand"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Great+Lift+at+Raldbthar)

Other exits:

-  **[Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand "Skyrim:Alftand")** — A large [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") southwest of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") containing [Dwarven automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons"), [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), and [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Alftand)
-  **[Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft")** — A medium-sized [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") southwest of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), [Dwarven automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons"), [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), and [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mzinchaleft)
-  **[Raldbthar](/wiki/Skyrim:Raldbthar "Skyrim:Raldbthar")** — A medium-sized [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") west-southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Raldbthar)
-  **[Tower of Mzark](/wiki/Skyrim:Tower_of_Mzark "Skyrim:Tower of Mzark")** — A small [Dwarven tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") in Blackreach. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Tower+of+Mzark)

## Related Quests

- **[Discerning the Transmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane")**: Uncover the secrets of the mysterious Dwemer lockbox.
- **[Elder Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Knowledge "Skyrim:Elder Knowledge")**: Recover an [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Scroll "Skyrim:Elder Scroll") to learn an [Ancient Secret](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrend "Skyrim:Dragonrend").
- **[A Return To Your Roots](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Return_To_Your_Roots "Skyrim:A Return To Your Roots")**: Go where a [famous alchemist](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinderion "Skyrim:Sinderion") could not in order to aid ground-breaking research.
- **[Scroll Scouting](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_Scouting "Skyrim:Scroll Scouting")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Obtain information on the Dragon Elder Scroll.

## Notes

- For historical information on Blackreach, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Blackreach "Lore:Blackreach").
- Aside from geode veins, Blackreach also has several ebony, gold, corundum, and other ore veins.
- Using the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout on the large orange globe hanging above the Silent City will summon the dragon [Vulthuryol](/wiki/Skyrim:Vulthuryol "Skyrim:Vulthuryol") to attack you. This, of course, will only happen once.
- One copy of the [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, MidYear, v6](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_MidYear,_v6 "Skyrim:2920, MidYear, v6")* can be found on a table at the top of the stands overlooking the arena-like ring just west of the [War Quarters](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Quarters "Skyrim:War Quarters").
- If you have the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") creation, some [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Supplies "Skyrim:Fishing Supplies") can be found by following the path leading out of Alftand Cathedral, as well as a bucket containing a [Fishing Rod](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Rod "Skyrim:Fishing Rod"), some Dwemer metal, and a dwarven dagger. Fish from [Underground](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_(activity)#Biomes "Skyrim:Fishing (activity)") waters can be caught here, and five [Tripod Spiderfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripod_Spiderfish "Skyrim:Tripod Spiderfish") can be manually picked up from the water.
- Although Blackreach is a dungeon, the game considers it to be outdoors. This makes the [Summon Arvak](/wiki/Skyrim:Summon_Arvak "Skyrim:Summon Arvak")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") spell and the [Storm Call](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Call "Skyrim:Storm Call") shout usable, but not the [Call Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Call_Dragon "Skyrim:Call Dragon") shout. In previous game versions, [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampirism "Skyrim:Vampirism") would suffer negative sun effects in Blackreach, but this was changed in an [official patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch").
  - Even with the patch, you still cannot fast travel here.
- [Sinderion's Field Laboratory](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinderion%27s_Field_Laboratory "Skyrim:Sinderion's Field Laboratory") and [Tower of Mzark](/wiki/Skyrim:Tower_of_Mzark "Skyrim:Tower of Mzark") do not respawn.
- The doors to the three Great Lift locations will reset if you are away from them long enough, and need to be reopened from the Blackreach side. The door to the Tower of Mzark stays open always if you have unlocked it twice, that means after you exit Tower of Mzark during [Elder Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Knowledge "Skyrim:Elder Knowledge"), it will reset, and need be opened once again from the Blackreach side, then it will stay open.
- Likewise, the entrances from the three Dwemer dungeons of Alftand, Mzinchaleft, and Raldbthar may reset, and have to be reopened from the dungeon side because of the necessity of using an Attunement Sphere, which cannot be used from below. This is also why it is impossible to use Blackreach to access one of the other Dwemer dungeons from below if you haven't cleared the dungeon all the way to its Blackreach entrance and unlocked it with your Attunement Sphere.

## Bugs

- Lifts to the surface can occasionally cause the game to freeze on the loading screen, thus preventing all actions apart from quick-loading.
  -  This can be fixed by pressing the tilde key to open the console and waiting 5-10 seconds, then pressing tilde again to close the console, or by repeatedly pressing Q or the appropriate assigned hotkey to open the favorites menu. This can also be prevented entirely by temporarily disabling autosaves on traveling, then enabling them after using the lifts. Another way of fixing this is typing in the console command "disableplayercontrols", closing the console, then reopening the console and typing in the command "enableplayercontrols".
  -  Hitting the guide button at the moment the loading screen goes away, but before it comes back, can also fix the glitch. Note that this glitch tends to occur when attempting to use the lift with more than one follower. When the glitch occurs, the screen will effectively go dark in an attempt to load; if autosave upon travel is enabled, all your previous autosave blocks will be overwritten with the autosave from using the lift. You will have to restart the Xbox or use the Xbox button to return to the dashboard and load Skyrim again. You will then have to choose a previous save before entering the lift that created the glitch.
  - Disabling autosave upon travel will prevent this bug from happening.
  - This appears to have been fixed by version 1.6 of the [Official Skyrim patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch#Version_1.6 "Skyrim:Patch"), although some may still experience this glitch.
- Using the Fireball spell on a Falmer may cause the game to crash.
- Casting a Summon Spell (e.g. Conjure Dremora Lord) will often cause the summoned creature to appear in a different location than that targeted by the caster. The creature may appear either to one side, behind the caster, or in areas with different vertical levels, on a different level.
- Sometimes followers can get stuck on the stairs of Sinderion's Lab.
  - Using [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") to push the follower off the stairs, or simply using the "wait" feature, can resolve this.
- A Falmer tent at the southeastern end, near the entrance to Raldbthar, cannot be entered. A Falmer enemy may spawn inside the tent, unable to leave.
- Entering a Falmer hut at the southwest end of Blackreach, near the Tower of Mzark, may cause you to become permanently stuck inside. For some reason, the collision around the hut's doorway allows the player to enter, but never to exit. This can also be observed with a Falmer that should spawn within the hut.
  - If you're a werewolf, you can enter beast form to get unstuck.
  - If a Falmer approaches, you can unstick yourself by performing a cinematic kill.
- Attempting to exit Blackreach to Mzinchaleft then immediately returning can cause Blackreach to have normal daylight or even snowy weather, just like any area above ground.
- Two Chaurus Reapers may spawn near the Catacombs entrance as completely unresponsive. Even when hit, they do not move or react.
- The corundum ore vein just south of the Farm Overseer's House cannot be interacted with.
- Attempting to enter Blackreach on any horse, which is done by activating the lift then immediately mounting the horse, can cause you to be placed out of bounds and unable to move. **?**
- Sometimes, when exiting Blackreach and reentering via a lift, the game might decide to put you into the dungeon twice simultaneously. This can get you stuck in an endless cycle of the game reloading the Blackreach interior and producing an endless cycle of autosaves, which will quickly load over any prior autosaves. These autosaves cannot be opened, as they are in "version zero". Autosave limits still apply, thus no loading from before the glitch works unless you have a deliberate save. If one is stuck because of this bug, then one should use the command

"Set BlackreachElevatorAlftandGlobal to 0" or "Set BlackreachElevatorRalbdbtharGlobal to 0" or "Set BlackreachElevatorMzinchaleftGlobal to 0",

according to the lift in question (it disables the lifts). After that, one may use the same command again, but replacing 0 by 1 to enable the lifts again.

- One of the Falmer tents is too low for you to enter. There is a falmer inside and a cinematic execution can leave you trapped inside.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- One of the Falmer tents may clip into the rock formation behind it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.8, addresses this issue. Several other references needed to be adjusted as a result of moving the tent.
- Followers may be unable to keep up with you if entering Blackreach via Mzinchaleft Gatehouse due to an incomplete navmesh.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.4, fixes this bug.
- The Blackreach mushrooms may miss their object bounds which can prevent them from being lit or culled properly when not in sight.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.7, fixes this bug.
- The Blackreach elevator systems could become stuck in an infinite loop due to timing issues on lower-end PCs.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.8, fixes this bug.

Blacksmith

The **Blacksmith** is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Skyrim:Blacksmith") who can be found working the forge within [Ashfall's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashfall%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Ashfall's Tear") if you choose to side with the [Tribunal Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Tribunal_Temple "Skyrim:Tribunal Temple") during the quest [Her Word Against Theirs](/wiki/Skyrim:Her_Word_Against_Theirs "Skyrim:Her Word Against Theirs"). Before this quest, the forge will be dilapidated, but it will be repaired if you help recruit more members for the cult.

He offers a selection of blacksmithing goods, including several pieces of [Indoril armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Indoril_Armor "Skyrim:Indoril Armor").

The Blacksmith Quarters in Windhelm

**Blacksmith Quarters** is a building on the east side of the market place in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") that belongs to [Oengul War-Anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Oengul_War-Anvil "Skyrim:Oengul War-Anvil"), the local [blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Skyrim:Blacksmith").

It is home to both Oengul and his assistant [Hermir Strong-Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Hermir_Strong-Heart "Skyrim:Hermir Strong-Heart"). The house itself does not serve as a shop; merchant services are offered at the forge area outside. There is only one zone, which is the [interior](#Blacksmith_Quarters).

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Oengul War-Anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Oengul_War-Anvil "Skyrim:Oengul War-Anvil") [Blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Blacksmith")  [Hermir Strong-Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Hermir_Strong-Heart "Skyrim:Hermir Strong-Heart")\* |

\* This person will take over running the shop if [Oengul War-Anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Oengul_War-Anvil "Skyrim:Oengul War-Anvil") dies.

### Exterior

Oengul's forge, located outside his home in Windhelm

During the day both [Oengul War-Anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Oengul_War-Anvil "Skyrim:Oengul War-Anvil") and [Hermir Strong-Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Hermir_Strong-Heart "Skyrim:Hermir Strong-Heart") can be found working at the forge. There is a tanning rack beside the forge, with a grindstone and workbench further to the right and against a wall to the north is a smelter. [Silda the Unseen](/wiki/Skyrim:Silda_the_Unseen "Skyrim:Silda the Unseen") will often use the forge as a source of warmth at night.

### Blacksmith Quarters

Hermir's bedroom in the Blacksmith Quarters

Upon entering the property there is a large open-plan area with fire pit along the north wall with a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") over it and a metal bowl containing three [tomatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato") on the floor beside it. To the left is a square wooden table with a joint of [horse meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Meat "Skyrim:Horse Meat") and [horker meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Meat "Skyrim:Horker Meat") on top and two baskets on the floor in front, one holds [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") and the other three [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"). Behind the table is a wall shelf with two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, two bunches of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") and a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") hanging from it. Beside the table is an empty cart. On the far side of the fire pit are three more wall shelves that mostly holding clutter along with an [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"). There is a chair in the northeastern corner and a long end table further along the east wall with a [blacksmith's apron](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith%27s_Apron "Skyrim:Blacksmith's Apron"), a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") and [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") on top. Against the south wall are several crates and an unusable [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"). Against the west wall, on the right of the entrance when entering are a row of three weapon racks, all of which are empty. In the center of the room is a large round table holding a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge") and a tomato.

There is a flight of stairs up to the second floor against the south wall heading to the east. At the top of the stairs is a large landing with a long wooden table against the east wall with an [iron greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Greatsword "Skyrim:Iron Greatsword"), a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), a [hide shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Shield "Skyrim:Hide Shield") and a [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield") on top. Against the north wall are a couple of bookcases holding sixteen common books including a non-skill version of *[Vernaccus and Bourlor](/wiki/Skyrim:Vernaccus_and_Bourlor "Skyrim:Vernaccus and Bourlor")*, a bottle of alto wine and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and in the northwestern corner is a chair. against the west wall is a small square wooden table holding an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword") and [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield") and a bottle of wine. By the stairwell is a small unit holding a bottle of alto wine and a leather strip.

To the right of the bookcases on the north wall is a doorway through into a bedroom containing a fireplace on the south wall with two chairs arranged in front of it. By one of the chairs is a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"). To the right of the fireplace is a small set of shelves holding a bottle of alto wine and a bottle of wine. There is a tall wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") against the west wall with an empty set of shelves to the right of it.

Opposite the fireplace, out from the north wall, so that you can walk all the way around it, is a single unowned bed used by Hermir Strong-Heart, with a small, low table on either side and a long unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing random items at the foot of it. In the northeast corner is a wash basin with a long end table against the east wall with a copy of *[Gods and Worship](/wiki/Skyrim:Gods_and_Worship "Skyrim:Gods and Worship")* on top.

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in the blacksmith's [Merchant Chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") every two days.

## Notes

- There is a  "Loot") Loot [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to the right of the entrance door.
- With the exception of most barrels and sacks, all containers in the house are [non-respawning](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning"), and you can safely store items in them.

## Bugs

- The house only has one bed, but two people live here so one of them would always be unable to sleep.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, addresses this issue. A second bed has been added. Ownership of each bed is now per NPC so they pick the same one each time. The navmesh has also been adjusted to accommodate this.

# Skyrim:Blacksmithing Tutorial

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Learn the basics of [smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant") |
| Location(s): | [Radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant") |
| Reward: | Products of Smithing |
| ID: | TutorialBlacksmithing |

A typical [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge")

## Radiant Options

This is a radiant quest which you can receive from any of the following people.

| QuestGiver | QuestGiverHome |
| --- | --- |
| [Adrianne Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Adrianne_Avenicci "Skyrim:Adrianne Avenicci") | [Warmaiden's](/wiki/Skyrim:Warmaiden%27s "Skyrim:Warmaiden's") ([Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun")) |
| [Alvor](/wiki/Skyrim:Alvor "Skyrim:Alvor") | [Alvor and Sigrid's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Alvor_and_Sigrid%27s_House "Skyrim:Alvor and Sigrid's House") ([Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood")) |
| [Lod](/wiki/Skyrim:Lod "Skyrim:Lod") (see [Bugs](#Bugs)) | [Lod's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Lod%27s_House "Skyrim:Lod's House") ([Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath")) |

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Forge an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") at the [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge").
2. Temper the iron dagger at the [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone").
3. Craft [leather](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather "Skyrim:Leather") at the [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack").
4. Craft a [hide helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Helmet "Skyrim:Hide Helmet") at the forge.
5. Temper the hide helmet at the [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench").

### Craft a Dagger

Take the [iron ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot") and the [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") from the quest giver and then use the [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") to create an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). As soon as the dagger is crafted, return it to the quest giver. Now they will ask you to sharpen the dagger with another iron ingot. Go to the [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") and sharpen the iron dagger, and present it to the smith.

### Craft a Helmet

Secondly, they will ask you to craft some [leather](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather "Skyrim:Leather"). Go to the [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") and craft leather, and again speak to the quest giver. Now you have to create a [hide helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Helmet "Skyrim:Hide Helmet") at the forge. Take the supplies you are given and use the forge to create the helmet, and then return to the smith.

Lastly, you have to temper the helmet. Use the [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench") to improve the hide helmet further, and return to the quest giver to complete the quest. They will allow you to keep the helmet and dagger that you have created as a reward.

## Notes

- Because this quest has a lot of objectives that can be completed very quickly, it is very useful if you are trying to earn the [Hero of the People](/wiki/Skyrim:Hero_of_the_People "Skyrim:Hero of the People") achievement.
- You can only initiate this quest during the day, when the quest giver is at work.

## Bugs

- Do not try to sharpen the blade or temper the helmet before you are told to, as the objective can not be completed until then. You will need to get another iron dagger or hide helmet to complete it.
- [Lod](/wiki/Skyrim:Lod "Skyrim:Lod") was supposed to be able to offer this quest as well, but he was left out of the quest condition formlist.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=17707))

## Quest Stages

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TutorialBlacksmithing stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TutorialBlacksmithing`.

# Skyrim:Blades

## Overview

This article is about the faction. For the class, see [Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Blade "Skyrim:Blade").

Sky Haven Temple, the last stronghold of the Blades

The **Blades** are a small group of [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") hunters, [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Talos "Lore:Talos") worshippers, and sworn protectors of [those of the Dragon blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dovahkiin "Skyrim:Dovahkiin") in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"). No longer are they the secret eyes and ears of the [Septim Emperors](/wiki/Lore:Septim_Dynasty "Lore:Septim Dynasty"); hunted and decimated by the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor"), they are but a shadow of their former glory. The Blades reformed with the return of the dragons. They are led by acting Grandmaster [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine"), one of the last surviving members, and are based in [Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple"). The Blades stand in opposition of the [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards"), and are strongly opposed to the existence of [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)"), whom they perceive as a menace.

For historical information on the Blades, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Blades "Lore:Blades").

## Blades in Skyrim

- [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine")

  

  Grandmaster Delphine
- [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern")

Once [Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple") is entered during [Alduin's Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Wall "Skyrim:Alduin's Wall"), it will become the headquarters of all Blades operations in Skyrim and you may live here if you choose to, so long as you get along with the Blades. You may recruit up to three [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") to join the Blades. The first recruit will take the oath right away, while the other two will begin training. The new recruits will train, patrol the area, and live in Sky Haven Temple, their former lives over. The Blade recruits will train with either Delphine, or one of the targets and training dummies; they will always use their preferred skill when training. The [Dragonslayer's Blessing](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonslayer%27s_Blessing "Skyrim:Dragonslayer's Blessing") may be received from Esbern upon request as well. The Blades will always show an opposition to the pacifist Greybeards, taking a stance that all dragons must be destroyed. The Blades recruits may also accompany you on trips to [slay dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Hunting "Skyrim:Dragon Hunting") living near dragon lairs. All Blade recruits are given a set of the standard [Blades armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Blades_Armor "Skyrim:Specialty Gear"), to which they will default in future: this is governed by the [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") skill, so keep this in mind when choosing recruits. If you choose the person in question as a follower in future, their Blades gear does not appear in their inventory to give back to you (although it does appear if they are killed). They can equip better gear, but apparently only do so while they are your follower, it appears they revert back to using the Blades gear if they leave your service. Also, before the follower joins be certain to retrieve any armor, helmet or shield that you might wish to keep since they are removed from the game and replaced by Blades equipment. They are also given a standard one-handed Blades Sword, although in this case it appears to be in addition to any other weapons they have, and their old weapons are not lost: thus if they prefer two-handed weapons or spells, and they have them, they will wield and use these in battle rather than the Blades sword.

## Related Quests

Quests involving the Blades include:

1. **[Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)")**: Retrieve the [Dragonstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonstone "Skyrim:Dragonstone").
2. **[The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Horn_of_Jurgen_Windcaller "Skyrim:The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller")**: Retrieve a [Greybeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards") artifact from [Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav").
3. **[A Blade in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Blade_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:A Blade in the Dark")**: Prove you are Dragonborn to [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine") by slaying the dragon [Sahloknir](/wiki/Skyrim:Sahloknir "Skyrim:Sahloknir").
4. **[Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity")**: Infiltrate a party at the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy").
5. **[A Cornered Rat](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Cornered_Rat "Skyrim:A Cornered Rat")**: Locate [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern").
6. **[Alduin's Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Wall "Skyrim:Alduin's Wall")**: Locate the prophecy within [Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple").
   - **[Rebuilding the Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades")**: Recruit new members for the Blades.
   - **[Dragon Hunting](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Hunting "Skyrim:Dragon Hunting")**: Kill a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") at its [lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs").
   - **[Dragon Research](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Research "Skyrim:Dragon Research")**: Help [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern") complete his research on [dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon").
7. **[Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending")**: Enforce a ceasefire to secure [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach").
   - **[Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(quest) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (quest)")**: Deal with a [potential threat](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)").

## Dialogue

Delphine training a recruit

|  |
| --- |
| After a follower is recruited into the Blades, they will greet you with one of these three phrases:   - *"I'm a Blade now, I can hardly believe it."* - *"By my honor, I pledge to rid [Tamriel](/wiki/Lore:Tamriel "Lore:Tamriel") of dragons."* - *"Dragonborn. What do you need?"* |

## Notes

A male Nord wearing [Blades armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades_Armor#Blades_Armor "Skyrim:Blades Armor")

- Any of the followers brought to Sky Haven Temple still function as followers, but will return to Sky Haven Temple after parting ways.
- If a follower is [a spouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage"), they can still join the Blades. Their home becomes Sky Haven Temple; however, they will only stay there if you decide to live at their house, otherwise they will stay in the home you choose.
- If a follower is [a personal steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Personal_Steward "Skyrim:Personal Steward")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"), they can still join the Blades. They will participate in Blades' quests, but will return to the [property they are in charge of](/wiki/Skyrim:Construction "Skyrim:Construction")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"), not Sky Haven Temple.
- Once a follower has become a Blade, he or she will be free to hire. This is particularly handy if your favorite followers are [hirelings](/wiki/Skyrim:Hireling "Skyrim:Hireling").
- Any Blades members that are slain cannot be replaced.
- The last of the Blades to survive the attack on Cloud Ruler Temple, Acilius Bolar, took refuge in [Bloated Man's Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloated_Man%27s_Grotto "Skyrim:Bloated Man's Grotto"). According to [his writ](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolar%27s_Writ "Skyrim:Bolar's Writ"), he later died at the hands of the Thalmor. His unique Blades sword, [Bolar's Oathblade](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolar%27s_Oathblade "Skyrim:Bolar's Oathblade"), can be found in the grotto under a statue of Talos before beginning the quest [Ill Met By Moonlight](/wiki/Skyrim:Ill_Met_By_Moonlight "Skyrim:Ill Met By Moonlight").
- [Fultheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Fultheim "Skyrim:Fultheim") of the [Nightgate Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn") possesses a Blades sword, and coupled with his comments on drinking away bad memories suggest that he was a Blade during the Great War.
- Version 2.0.3 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") moves the Blades into a new crime faction created just for them when they arrive at Sky Haven Temple. This avoids some complications from becoming [wanted](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime "Skyrim:Crime") in The Reach, which logically they wouldn't really care about.

Blaise

**Blaise** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child") who works and lives at [Katla's Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Katla%27s_Farm "Skyrim:Katla's Farm") near [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). He sleeps outside on a hay pile in the stables.

## Dialogue

When you first approach him, he may tell you:

:   *"You probably want someone else. I'm just the stable boy."*
:   *"I take care of the horses. And the goats. And the chickens. And the garden."*
:   *"Talk to [Geimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Geimund "Skyrim:Geimund") if you want a horse, or [Katla](/wiki/Skyrim:Katla "Skyrim:Katla") if you're looking for work. I can't help you."*

If spoken to directly he can be asked questions about himself:

:   **How do you like the farm?**
:   *"I hate it. Everyone feels sorry for me, so they don't treat me too bad, but..."*
:   **Sorry for what?** or **What was your story again?** (if you asked about him before)
:   *"Both my parents were in the Legion. There was... an ambush. Katla said she could feed me if I could make myself useful. I take care of the animals, run errands, that kind of thing. I guess it could be worse. But... I'm sick of sleeping outside with the horses. I want a real home, real parents. Not... this."*

You will then have a dialogue option to [adopt](/wiki/Skyrim:Child#Adoption "Skyrim:Child") him. You can only go through with the adoption if you have a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") with a child's bed and container.

Blasphemous Priest

The **Blasphemous Priest** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior_(class) "Skyrim:Warrior (class)") who may appear in the [Temple of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Temple of Kynareth") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") during the quest [The Dark Brotherhood Forever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dark_Brotherhood_Forever "Skyrim:The Dark Brotherhood Forever"). He will only be enabled if the [Night Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother") picks him as the contract giver. He carries a copy of *[A Kiss, Sweet Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Kiss,_Sweet_Mother "Skyrim:A Kiss, Sweet Mother")* and wields an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger").

He will be chosen randomly from a list of ten people who performed the Black Sacrament and want someone killed. When approached, he will choose between a total of ten possible targets, hand you a leveled amount of gold and blindly expect you to carry out the task.

He shares his dialogue with the nine other potential quest givers; see [this section](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dark_Brotherhood_Forever#Detailed_Walkthrough "Skyrim:The Dark Brotherhood Forever") for details.

## Related Quests

- **[The Dark Brotherhood Forever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dark_Brotherhood_Forever "Skyrim:The Dark Brotherhood Forever")**: Yet another child has prayed to their [mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother").

## Notes

- He is the only non-[Greybeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards") to wear [Greybeard's Robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeard%27s_Robes "Skyrim:Greybeard's Robes").

# Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (place)

## Overview

This article is about the place. For the quest, see [Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)").
