He seemed to be expecting us, and I'm afraid he led us here with the express purpose of eliminating the Nightingales once and for all. *Objective 40:* Slay Mercer Frey |
| 45 |  | Mercer Frey, betrayer of the Thieves Guild and Gallus's murderer is finally dead. Upon his death, a wave of magic issued from his body and has caused the already crumbling chamber to collapse and fill with water. *Objective 45:* Retrieve the Skeleton Key |
| 50 |  | Mercer Frey is dead and I've recovered the Skeleton Key of Nocturnal from his corpse. I need to escape Irkngthand before the place collapses around me. *Objective 50:* Escape from Irkngthand |
| 60 |  | Safe from the dangers below, Karliah, Brynjolf and I finally have a moment to breathe. Mecer *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* Frey is dead, the Skeleton Key of Nocturnal is in my possession and, most importantly, the Nightingales have survived. *Objective 60:* Speak to Karliah |
| 200 | ☑ | Karliah, Brynjolf and I have slain Mercer Frey, escaped Irkngthand and recovered the Skeleton Key. All that remains is returning the artifact to the Twilight Sepulcher where it belongs; a journey I must undertake alone. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 32, 33, 35, 37, 41, 47.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TG08B stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TG08B`.

# Skyrim:Blizzard Rest

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |

Blizzard Rest

**Blizzard Rest** is a [giant camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Camps "Skyrim:Giant Camps") south of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar").

## Related Quests

- **[Bounty: Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Giant "Skyrim:Bounty: Giant")**: Kill a problematic [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") for a bounty reward. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Kill the Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Giant_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Giant (Jarl)")**: Do a favor for the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") by killing a [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Walkthrough

The camp is a short distance from the road that runs between Dawnstar and [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"); if *[Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")* is installed, it is just east of [Heljarchen Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Heljarchen_Hall "Skyrim:Heljarchen Hall"). Two [giants](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") and two [mammoths](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth") occupy the camp. The camp is on a ledge with a rock overhang above, with the mammoths normally found below the ledge. The typical painted stones and mammoth bones surround the camp. The fire has a ring of rocks circling it. Two [charred skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide") are on stakes cooking over the fire. A few paces to the southwest of the fire is an expert-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") under the overhang, and to the south are three large [mammoth cheese bowls](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Cheese_Bowl "Skyrim:Mammoth Cheese Bowl"). The first giant is near the fire, while the second giant is either a short distance east next to a dead mammoth or roaming the tundra south of the camp.

# Skyrim:Bloated Man's Grotto

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Bloated Man's Grotto ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bloated+Man%27s+Grotto)) | | |

Bloated Man's Grotto

**Bloated Man's Grotto** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") north of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals") and [spriggans](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan"). It contains only one zone, *[Bloated Man's Grotto](#Bloated_Man.27s_Grotto)*.

The grotto during the quest

During the quest [Ill Met By Moonlight](/wiki/Skyrim:Ill_Met_By_Moonlight "Skyrim:Ill Met By Moonlight"), a [Great Hunt](/wiki/Lore:Great_Hunt "Lore:Great Hunt") is hosted here, and the sky is dominated by a [Bloodmoon](/wiki/Lore:Bloodmoon "Lore:Bloodmoon"). The regular inhabitants are replaced by [Sinding](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinding "Skyrim:Sinding") and a host of [hunters](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloated_Man%27s_Grotto_People "Skyrim:Bloated Man's Grotto People"), as Sinding tries to use the grotto as a sanctuary after escaping from [Falkreath jail](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Jail "Skyrim:Falkreath Jail").

## People

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| | Bloated Man's Grotto | | --- | | **[Ahjisi](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahjisi "Skyrim:Ahjisi")**  **[Batum gra-Bar](/wiki/Skyrim:Batum_gra-Bar "Skyrim:Batum gra-Bar")**  **[Eriana](/wiki/Skyrim:Eriana "Skyrim:Eriana")**  **[Heratar](/wiki/Skyrim:Heratar "Skyrim:Heratar")**  **[Hoddreid](/wiki/Skyrim:Hoddreid "Skyrim:Hoddreid")**  **[J'Kier](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27Kier "Skyrim:J'Kier")**  **[Ma'tasarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Ma%27tasarr "Skyrim:Ma'tasarr")**  **[Ra'kheran](/wiki/Skyrim:Ra%27kheran "Skyrim:Ra'kheran")**  **[Rissing](/wiki/Skyrim:Rissing "Skyrim:Rissing")**  **[Sinding](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinding "Skyrim:Sinding")**  **[Torkild the Fearsome](/wiki/Skyrim:Torkild_the_Fearsome "Skyrim:Torkild the Fearsome")**  **[Tsrasuna](/wiki/Skyrim:Tsrasuna "Skyrim:Tsrasuna")**  **[Yar gro-Gatuk](/wiki/Skyrim:Yar_gro-Gatuk "Skyrim:Yar gro-Gatuk")** | |

\* All of these hunters only appear during the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Ill_Met_By_Moonlight "Skyrim:Ill Met By Moonlight") to hunt the werewolf [Sinding](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinding "Skyrim:Sinding").

## Related Quests

- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Ill Met By Moonlight](/wiki/Skyrim:Ill_Met_By_Moonlight "Skyrim:Ill Met By Moonlight")**: Participate in the Daedric Prince [Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:Hircine "Skyrim:Hircine")'s Great Hunt.

### Exterior

The cave is south of [Sleeping Tree Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Tree_Camp "Skyrim:Sleeping Tree Camp") and north-northwest of [Ilinalta's Deep](/wiki/Skyrim:Ilinalta%27s_Deep "Skyrim:Ilinalta's Deep"), a short distance south of the main road between [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") and [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). The path leading to the entrance is marked by a pile of stones with human bones and a skull lying on them. Many [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") and [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), [purple](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"), and [red mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") grow along the path. A [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") fungus is to the right of the entrance, and a [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") fungus is to the left.

### Bloated Man's Grotto

The entrance leads into a natural tunnel, with torches on the walls lighting the way as it descends to the northwest. There is vegetation all along the passage. At the bottom, it opens into an idyllic grotto, with trees, plants, waterfalls, and flowers, [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit "Skyrim:Rabbit") and [butterflies](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Butterfly "Skyrim:Blue Butterfly") during the day, and [luna moths](/wiki/Skyrim:Luna_Moth "Skyrim:Luna Moth") and [torchbugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Torchbug "Skyrim:Torchbug") in the evening and at night, all sheltered from the outside world. The grotto consists of a single path that winds around the perimeter of a large vale. Depending on your level, there will be two animals ([wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf"), [sabre cats](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Sabre Cat"), or [cave bears](/wiki/Skyrim:Cave_Bear "Skyrim:Cave Bear")) ahead in a clearing. On your right is a ledge against the southeast wall, with a dead tree stump hiding an apprentice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). To the east is a small pool being fed by a low waterfall. Under the water is an unlocked wooden chest and two [Nordic barnacles](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle").

The grotto's inhabitants

A path continues to the north in front of the pool, passing between ledges on either side. Above you, a fallen tree spans the ledges over the path. Many of the rocks have [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") growing from them, with at least 45 moss found throughout the grotto. Ahead is a leveled animal, and hiding behind a tree stump on the left is a spriggan. You may also see a leveled animal high on a rock ahead; it is in the same place as where you first see Sinding during the quest Ill Met By Moonlight. The ledges on either side can be climbed in several places, where additional mountain flowers and [butterflies](/wiki/Skyrim:Monarch_Butterfly "Skyrim:Monarch Butterfly") can be found. To the right of the first spriggan is a stone flight of stairs. To the right of these stairs, it is possible to climb the rocks until you reach a small pool fed by another waterfall. Climb the rocks and head northwest from the pool to find a [gold ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein").

Shrine of Talos with Bolar's Oathblade

The path continues to the west, climbing a second flight of stairs before passing under an arch and into the remains of an old fort-like structure. In the center is an altar with a [shrine of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Talos "Skyrim:Shrines"), an empty random [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), and a random [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") on top. Behind this, in front of a statue of [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Talos "Lore:Talos"), is *[Bolar's Writ](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolar%27s_Writ "Skyrim:Bolar's Writ")* and [Bolar's Oathblade](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolar%27s_Oathblade "Skyrim:Bolar's Oathblade"), an enchanted [Blades sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades_Sword "Skyrim:Blades Sword"). There are many more hanging moss growing from the walls around this area, and opposite the statue among some rubble is an unlocked chest. Climbing the rocks here, it is possible to cross the walls above the arches and head west, staying as high as possible. At the end of the rocks is a hawk's nest, with a [hawk](/wiki/Skyrim:Hawk "Skyrim:Hawk") flying in circles and then landing. A second nest and hawk are to the south of the arches on top of the rocks. Each of these can be harvested for a [hawk beak](/wiki/Skyrim:Hawk_Beak "Skyrim:Hawk Beak") and three [hawk feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hawk_Feathers "Skyrim:Hawk Feathers"). Returning to the altar area and continuing to the west, you pass under another arch and descend a short flight of stairs.

Low point to access master-locked chest

Past the bottom of the stairs is another clearing, with a leveled animal, a spriggan hiding against the tree stump on the right, and a second spriggan hiding by another tree stump ahead on the left. The path then turns to the south, and in another clearing is another leveled animal. The path continues across a stream, then passes under another fallen tree and turns southeast. The next clearing has a spriggan hiding against a tree trunk, with a leveled animal standing over the corpse of a [deer](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer "Skyrim:Deer") in the center of the clearing. Climb the rim's rocky ridge at its lowest point to the east of this clearing to find a master-locked chest tucked between two taller rocks. From the clearing with the dead deer in the middle, the path continues to the east and eventually returns to the entrance.

The campsite used by Hircine's hunters

Bloated Man's Grotto is used by Sinding as a sanctuary during the quest Ill Met By Moonlight. During this quest, the grotto's appearance changes drastically. It becomes much darker, with a huge, red full moon dominating the sky. The shrine, Oathblade, and writ are removed, and the animals and spriggans are replaced by a variety of hunters. Upon entering during the quest, you will find an encampment in the first clearing where [J'Kier](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27Kier "Skyrim:J'Kier") sits dying. Around the camp [Batum gra-Bar](/wiki/Skyrim:Batum_gra-Bar "Skyrim:Batum gra-Bar"), [Hoddreid](/wiki/Skyrim:Hoddreid "Skyrim:Hoddreid"), and [Ma'tasarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Ma%27tasarr "Skyrim:Ma'tasarr") already lie dead among two small tents containing bedrolls and two other bedrolls by a campfire. The latter two bedrolls are still usable. The path to the northwest is blocked by broken tree trunks. Following the path past the pool and continuing onward, Sinding will spot you from atop a rock high above. You can decide to spare him or kill him. As you continue up the stairs, you will find [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") hanging from the arches. Regardless of your choice, Sinding will run off to the west and start killing the hunters with or without you. As you descend the stairs, [Rissing](/wiki/Skyrim:Rissing "Skyrim:Rissing") will attack, shortly followed by [Tsrasuna](/wiki/Skyrim:Tsrasuna "Skyrim:Tsrasuna"). In the next clearing, you will find [Eriana](/wiki/Skyrim:Eriana "Skyrim:Eriana"), [Torkild the Fearsome](/wiki/Skyrim:Torkild_the_Fearsome "Skyrim:Torkild the Fearsome"), and [Yar gro-Gatuk](/wiki/Skyrim:Yar_gro-Gatuk "Skyrim:Yar gro-Gatuk"), who will attack in unison. Cross the stream and continue to the next clearing to find [Ahjisi](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahjisi "Skyrim:Ahjisi"), [Heratar](/wiki/Skyrim:Heratar "Skyrim:Heratar"), and [Ra'kheran](/wiki/Skyrim:Ra%27kheran "Skyrim:Ra'kheran"), who will also make quite a combination.

## Notes

- The Oathblade is only present in the non-quest version of the grotto, and the location will only be marked as cleared after killing the animals and spriggans in the non-quest version. Therefore, if you wish to acquire the Oathblade and/or mark the location as cleared while letting Sinding live here in peace, you must visit the grotto before the quest Ill Met By Moonlight, as it won't revert to its non-quest version without killing Sinding.
  -  The grotto can be reverted to its non-quest form during Ill Met By Moonlight by opening the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") and entering the codes `prid 95586` and `disable`.
- Entering the grotto when directed by Ill Met By Moonlight will result in the time being set to 11pm upon entering, unless you enter the grotto between 7pm and 2am. If the first case is true, you may lose your [rested](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping "Skyrim:Sleeping") bonus, even if you sleep right before entering the grotto. If you are using [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode"), you may instantly incur [fatigue](/wiki/Skyrim:Fatigue "Skyrim:Fatigue").

# Skyrim:Blood Horker

## Overview

[Japhet's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Japhet%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Japhet's Folly"), the secret fortress of the Blood Horkers

The **Blood Horkers** are a notorious group of pirates led by a powerful battlemage, [Haldyn](/wiki/Skyrim:Haldyn "Skyrim:Haldyn"), who prowl the waters of the [Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sea_of_Ghosts "Skyrim:Sea of Ghosts"), raiding alongside the northern coastline of [Tamriel](/wiki/Lore:Tamriel "Lore:Tamriel"). The [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") has given the pirates the opportunity to increase their attacks without fear of serious retaliation from either the [Empire](/wiki/Lore:Empire "Lore:Empire") or [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). In fact, the only ships which sail the Sea of Ghosts unscathed are those owned by Clan Shatter-Shield, a *"very powerful family in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm")"*, due to an [agreement](/wiki/Skyrim:Suvaris_Atheron%27s_Logbook "Skyrim:Suvaris Atheron's Logbook") forged with Shatter-Shield gold between Blood Horker captain [Stig Salt-Plank](/wiki/Skyrim:Stig_Salt-Plank "Skyrim:Stig Salt-Plank") and [Suvaris Atheron](/wiki/Skyrim:Suvaris_Atheron "Skyrim:Suvaris Atheron"), the employee of the clan's patriarch, [Torbjorn Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Torbjorn_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Torbjorn Shatter-Shield"), and the overseer of their shipping operations. Through this agreement, the Shatter-Shields hold a monopoly on foreign shipping, as their competitors are dealt with by the pirates. Recently, the Blood Horkers have even been [interfering](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East") in the operations of the powerful [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company").

The Blood Horkers *"draw council"* in their island fortress, [Japhet's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Japhet%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Japhet's Folly"), the location of which is kept secret through discretion and Haldyn's magic, which he uses to create fog to hide the island.

The first five entries on this page are encountered in Japhet's Folly while the last two are part of the random encounter.

## Related Quests

- **[Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East")**: Help the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") take care of some pirates.

Blood Horker Wizard

These two **Blood Horkers** are [bandit wizards](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Wizard "Skyrim:Bandit Wizard"). They each wear [fur armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Armor "Skyrim:Fur Armor") with a pair of leveled [light boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor") (up to [scaled](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled "Skyrim:Scaled") quality). They each carry a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") (up to [daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric") in quality), a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick"), and 25-125 gold, dependent on their level.

Blood Horker Bandit

These four **Blood Horkers** are members of the [bandit class](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)"). They each wear a set of leveled [light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor_(item) "Skyrim:Light Armor (item)"), including boots and bracers (up to [scaled](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled "Skyrim:Scaled") in quality). They each carry a leveled [weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") (up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") in quality) and 25-125 gold, dependent on their level.

| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Very Aggressive |

Two-Handed Blood Horker Bandit

These two **Blood Horkers** are members of the [bandit class](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)"). They each wear a set of leveled [light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor_(item) "Skyrim:Light Armor (item)"), including boots and bracers (up to [scaled](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled "Skyrim:Scaled") in quality). They each carry a leveled [two-handed weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-Handed_Weapons "Skyrim:Two-Handed Weapons") (up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") in quality) and up to 25-125 gold, dependent on their level.

Blood Horker out for revenge

This **Blood Horker** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") member of the [bandit class](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)"). He wears a set of leveled [light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor_(item) "Skyrim:Light Armor (item)"), including boots and bracers (up to [scaled](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled "Skyrim:Scaled") in quality). He carries a leveled [two-handed weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-Handed_Weapons "Skyrim:Two-Handed Weapons") (up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") in quality) and 25-125 gold, dependent on his level.

He is [randomly encountered](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Blood_Horker_Revenge "Skyrim:World Interactions") after completing [Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East"). He hunts you down to seek revenge on you for your actions during the quest.

He can shout:

:   *"Horkers' revenge!"*
:   *"Yarr!"*
:   *"Avast, dog!"*
:   *"Die, ya cowardly lubber!"*
:   *"This is for Haldyn!"*

# Skyrim:Blood in the Water

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: *not written*  **Reward**: *not written* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Deliver vengeance upon the enemies of the [Bloodfall Queen](/wiki/Lore:Bloodfall_Queen "Lore:Bloodfall Queen").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Any innkeeper |
| Location(s): | [Lost Knife Hideout](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Knife_Hideout "Skyrim:Lost Knife Hideout") |
| Reward: | [Headman's Cleaver](/wiki/Skyrim:Headman%27s_Cleaver_(item) "Skyrim:Headman's Cleaver (item)") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE068\_Quest |
| Added by: | [Headman's Cleaver](/wiki/Skyrim:Headman%27s_Cleaver "Skyrim:Headman's Cleaver") |

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to an innkeeper.
2. Read the [Letter from Shogarz gro-Batul](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Shogarz_gra-Batul "Skyrim:Letter from Shogarz gra-Batul").
3. Eliminate the bandits in [Lost Knife Hideout](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Knife_Hideout "Skyrim:Lost Knife Hideout").
4. Retrieve the Headman's Cleaver.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Talking to any innkeeper will give you this quest. They will hand you a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Shogarz_gra-Batul "Skyrim:Letter from Shogarz gra-Batul") that explains that remnants of a group of bandits called the Greencap Bandits have stolen the Headman's Cleaver of the [Bloodfall Kingdom](/wiki/Lore:Bloodfall_Kingdom "Lore:Bloodfall Kingdom"). The Bloodfall Queen wants vengeance and will grant the Headman's Cleaver to whoever eliminates the Greencap Bandits.

Once you have read the letter, travel to [Lost Knife Hideout](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Knife_Hideout "Skyrim:Lost Knife Hideout"). There are two parts to the cave system - Lost Knife Cave and Lost Knife Hideout. In Lost Knife Cave, there will be several Greencap Bandits you will have to fight to find the entrance to Lost Knife Hideout. You will have to defeat more Greencap Bandits inside, until you reach the area with cages. This is where the thief, known as the 'Darkwater Snake', will be located, as well as several Greencap Bandits. Defeat the Darkwater Snake and loot his body for the stolen cleaver, as well as a full set of unenchanted Orcish armor. [Shogarz gro-Batul's](/wiki/Skyrim:Shogarz_gro-Batul "Skyrim:Shogarz gro-Batul") dead body will be lying in another cage, and looting him will give you [Shogarz's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Shogarz%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Shogarz's Journal"). [Urzog's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Urzog%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Urzog's Journal") will also be sitting on one of the tables.

## Bugs

- It is possible that the [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Shogarz_gra-Batul "Skyrim:Letter from Shogarz gra-Batul") from Shogarz doesn't appear in your inventory after getting the quest. This is possible when a radiant quest for a bandit camp indicates the same camp, and is completed before getting the letter. **?**
  -  A workaround is either to either enter `setstage ccBGSSSE068_Quest 30` in the console to update the quest stage, or `player.additem FExxx801 1` to place the letter in your inventory.

## Quest Stages

| Blood in the Water (ccBGSSSE068\_Quest) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Talking to innkeepers has always been a good way to find work. I should head to the local inn and see if there's anything worthwhile. *Objective 10:* Ask an innkeeper for work |
| 20 |  | Talking to innkeepers has always been a good way to find work. I received a note from one that may provide a lead. *Objective 20:* Read the Letter from Shogarz gra-Batul *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* |
| 30 |  | I received a note from a vassal of the Bloodfall Queen stating a group of bandits have stolen her weapon. I should head to Lost Knife Hideout to see what's become of it. *Objective 30:* Eliminate the bandits in Lost Knife Hideout |
| 40 |  | I received a note from a vassal of the Bloodfall Queen stating a group of bandits have stolen her weapon. I made my way to Lost Knife Hideout and encountered their leader. *Objective 40:* Retrieve the Headman's Cleaver |
| 100 | ☑ | I received a note from a vassal of the Bloodfall Queen stating a group of bandits have stolen her weapon. I made my way to Lost Knife Hideout and retrieved the Headman's Cleaver from the bandits. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 50, 60, 70, 80, 90, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE068_Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE068_Quest`.

# Skyrim:Blood on the Ice

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **[Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") is plagued by a shadowy killer.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Windhelm Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Guard "Skyrim:Windhelm Guard") (see [this section](#How_to_Start_the_Quest) for details) |
| Location(s): | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") |
| Reward: | Allows decoration of [Hjerim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjerim "Skyrim:Hjerim") when purchased, optional [Necromancer Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer_Amulet "Skyrim:Necromancer Amulet") |
| ID: | MS11, MS11b |

A serial killer is on the loose in Windhelm

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Go to the murder scene in Windhelm's graveyard and talk to the guard.
2. Talk to [Jorleif](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorleif "Skyrim:Jorleif") in the Palace of Kings in Windhelm.
3. Talk to [Helgird](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgird "Skyrim:Helgird") in Windhelm's [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Windhelm) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Windhelm)").
4. Follow the trail of blood to [Hjerim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjerim "Skyrim:Hjerim") and obtain the key.
5. Search Hjerim for evidence.
6. Talk to [Viola Giordano](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano "Skyrim:Viola Giordano") and [Calixto Corrium](/wiki/Skyrim:Calixto_Corrium "Skyrim:Calixto Corrium").
7. Make an important [choice](#Follow_Your_Instincts).
8. Patrol the Stone Quarter at night and catch the murderer.
9. Report back to Jorleif.

### A Killer on the Loose

When you first visit Windhelm, a few of the citizens and guards will mention a serial killer on the loose. A general fear is noticeable, but nobody will really talk about the killings, and it remains nothing but a rumor. When the right conditions have been met (see [this section](#How_to_Start_the_Quest) on how to trigger), the body of the [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall") barmaid, [Susanna the Wicked](/wiki/Skyrim:Susanna_the_Wicked "Skyrim:Susanna the Wicked"), will appear, surrounded by witnesses, in the graveyard. If you approach the scene, a [guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Guard "Skyrim:Windhelm Guard") will stop you and explain a bit about the murders. The guard also explains about the local guards being too busy with the war to do any real investigation, and they would gladly accept some help from you. For starters, he tasks you with questioning the three townsfolk gathered around the body.

### Investigator of Windhelm

On a rare venture outside the [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Windhelm) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Windhelm)"), [Helgird](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgird "Skyrim:Helgird") will be little help at the moment, but will point out that Susanna's coin purse is still intact. [Calixto Corrium](/wiki/Skyrim:Calixto_Corrium "Skyrim:Calixto Corrium") claims he 'saw a fellow running away, but didn't get a good look at him', while local beggar [Silda the Unseen](/wiki/Skyrim:Silda_the_Unseen "Skyrim:Silda the Unseen") didn't make it to the scene before Susanna was dead and the killer gone. The guard will not be particularly surprised with the lack of hard evidence or witnesses, and will point you towards Castle Steward [Jorleif](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorleif "Skyrim:Jorleif") for assistance and helpful advice.

*"Large diagonal cut from left shoulder..."*

In the [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings"), Jorleif will be shocked to hear about the third killing, and will gladly accept your help. He will promise you assistance from himself and all the town guards during the investigation. A map marker will now always point towards him, but he will rarely have anything helpful to add. Now it's time to investigate the crime scene without interference from the guard. Susanna's body will have been removed from the crime scene, and only the spatters of blood remain. The guard has noticed the blood as well, and hints that this evidence possibly holds a clue; however, for now you are urged to talk to [Helgird](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgird "Skyrim:Helgird") in the Hall of the Dead. Due to her profession and life-long experience with dead bodies, she may be able to come up with some answers.

Enter the Hall of the Dead and find Helgird busy examining Susanna's dead body, obviously puzzled by the large diagonal cuts she finds. When asked, she will reveal the shape of the cuts to be somewhat unusual, like they were made with a curved blade designed for embalming, the exact tools she uses. You can choose to indicate her involvement in the killings or simply to leave the conversation, but the results are the same. Helgird will refuse to speak to you further and will ask to be left in peace so she can prepare the body for the funeral. Because both [Jorleif](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorleif "Skyrim:Jorleif") and the guard are unable to do anything at the moment, your only hope for finding a clue is in the graveyard.

The remaining evidence seems to be a trail of blood leading from the graveyard. Follow the bloody trail around the corner and up the stairs, where it ends at the entrance to [Hjerim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjerim "Skyrim:Hjerim"), a huge manor opposite the [House of Clan Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:House of Clan Cruel-Sea"). (If you chose to follow the bloody trail before speaking to Helgird, the map marker pointing toward her will now be gone.)

### Hjerim

The front door is locked, so either pick the lock or ask Jorleif and/or any guard in town about access to Hjerim. They will briefly tell you about how the house used to belong to the now deceased Friga Shatter-Shield, and it has been abandoned ever since her untimely death. They will also point you towards her mother, [Tova Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Tova_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Tova Shatter-Shield"). Wait for Tova to leave her house. She will be browsing the market between 11am and 3pm, while she spends her afternoons at Candlehearth Hall. When you approach the grieving mother, it becomes apparent that Friga was one of the victims of the killer. Naturally, Tova will be more than willing to hand you the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Hjerim "Skyrim:Key to Hjerim") so you can go take a look inside. If you cannot find her, she may be in her home dead after committing suicide (if you have previously committed a certain murder for the Dark Brotherhood) and you can simply take the key off her body.

The secret chamber

When entering Hjerim, a [quest update](#Journal._Entries) will immediately tell you to look for clues, so take a look around. The blood trail leads to a chest in the southeastern corner, so investigate it and pry it open. Within, you will find eleven pamphlets called *[Beware the Butcher!](/wiki/Skyrim:Beware_the_Butcher! "Skyrim:Beware the Butcher!")* along with the *[Butcher's Journal #1](/wiki/Skyrim:Butcher_Journal_1 "Skyrim:Butcher Journal 1")*. Even though your quest journal now encourages you to follow up on these clues, keep looking around the house. Ignore the mead scattered on the floor and proceed to the two wardrobes in the western alcove. The wardrobe to the right is nailed to the wall, so open it and remove the false back panel. This will reveal the killer's hideout, a room filled with bones, bloody remains and the suspected embalming instruments. Investigate the altar and pick up the *[Butcher's Journal #2](/wiki/Skyrim:Butcher_Journal_2 "Skyrim:Butcher Journal 2")* for more evidence. Leave the room, and look at the small shelf between the wardrobes. It contains even more pamphlets, but also a [strange amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Strange_Amulet "Skyrim:Strange Amulet"). This is the last item of evidence, so make sure to pick it up. Read the pamphlet to learn about a Windhelm citizen named [Viola Giordano](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano "Skyrim:Viola Giordano"). Before leaving, if you want to avoid investigating Hjerim with Viola later on, pick up *[Butcher's Journal #2](/wiki/Skyrim:Butcher_Journal_2 "Skyrim:Butcher Journal 2")*, if you want to experience the full quest scene, just taking *[Beware the Butcher!](/wiki/Skyrim:Beware_the_Butcher! "Skyrim:Beware the Butcher!")* and [Strange Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Strange_Amulet "Skyrim:Strange Amulet") is enough, *[Butcher's Journal #1](/wiki/Skyrim:Butcher_Journal_1 "Skyrim:Butcher Journal 1")* has nothing to do with progressing the quest stage.

### Follow up on the Clues

Pay a quick visit to the helpful Jorleif (or a guard) for advice on how to proceed. When you show him the amulet, he will be quite puzzled but will point you to Calixto at the [House of Curiosities](/wiki/Skyrim:Calixto%27s_House_of_Curiosities "Skyrim:Calixto's House of Curiosities") for an opinion. When asked about the term 'the Butcher' he will spitefully refer you to Viola Giordano, the author of the pamphlets and the one to seek out for background information on the killings. At this point, map markers will point to both Viola and Calixto, but it is recommended to visit Calixto first.

#### Calixto Corrium

Calixto had opened up his small museum with his now-deceased sister, showcasing the various items they found during the adventures they shared back in the day. These days, Calixto spends most of his time sitting in a chair doing absolutely nothing but mourning the loss of his sister and rambling about how happy she'd have been seeing all the curious items under one roof. Not surprisingly, Calixto will, for a small fee, offer a guided tour around the small House of Curiosities and explain the background for a few of the items. It is a good idea to accept this tour, just for the investigation. When you present him with the strange amulet, he will tell you that it's the Wheelstone, traditionally carried by court mages. He will then offer to take it off your hands for 500 gold. Due to a [bug](#Bugs) with the amulet, it is recommended to accept this offer.

#### Viola Giordano

Viola is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") who tends to wander the streets of Windhelm during the day and hang out at [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall") in the evening. Track her down (with a "Beware the Butcher!" flyer from Hjerim in your inventory) and question her. She is understandably upset about the presence of a serial killer and the apathy of the town guards. If you failed to pick up the journal in the hidden chamber back in Hjerim, Viola will immediately take interest in the old house and set off at a running pace to help with the investigation. If you already have the journal, Viola will point to [Wuunferth](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuunferth_the_Unliving "Skyrim:Wuunferth the Unliving"), the court mage in the Palace of the Kings, as the most likely person to be experimenting with Necromancy. If you chose to speak to Viola before Calixto, the map marker pointing toward him will now be gone. Still, go sell him the strange amulet before going anywhere near the Palace of the Kings. This will net you 500 gold and one less [bug](#Bugs) to worry about.

**At this point, your next decision will affect how the quest proceeds, and whether the killer is able to strike again.**

Even if the map marker now points you towards the Palace and your journal tells you to confront Jorleif with the evidence against the court mage, talking to Jorleif can be fatal for the townsfolk of Windhelm. Another option is available, although it's unsaid. You can go directly to the accused [Wuunferth](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuunferth_the_Unliving "Skyrim:Wuunferth the Unliving") and confront him yourself, without ever talking to Jorleif.

- See [this section](#Wuunferth) if you choose to confront **Wuunferth**.
- See [this section](#Jorleif) if you choose to speak to **Jorleif**.

Your reward will remain the same regardless of your choice.

#### Wuunferth

Wuunferth the Unliving lives a secluded life in the Palace of the Kings, but you are free to go visit him at any time. During the day, he will be in his quarters (first door on the left on entering, upstairs, at the far end). He spends his nights wandering around downstairs. Confront him with the rumors about him performing necromancy. He will be quite insulted and will retort that he's a member in good standing of the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)"). When you mention the journals and describe the amulet he will immediately identify it as the legendary [Necromancer Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer_Amulet "Skyrim:Necromancer Amulet"), and dismiss Calixto's theories about it being the Wheelstone.

He reveals that he's also been investigating the killings in Windhelm for quite some time. Noting a pattern with their location and timing, he predicts the killer will strike again the next day in the Stone Quarter, and asks you to keep watch. Now leave Wuunferth alone, ignore the map marker still pointing towards Jorleif, and head to the Stone Quarter and wait until nighttime.

Proceed with the walkthrough in [this section](#Catch_the_Killer.21).

#### Jorleif

*"Has the whole city lost their brains?"*

When you tell Jorleif that Wuunferth is the main suspect, and about the necromancer lair in Hjerim, he will be shocked at first; he will, however, find the evidence convincing enough to take action. After thanking you for making the streets of Windhelm safe again, he will set off towards the guard patrolling the palace entrance and order him to come along for an arrest. At this point, the quest will end and you will be left behind in the main hall, without any reward whatsoever.

If you follow Jorleif and the guard into Wuunferth's chambers and eavesdrop during the arrest, a frustrated Wuunferth will claim that he was investigating the murders as well, and will shout that this isn't over when the guard drags him to the [barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Barracks "Skyrim:Windhelm Barracks"). At this point, it will be impossible to discuss the subject with any of the characters.

*"Looks like you aren't such a sharp investigator after all."*

After three full calendar days spent outside Windhelm, you will see a familiar scene upon your return. A guard will be standing next to yet another slain victim (she is on the right of Candlehearth Hall when approaching from the Palace of the Kings): an [Altmer](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") named [Arivanya](/wiki/Skyrim:Arivanya "Skyrim:Arivanya") from [Windhelm Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Stables "Skyrim:Windhelm Stables"). The guard will be devastated and quick to inform you of your failure. A new quest with the same name will pop up in your journal, and the guard will suggest you remedy your mistake by talking to the imprisoned Wuunferth. Head to the barracks underneath the Palace and speak to the wizard. When you tell him that the Butcher has claimed yet another victim, he will point out that he's behind bars, and make a jab at your abilities as an investigator. When you tell him about the journal and the amulet, he will deny any knowledge of a journal and ask you to describe the shape of the amulet. He will then identify it as the rare and legendary [Necromancer Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer_Amulet "Skyrim:Necromancer Amulet"). While he rejects Calixto's Wheelstone theory on the spot, he will reveal that he has noted a pattern in the location and timing of the killings, and asks you to keep watch in the Stone Quarter at night, as he predicts the killer will strike again.

### Catch the Killer!

The killer strikes again.

When you head outside, the Stone Quarter will be incredibly quiet. The entire market is usually devoid of people at night, with the exception of a guard that may be present. You can spot the murderer following his final potential victim through the graveyard and the alley, up to the steps into the market from the west. As they enter the market, you will witness elderly museum owner [Calixto Corrium](/wiki/Skyrim:Calixto_Corrium "Skyrim:Calixto Corrium") sneak up behind a female citizen (normally [Arivanya](/wiki/Skyrim:Arivanya "Skyrim:Arivanya"), but another woman will be randomly chosen if she is already dead), with his knife drawn for the next kill. You can attack Calixto or use a spell on him to save his would-be victim. If you fail to dispose of him before he slits her throat, or if you attack Calixto and save her, he will panic and take off at a running pace towards his necromancer chamber in Hjerim. Follow him and be ready for a fight, although he shouldn't pose much of a problem. Once dead, loot him for the now-restored Necromancer Amulet (if you sold it to him) and a few other valuable items. Make sure to pick up his [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Calixto%27s_Key "Skyrim:Calixto's Key"), as it will help you reveal the truth behind the murders. If you managed to slay him outside, guards will arrive and point you towards Jorleif for one final conversation. If you slay him outside with a ranged attack, the guards will not approach even after you loot the body, instead continuing to patrol the area. When you speak to Jorleif, he will thank you and say that the city guard will be more cordial to you in the future.

While optional, it is worth your time to pay a visit to Calixto's now abandoned museum of curiosities to find out the motive behind his murders. In the upstairs area, you will find his chest, unlocked with the key you claimed from his body. Inside are all of his embalming tools, along with the first part of his *[Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Butcher_Journal "Skyrim:Butcher Journal")*. When reading through it, it becomes apparent that the untimely death of his sister Lucilla drove him to madness and that the murders, body parts, and necromancer rituals were all part of a desperate attempt to bring her back to life.

After completing the quest, Windhelm guards will sometimes say, *"You did this city a great service by catching that killer. Well done."* or *"I was this close to catching that killer. I swear it."*

## How to Start the Quest

There's a global variable counter that will increase each time you enter Windhelm or the immediate surrounding area, either by walking or fast-traveling. It need reach at least 4 to make the quest available. When arriving [Windhelm Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Stables "Skyrim:Windhelm Stables"), You can use the console command `show MS11EnteringWindhelmCount` to check it, it must be 1 if you arrive the first time, and then you can use console command `tb` to show the border of Windhelm immediate surrounding area, the nearest border is just the main rode west of the [Alfarinn](/wiki/Skyrim:Alfarinn "Skyrim:Alfarinn")'s carriage a bit. Then walk back and forth the border twice to make the `MS11EnteringWindhelmCount` increased to 3. Then make sure the time is between 7pm and 7am, if not, wait until the time meets. Then walk back and forth the border one more time to make the `MS11EnteringWindhelmCount` increased to 4, then enter Windhelm.

If `MS11EnteringWindhelmCount` is increased to 4 but the time isn't between 7pm and 7am, the quest will not be available, you'll have to enter one more time in the right time, which will increase `MS11EnteringWindhelmCount` to 5 or greater.

[Tova Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Tova_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Tova Shatter-Shield") and [Arivanya](/wiki/Skyrim:Arivanya "Skyrim:Arivanya") also need to be alive (see [bugs section](#Bugs)).

When the quest becomes available, besides the dead [Susanna the Wicked](/wiki/Skyrim:Susanna_the_Wicked "Skyrim:Susanna the Wicked"), the lock to [Hjerim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjerim "Skyrim:Hjerim") will also change from a "key required"-lock to a Master-level lock.

If you prefer to start the quest before `MS11EnteringWindhelmCount` reaches 4, you can manage to obtain [Key to Hjerim](/wiki/Skyrim:Keys#Key_to_Hjerim "Skyrim:Keys") from [Tova Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Tova_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Tova Shatter-Shield"), then enter Hjerim and pick up one of the Beware the Butcher! pamphlets to trigger the quest. The quest can't be triggered if the unofficial patch is installed. However, the quest will not start in the same way as outlined in the walkthrough above; you will have to figure out what to do on your own without help from Jorleif, however all of the same options will be open to you except that none of the witnesses will be present in the graveyard; you can sell Calixto the Strange Amulet, you can have Wuunferth arrested or talk to him to catch Calixto, and you will have to talk to Viola in order to continue on with the quest after picking up a pamphlet.

## Notes

- Either civil war side is joined, this quest has nothing to do with [Thane of Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Eastmarch "Skyrim:Thane of Eastmarch") without unofficial patch, and this quest must be completed if unofficial patch is installed.
- There are three known murder victims prior to those encountered on the quest: Friga Shatter-Shield, the twin sister of [Nilsine](/wiki/Skyrim:Nilsine_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Nilsine Shatter-Shield"); Isabella, as mentioned by [Adonato Leotelli](/wiki/Skyrim:Adonato_Leotelli "Skyrim:Adonato Leotelli"); and Fjotli Cruel-Sea, as mentioned by both her father [Torsten](/wiki/Skyrim:Torsten_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:Torsten Cruel-Sea") and [Niranye](/wiki/Skyrim:Niranye "Skyrim:Niranye") during the quest [Summerset Shadows](/wiki/Skyrim:Summerset_Shadows "Skyrim:Summerset Shadows"). Since Hjerim's hidden room contains several peoples' remains, these hint that the killer was also either a grave robber, or committed even more murders.
  - Despite there being (at least) three victims prior to Susanna, the guard near her body will claim that she is the third victim.
- If you've killed [Nilsine](/wiki/Skyrim:Nilsine_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Nilsine Shatter-Shield") in order to get a bonus reward in the quest [Mourning Never Comes](/wiki/Skyrim:Mourning_Never_Comes "Skyrim:Mourning Never Comes"), Tova will be dead inside her house, and you must retrieve the key to Hjerim from her corpse in time or it will disappear after several days.
- When Arivanya is killed by the Butcher, she may show the same type of wounds as Susanna did.
- Sometimes, on completion of this quest, the message that the quest is completed will be displayed twice. This is because two quests with the same name are running simultaneously. The second instance of quest completion occurs due to Wuunferth being absolved of guilt.

### Initiating the Quest

- Although most of the NPCs needed for the quest to initiate are marked as essential, another quest, namely the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") quest [Mourning Never Comes](/wiki/Skyrim:Mourning_Never_Comes "Skyrim:Mourning Never Comes"), will encourage you to kill [Nilsine Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Nilsine_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Nilsine Shatter-Shield"). Even though she is not related to this quest, her mother, [Tova Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Tova_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Tova Shatter-Shield"), will commit suicide if Nilsine is killed, and will therefore render this quest impossible to initiate.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.1, fixes this bug.
- This quest can fail to start if Susanna's body is purged by the corpse cleanup code.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.1, addresses this issue. A new replacement body is generated to correct this as well as making the body's alias optional so the quest will start.
- If Viola has died for some reason the quest may not start or will be impossible to finish.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.5, fixes this bug.
- [Arivanya](/wiki/Skyrim:Arivanya "Skyrim:Arivanya"), the stable hand, is also needed for this quest to trigger, but is not marked as essential.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.1, fixes this bug.
  -  This can also be fixed by reviving the characters with the console commands `prid <RefID of NPC>`, `enable`, `moveto player` (for Nilsine because her body doesn't disappear), `resurrect` and `resetAI`. This fix works on Skyrim version 1.7 but only after a day has passed after resurrecting NPCs.
- If you [capture Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm") for the Imperials before triggering the graveyard scene, the witnesses and the corpse will still show up, but the guard may not, since the Windhelm guards have been replaced by Imperial Legion soldiers. This makes it impossible to start the quest. **?**
  -  The remaining portion of this bug has been fixed by version 1.2.4 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch").
  -  Use the console command `sqv ms11` to bring up a list of quest variables and search for a RefID labeled "CrimeSceneInvestigator", then use the commands `prid <Investigator's RefID>` and `moveto player`. This will move the guard to your location, allowing you to start the quest.
  - This bug can trigger even if you join the Stormcloaks. Try reloading a previous save from before you entered Windhelm.[*verification needed — is this true?*]
  - Follow the blood splatters to Hjerim and pick the lock to the front door. Once you walk inside you will get the quest.
- If you acquire a key to Hjerim before the quest has initiated, then enter and pick up a copy of [Beware the Butcher!](/wiki/Skyrim:Beware_the_Butcher! "Skyrim:Beware the Butcher!"), the quest will initiate and jump directly to stage 70 with no other journal notes indicating what it's about.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- You can also initiate the quest by picking the Master Lock to Hjerim, that starts the quest with the objective "Look for clues".
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- If you begin the [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") add-on's [first main quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_(quest) "Skyrim:Dragonborn (quest)") before starting this quest, then this quest may not start.
- If you go to Windhelm but don't go to the crime scene, after a while it may disappear, Susanna may come back to life and the quest won't start **?**.
  - One fix is to fast travel somewhere. Then wait a while and go to the graveyard.[*verification needed — Is this true? And how long to wait?*]
  -  Alternatively, step outside the gate and use the console command `resetquest ms11`.[*verification needed — see [talk page](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Blood_on_the_Ice)*]
- The guard who is supposed to be near the crime scene never shows up.
  - Enter the console commands `player.setstage ms11 10`, `player.setstage ms11 20`, and `player.setstage ms11 30`. Talk to Jorleif, then go to look at the door to Hjerim. The quest proceeds normally from this point on.
- If the conditions for initiating the quest have not yet been met, entering Hjerim by picking the lock results in several glitched interaction prompts. Picking up the Strange Amulet prevents the quest from ever initiating, leaving Susanna permanently alive and the Strange Amulet as a non-quest item. **?**

### Quest Progression

- If a dragon attacks Windhelm, it may kill the guard you are required to talk to after questioning the witnesses. The body will remain there indefinitely.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
- [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") has an alias during this quest, which can delay [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter") becoming Jarl if this quest is still running when [Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm") is finished.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
- If the quest is started and you wait too long before continuing it, the blood splatters leading to Hjerim can disappear.
- When you are told to question the witnesses, stay away from Hjerim. Approaching the front door will trigger the 'Gain access to Hjerim' [update](#Journal_Entries) and clear the graveyard. This will leave you with no witnesses or map markers for the remainder of the quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- The "Beware the Butcher!" pamphlets are not quest items, and if they are all lost or destroyed before talking to Viola the quest will be unable to proceed.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, fixes this bug.
- Sometimes the game only recognizes the "Beware the Butcher" pamphlets on top of the amulet as 1 of the 5 quest items (3 journals, 1 amulet, 1 pamphlet). Pick them up to progress to the next stage.
- The "Get Assistance from Jorleif" objective will never register as completed.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.1, fixes this bug.
- If you take the first journal to Viola, she will direct you to talk to Jorleif whether or not you have found the amulet. The quest will proceed as though you had found the amulet when talking to Jorleif and Wuunferth, even though you have not.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.9, fixes this bug.
- The quest marker will remain over Viola when you find the journal and show it to her when she wasn't assisting you in finding it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.6, fixes this bug.
- If the quest is started and you do the Stormcloak/Imperial questline first, the quest can become unable to be completed. The guard near the crime scene may be missing after you question the witnesses. One possible solution is to follow the trail of blood to Hjerim in an attempt to skip part of the quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, fixes this bug.
- If Wuunferth is arrested and you never talked to Calixto, thus still having the strange amulet, Wuunferth will always stay guilty and the next murder will never take place, making you unable to finish the entire quest or kill Calixto.
  -  To fix this, type `setstage MS11 105` in the console to trigger the next murder and continue the quest. However, if you talk to Wuunferth after completing the quest, you may begin a second instance of the quest which can never be completed, as he will set you back to the stage where you witness another murder that will not occur.
  - This problem can be addressed by speaking to Wuunferth in his cell after the three day wait period for the second murder. The quest will be resumed after completing the dialogue with him.
- It is possible to pickpocket Calixto's key, and open the chest in his museum/house containing the fairly obvious evidence, but it doesn't change anything in the quest. It won't prevent you accusing Wuunferth when talking to Jorleif.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, addresses this issue. The key will only appear if Calixto is killed.
- When asked to patrol the Stone Quarter at night, Arivanya may not approach, causing Calixto to stand there not doing anything. He may also stand near her without attacking. He will be "busy" if you try to talk to him, and attacking him will incur a bounty, preventing you from finishing the quest.
  - Normally, waiting for an hour will cause Calixto to start moving, allowing the scene to progress as normal. If this does not work, wait until around 8pm the following night for the murder to happen.
  -  Use the console commands `disable` and `enable` on Calixto, then type `prid 0001B144` followed by `moveto player` to teleport Arivanya to your location. She should walk forward and Calixto will try to kill her. You can then kill him.
  -  You may use the `kill` command in the console on Arivanya to progress to the next stage if Calixto does not kill her.
- If you conquered Windhelm before patrolling, the next murder will be in front of Blacksmith Quarters but the next murder will not take place and you will be unable to finish the entire quest or kill Calixto. Calixto will be standing next to the victim and never do the crime. **?**
  -  To fix this, type `setstage MS11 130` and follow the indicator to catch Calixto. Calixto won't run and you only need to follow the indicator. You will find Calixto behind the victim and the victim will be alive. However now you can kill him and go to talk to Wuunferth to complete the quest. When you will go again in that place, even if the victim survived, she won't be there.
- Sometimes the room behind the wardrobe may be completely empty, preventing you from finding the second butcher journal. **?**
  -  You can add the missing item with `player.additem 00066182 1`.
- Calixto sometimes "stalks" Arivanya into the stables during the day hours when the door is unlocked. In the evening, the stable door becomes locked, and Calixto can't get out and make his way to the market to attempt murdering Arivanya. **?**
  - Lockpicking the stables door and interacting with Calixto seems to reset his routine.
- The scene where Calixto's final victim cries for help can only be spoken by one voicetype (FemaleEvenToned).
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, addresses this issue. This has now been changed to a generic shared bystander shout so all of the potential victims can use it regardless of their voicetypes.
- There are several dialogue options that are known to check and see if Jorleif is the one who should be saying them.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.6, addresses this issue. Since Jorleif is exiled and replaced with [Captain Lonely-Gale](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Lonely-Gale "Skyrim:Captain Lonely-Gale") if the [Empire captures Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm") with Unofficial Skyrim Patch 1.3.2 or later, they are now set to use the AuthorityFigure alias instead.

### Wuunferth Arrested Variation

If you speak to Wuunferth directly, instead of Jorleif, then Calixto will attempt to murder Arivanya in the Stone Quarter. If you choose to have Wuunferth arrested, then Arivanya will be found murdered. For the [final showdown](#Catch_the_Killer.21), a random, female NPC will be chosen as the market victim. If the game runs out of potential victims, one of two bugs will trigger:

- After speaking to Wuunferth, the journal will immediately update to stage 130. After chasing Calixto into Hjerim, he cannot be killed. He then will not leave Hjerim and becomes hostile when you enter.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
  -  To complete quest, exit Hjerim and use console commands: `prid 1B11D` and `moveto player`.
- Calixto will stay inside his House of Curiosities and will never attempt his last kill.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
- If you buy Hjerim and arrest Wuunferth, when you get the objective to patrol Windhelm's streets Calixto may appear inside Hjerim, in the room behind the wardrobe, and use any equipment you may have left in it. He will be immediately aggressive and killing him advances the quest normally (go talk to Wuunferth in jail to get next quest entry into journal). **?**
- Upon receiving the objective to "patrol the streets of the Stone Quarter at night" after speaking to Wuunferth, said objective may already appear completed and a quest marker will appear on Hjerim, where Calixto Corrium is hiding. Killing Calixto Corrium there, even during the day, will advance the quest normally.

### Other

- When selling the amulet to Calixto he gives 500 gold; if you then pickpocket it from him and ask about the amulet he gives you the option to sell it again. This can be repeated as many times as you'd like.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.5, fixes this bug.
- While Arivanya is needed to initiate the quest, she is scripted to be the victim found near Candlehearth Hall. This means she can be killed during the quest and a second copy of her will turn up when the quest initiates for the second time.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- When confronting Wuunferth with the evidence, you can always mention that Calixto was wrong about the amulet, even if you haven't spoken to Calixto about it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- You can accuse Wuunferth of necromancy without ever having read any of the available journal pages or taken the amulet from Hjerim.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.9, addresses this issue. You can no longer get him arrested OR confront him directly unless you've done this, which is what the scripting shows was supposed to have been done all along.
- You can accuse Wuunferth without having taken possession of the amulet because the amulet and the butcher flyers both share the same script which was only setting a quest stage.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, addresses this issue. Two tracking variables have been added to make sure that BOTH clues are required to make the accusation, as intended.
- Even before the quest is initiated, speaking to Calixto outside his museum will cause him to close it permanently. Do not attempt to pick the lock, as he will become hostile. Instead, if you want information about the Amulet, find him at Candlehearth Hall between 5pm and 7pm.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.
- Selling Calixto the strange amulet is the only way to turn it into the Necromancer's Amulet.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.1, fixes this bug.
- If you reject Calixto's offer or otherwise fail to remove the strange amulet, the necklace will permanently remain a quest item and be stuck in your inventory indefinitely, though it can be placed into the inventories of Susanna the Wicked or Arivanya after they've been murdered, as long as the bodies are around.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- Although this quest is categorized as a Side Quest in your journal, it does not count towards the "Side Quests Completed" statistic in your General Stats, nor does it count towards the [Sideways](/wiki/Skyrim:Sideways "Skyrim:Sideways") [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.1, fixes this bug.
- Sometimes when you enter Hjerim, it will be impossible to interact with any of the items in the building even with USLEEP or USSEP installed.
  - This bug was caused by USSEP because it deactivated the activators necessary for the quest progression but it seems to be fixed in version 4.2.5b and later.

  - MS11: 0, 1, 105, 200, 205.
  - MS11b: 0, 10.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MS11, MS11b stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MS11, MS11b`.

# Skyrim:Blood's Honor

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Companions.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Companions.png) | **Claim the head of a [Glenmoril Witch](/wiki/Skyrim:Glenmoril_Witch "Skyrim:Glenmoril Witch") for [Kodlak Whitemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Kodlak Whitemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane") |
| Location(s): | [Glenmoril Coven](/wiki/Skyrim:Glenmoril_Coven "Skyrim:Glenmoril Coven"), [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr") |
| Reward: | None |
| ID: | C04 |
| Suggested Level: | 14 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [The Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silver_Hand "Skyrim:The Silver Hand"), two [radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions#Radiant_Quests "Skyrim:Companions") | **Next →** [Purity of Revenge](/wiki/Skyrim:Purity_of_Revenge "Skyrim:Purity of Revenge") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [The Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silver_Hand "Skyrim:The Silver Hand"), two [radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions#Radiant_Quests "Skyrim:Companions") | | → Next | [Purity of Revenge](/wiki/Skyrim:Purity_of_Revenge "Skyrim:Purity of Revenge") | | |

Off with her head!

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Kodlak Whitemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane").
2. Collect a [Glenmoril Witch](/wiki/Skyrim:Glenmoril_Witch "Skyrim:Glenmoril Witch")'s head.
3. (Optional) Wipe out the [Glenmoril Witches](/wiki/Skyrim:Glenmoril_Witch "Skyrim:Glenmoril Witch").
4. Return to [Kodlak](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane").

### The Price of Power

After completing two radiant quests for the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") (one of which must be for [Aela](/wiki/Skyrim:Aela_the_Huntress "Skyrim:Aela the Huntress")), your next major assignment will be available, courtesy of the elderly Harbinger himself, [Kodlak Whitemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane"). He will chastise you for your actions against the [Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand"), and will then tell you the true story about how the Companions contracted [Lycanthropy](/wiki/Skyrim:Lycanthropy "Skyrim:Lycanthropy"). Apparently, one of his predecessors made a pact with the [Glenmoril Witches](/wiki/Skyrim:Glenmoril_Witch "Skyrim:Glenmoril Witch") to gain more power, not knowing the true price of his actions: an afterlife spent in [Hircine](/wiki/Lore:Hircine "Lore:Hircine")'s [Hunting Grounds](/wiki/Lore:Hunting_Grounds "Lore:Hunting Grounds"), not in [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)"). It is this fate which compels Kodlak to seek a cure. He then sends you off by yourself, in search of the Glenmoril Witches.

### The Coven

[Glenmoril Coven](/wiki/Skyrim:Glenmoril_Coven "Skyrim:Glenmoril Coven") is located in the northwest reaches of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"), southeast of [Lost Valley Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Valley_Redoubt "Skyrim:Lost Valley Redoubt"). Upon entering, proceed to the main chamber where you will encounter the first Glenmoril Witch, a powerful variety of [Hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven"). She will attack you on sight, accompanied by a [Frostbite Spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") or [Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"). After the battle, claim her [head](/wiki/Skyrim:Glenmoril_Witch_Head "Skyrim:Glenmoril Witch Head"). The chamber functions as a nexus to four smaller chambers, each with a witch and some valuable loot. The [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") skill book *[The Horror of Castle Xyr](/wiki/Skyrim:Horror_of_Castle_Xyr "Skyrim:Horror of Castle Xyr")* is in a tent in the northwestern chamber and the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") skill book *[A Tragedy in Black](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Tragedy_in_Black "Skyrim:A Tragedy in Black")* is in the northernmost chamber. While it is optional to kill all five witches, killing at least four is recommended if you want to [cure yourself of lycanthropy](/wiki/Skyrim:Lycanthropy#Curing_Lycanthropy "Skyrim:Lycanthropy") later on. Despite the described weight of the heads, no weight penalty is added when you pick them up as quest items.

### Jorrvaskr Attacked!

When you return to [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), things will be different and you will notice several citizens gathered around near the stairs leading to [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr"). Halfway up the stairs, you will find both [Torvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Torvar "Skyrim:Torvar") and Aela the Huntress next to dead Silver Hand members. When you enter the building, [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") will seek you out and ask you where you were in the time of need. In your absence, the Silver Hand attacked Jorrvaskr, managing to kill old Kodlak and take off with all the fragments of [Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Wuuthrad"). You will find Kodlak's dead body near the central fireplace, with [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas") and [Njada Stonearm](/wiki/Skyrim:Njada_Stonearm "Skyrim:Njada Stonearm") kneeling next to him; both unresponsive. Vilkas will claim that his death will be avenged, which will end the quest and immediately start the next one, [Purity of Revenge](/wiki/Skyrim:Purity_of_Revenge "Skyrim:Purity of Revenge").

## Notes

- You won't be able to ask Farkas or Vilkas for work once this quest becomes available. They will both decline, and advise you to stick with Aela instead. Farkas will say *"Aela said you were hers, and I wasn't supposed to interfere. She scares me."* and Vilkas will say *"Aela's laid claim to your services, and I've learned the hard way not to upset her. Best you stick to her for now."* Neither of them will be available for work until you finish the Companions questline. The same thing goes for Aela once this quest is finished.
- If you decide to become a werewolf inside Glenmoril Coven and attack the Glenmoril Witches there, they will say "So the beast returns" during combat.
- If you have a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") prior to completing this quest, he/she will be replaced by Vilkas once you enter Jorrvaskr at the end of this quest. This will cause your previous follower to "reset", meaning they will return to their respective origin, and will appear again as they did when you first met. However, any items that were given to them will still be in their inventory if you return later to regain them as a follower.
- Kodlak's body cannot be interacted with or searched, as the quest script makes it uninteractable.
- Regardless of whether you kill all the Glemoril Witches or not, the [guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Guards "Skyrim:Guards") will praise you upon the completion of Blood's Honor.

## Bugs

- After finishing the two radiant quests for Aela, Blood's Honor may not show up, as Aela won't initiate the quest. This may be caused by a conflicting radiant quest which is already active at Glenmoril Coven. Attempt to complete the radiant quest as early as possible and it should function as normal.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.0, fixes this bug.
- At the beginning of the quest, you can mention to Kodlak that he wanted to see you and start the quest that way. It doesn't make sense if you haven't talked to Aela yet, given that you couldn't have possibly known that Kodlak was wanting to see you. This is due to an incorrect condition check on the dialogue.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.2, addresses this issue. You now MUST talk to Aela first before the dialogue topic to Kodlak that he wanted to see you becomes available.

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.

- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage C04 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest C04`.
