Bloodskal Barrow

**Bloodskal Barrow** is a small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") north of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") containing [reavers](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver "Skyrim:Reaver"). It contains only one zone, *[Bloodskal Barrow](#Bloodskal_Barrow)*.

There are two entrances to the barrow, with the exterior entrance north of Raven Rock and another entrance inside [Raven Rock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine"). Much of the interior of the barrow can initially be accessed from the exterior entrance, but the deepest section of the barrow can only initially be accessed from the mine, as reflected in the walkthrough below. A tiny separate room in the barrow with an upright sarcophagus containing a [stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim "Skyrim:Stalhrim") deposit flanked by two large [urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") can also only be accessed from the mine, as described on the mine's location page.

## Related Quests

- **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader")**: Do a favor by slaying a bandit leader. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Final Descent](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Final_Descent "Skyrim:The Final Descent")**: Find out what happened to the [great-grandfather](/wiki/Skyrim:Gratian_Caerellius "Skyrim:Gratian Caerellius") of [Crescius Caerellius](/wiki/Skyrim:Crescius_Caerellius "Skyrim:Crescius Caerellius").

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Bloodskal Barrow

To explore the entire barrow, it must be initially entered via Raven Rock Mine. The entrance from the mine leads into a short twisting tunnel that ends at a concealed door opened using the pull chain to its left. Beyond the door is a typical Nordic crypt inhabited by reavers, with a stool to the left holding a copy of *[The Holds of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Holds_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:The Holds of Skyrim")*, and four loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") on the ground near the stool. Unless you are [sneaking](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak"), it is likely you will encounter a reaver and a reaver boss at this point. Like other Nordic crypts, rows of small alcoves line the walls to hold the dead, but here most are empty except for the occasional unlootable skeleton. In the south corner of the crypt room is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"). Along the southwest wall are five whole [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") hanging from a rope strung against the wall, with a bunch of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), a bunch of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), and a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braid hanging above. Behind the salmon in the lower burial alcove are two baskets containing six [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") and eleven [ash yams](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Yam "Skyrim:Ash Yam"). To the right of the salmon in another alcove and on the ground are six bottles of bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and four [empty wine bottles](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle"). In the west corner is a table with a built-in [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs").

Northeast of the salmon is a campfire with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") hanging over it. Northeast of the campfire are two chairs and a small round table holding an ash yam and a piece of [boar meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Boar_Meat "Skyrim:Boar Meat"), with an open box containing six more ash yams on the floor next to the table. In the north corner is a sleeping area used by the reaver boss featuring a double bed and a dresser with a copy of *[Deathbrand](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_(book) "Skyrim:Deathbrand (book)")* on top. To the left of the dresser is a boss-level [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). Opposite the foot of the bed are two sets of shelves holding several sets of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), three common books, a copy of *[The Red Book of Riddles](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Red_Book_of_Riddles "Skyrim:The Red Book of Riddles")*, a [deer hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Hide "Skyrim:Deer Hide"), a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), four loose coins, and two sacks. To the left of the two sets of shelves is a shorter set of shelves holding eleven books common on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"), including another copy of *Deathbrand*, and a medium coin purse. Another sack and a fish barrel are along the back of the two sets of shelves, at the base of the rising path northwest of the campfire.

At the top of the path is a fire to the right fueled by a pile of five [burnt corpses](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Burnt_Corpse "Skyrim:Containers") apparently taken from the burial alcoves, with five [dead draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Draugr "Skyrim:Containers") on the floor and in a cart next to the fire. To the left the path turns back to the northwest and then again to the northeast. The stone stairs leading up to the exit are on the left to the northwest, while ahead to the northeast are the corpses of a [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf_(NPC) "Skyrim:High Elf (NPC)") and an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_(dead) "Skyrim:Imperial (dead)"), both of which hold little but the clothes on their backs.

### Exterior

At least four reavers are stationed outside in the two ruined towers. The exit from the barrow leads to a ledge with a stone walkway crossing to the northwest. On the far side of the walkway is a wooden ramp leading down to the left and a doorway immediately ahead leading into the southwest tower. Beyond the doorway, the first room contains three chairs and a table to the west holding a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), and a rare [knife](/wiki/Skyrim:Knife_(weapon) "Skyrim:Knife (weapon)") and two rare [forks](/wiki/Skyrim:Fork_(weapon) "Skyrim:Fork (weapon)") usable as weapons. Along the southwest wall is a set of shelves holding a [chitin helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Chitin_Helmet "Skyrim:Chitin Helmet"), a pair of [chitin boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Chitin_Boots "Skyrim:Chitin Boots"), two [ash yams](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Yam "Skyrim:Ash Yam"), and an [ash creep cluster](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Creep_Cluster "Skyrim:Ash Creep Cluster"), with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") and a wood pile to the left of the set of shelves. Along the southeast wall is a flight of stairs ascending to the next level of the tower, with a fish barrel and a cooking pot on a stand beneath the stairs.

At the top of the stairs is another room, with an alchemy lab in the west corner. To the northeast are three [tanning racks](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"), with a chair and a small round table between two of the racks holding a hooded red [Dunmer outfit](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmer_Outfit "Skyrim:Dunmer Outfit") and another fork weapon. Along the southeast wall is a set of shelves holding two [horker tusks](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Tusk "Skyrim:Horker Tusk"), a [horse hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Hide "Skyrim:Horse Hide"), two bottles of [sujamma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sujamma "Skyrim:Sujamma"), and copies of *[The Poison Song, Book I](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Poison_Song,_Book_I "Skyrim:The Poison Song, Book I")*, *[The Tale of Dro'Zira](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Tale_of_Dro%27Zira "Skyrim:The Tale of Dro'Zira")*, *[The Reclamations](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reclamations "Skyrim:The Reclamations")*, and *[Trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Trap "Skyrim:Trap")*. Along the northwest wall is another flight of stairs leading up, with two ingredient barrels beneath the stairs. These stairs ascend to a bridge crossing to the northeast to the top level of the other tower.

On the far side of the bridge is a flight of stairs leading down to the room on the top level of the northeast tower, with three food barrels beneath the stairs. Along the northeast wall opposite the stairs is a food barrel, a single bed, and an adept-locked chest. Along the southeast wall is a table holding a [scroll of chain lightning](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Chain_Lightning "Skyrim:Scroll of Chain Lightning") and a [scrawled note](/wiki/Skyrim:Scrawled_Note "Skyrim:Scrawled Note"). As there is no other exit from this room, backtrack to the ramp leading down from the initial walkway crossing from the barrow exit.

At the bottom of the ramp is a doorway into a lower level of the southwest tower, with a narrow table opposite the doorway holding two random [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"). To the right to the northeast is a flight of stone stairs descending to the lowest accessible level of the southwest tower. At the bottom of the stairs is a chest to the southwest next to the stairs, a single bed to the southeast, and a doorway to the northwest leading outside. Beyond the doorway is a stone bridge crossing to the northeast to the other tower, with a doorway ahead and a wooden ramp leading up to the right. At the top of the ramp is a room containing a reaver sleeping on a bedroll, two other bedrolls, and a pair of random [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") on a crate. Again, there is no other exit from this room.

Beyond the doorway at the end of the stone bridge is a food barrel and a flight of stone stairs down to the ground level, where a doorway exits the northeast tower. At least two more reavers can be found here. West of the towers near the shore is a [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") plant, while around the towers are several other plants that can be harvested for [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") unique to Solstheim.

## Notes

- From the ground south a little of Bloodskal Barrow, climb up the mountain, on the halfway, north side is a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel") and a boss-level chest, continue to climb up and see an [emerald geode](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald "Skyrim:Emerald") and a [gold ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein"), there is another emerald geode a short distance east of the first geode.
  - With the [Ghosts of the Tribunal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal") Creation, [Ashfall's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashfall%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Ashfall's Tear") can be found south of the second emerald geode.
- South of the barrow is a [shrine of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Shrine of Kynareth") and a respawning albino spider egg.
- Bloodskal Barrow also [appears](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Bloodskal_Barrow "Bloodmoon:Bloodskal Barrow") in *[Bloodmoon](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon "Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon")*.

# Skyrim:Bloodthirst (quest)

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Zavieriot](/w/index.php?title=User:Zavieriot&action=edit&redlink=1 "User:Zavieriot (page does not exist)"), *not checked*  **Reward**: *not written* |

| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [A Soul Divided](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Soul_Divided "Skyrim:A Soul Divided") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [A Soul Divided](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Soul_Divided "Skyrim:A Soul Divided") | | |

Find Bloodthirst in Broken Fang Cave

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read [Verrick's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Verrick%27s_Note "Skyrim:Verrick's Note"). The note is located in the green room inside the Guardian Vault, on a table to the left of the torture devices.
2. Go to [Faldar's Tooth](/wiki/Skyrim:Faldar%27s_Tooth "Skyrim:Faldar's Tooth"), and find a note on one of the bodies after the fight there.
3. Read [Cage Bandit's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Cage_Bandit%27s_Note "Skyrim:Cage Bandit's Note").
4. Go to [Broken Fang Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Fang_Cave "Skyrim:Broken Fang Cave"), defeat the denizens there and find the sword [Bloodthirst](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodthirst "Skyrim:Bloodthirst") among the loot there.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Halfway through [The Guardian Vault](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Guardian_Vault "Skyrim:The Guardian Vault") during the [Dawnfang/Duskfang Quest](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Soul_Divided "Skyrim:A Soul Divided"), in the green room on a table to the left of the torture devices, there is a note with a dagger through it. On reading [Verrick's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Verrick%27s_Note "Skyrim:Verrick's Note"), a miscellaneous side quest is added, 'Investigate Faldar's Tooth.' Leave the Ratway and travel there.

Arriving at [Faldar's Tooth](/wiki/Skyrim:Faldar%27s_Tooth "Skyrim:Faldar's Tooth"), there is a bandit labeled 'Bouncer' and 2 pit wolves outside. As you enter, there is another bandit labeled 'Bouncer' immediately inside. Straight ahead through the narrow passageway, turn right into the main room. You come out on a wooden deck, with barrels and sacks to your left, and stairs down to your right. The room has a cage in the middle, with 2 fighting wolves inside. There are 2 gamblers and a barkeep who will all become hostile to you as you enter. As the fighting starts, a leveled bandit labeled 'the butcher' will come out from the back room. This enemy has strong leveled gear, so be careful. Along the wall, there is a gambler cage, which has inside gold, many coin purses, skooma, a healing potion, a leveled chest, and the [Cage Bandit's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Cage_Bandit%27s_Note "Skyrim:Cage Bandit's Note"), giving you a new miscellaneous objective to 'Retrieve [Bloodthirst](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodthirst "Skyrim:Bloodthirst") from [Broken Fang Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Fang_Cave "Skyrim:Broken Fang Cave")'.

As you get to [Broken Fang Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Fang_Cave "Skyrim:Broken Fang Cave"), you will enter into a small corridor, with a staircase leading down into a large room. There are many raised platforms with empty crypts along the walls, and a cafe and chains hanging from the ceiling. As you walk down, there is a [Vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") sitting in the room who will attack. If you have [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") installed, this may be a [Volkihar Vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan"). There are 3 [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") to the left of the room who will join the attack. Once you deal with the enemies, you can continue forward through the room. There is an adept-locked chest in the southeast corner.

From here, the western raised platform has a doorway leading to a narrow walkway. You come out into a nicer looking small room with a high leveled Vampire. The room has an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") to the right, a [dead bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(dead) "Skyrim:Bandit (dead)") and a cage in front of you, a large table with platters along the wall to your left, and a small table with 3 chairs in the middle. As you walk in you'll see 2 beds to the side, an [enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") in an alcove next to the cage, and a double bed with a bookshelf to the right of it and a boss chest on its left. This chest contains [Bloodthirst](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodthirst "Skyrim:Bloodthirst") and some leveled loot. As you collect Bloodthirst the objective will complete, and you're free to leave back the way you came in.

## Bugs

-  Reading Verrick's note may not start the quest. **?**

| 40 |  |  |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE013_BloodthirstQuest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE013_BloodthirstQuest`.

# Skyrim:Bloody Nose

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Defeat [Hofgrir Horse-Crusher](/wiki/Skyrim:Hofgrir_Horse-Crusher "Skyrim:Hofgrir Horse-Crusher") in a [brawl](/wiki/Skyrim:Brawl "Skyrim:Brawl").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Hofgrir Horse-Crusher](/wiki/Skyrim:Hofgrir_Horse-Crusher "Skyrim:Hofgrir Horse-Crusher") |
| Location(s): | [Riften Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Stables "Skyrim:Riften Stables") |
| Reward: | 100 gold |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Hofgrir Horse-Crusher](/wiki/Skyrim:Hofgrir_Horse-Crusher "Skyrim:Hofgrir Horse-Crusher")) |
| ID: | FreeformRiften19 |
| Required Items: | 100 gold |
| Suggested Items: | [Gloves of the Pugilist](/wiki/Skyrim:Gloves_of_the_Pugilist "Skyrim:Gloves of the Pugilist") or [Heavy Gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Heavy Gauntlets") if you have the [Fists of Steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Fists_of_Steel "Skyrim:Fists of Steel") perk |

Hofgrir defeated in an unarmed brawl

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Defeat [Hofgrir Horse-Crusher](/wiki/Skyrim:Hofgrir_Horse-Crusher "Skyrim:Hofgrir Horse-Crusher") in an unarmed [brawl](/wiki/Skyrim:Brawl "Skyrim:Brawl").

### Meeting Hofgrir

Meet [Hofgrir Horse-Crusher](/wiki/Skyrim:Hofgrir_Horse-Crusher "Skyrim:Hofgrir Horse-Crusher") at the [Riften Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Stables "Skyrim:Riften Stables"), just to the north of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). Talk to him about the dangers of living outside the walls, which will lead to him boasting about being the strongest brawler in Skyrim. Make a 100 gold bet with him that you can beat him. This [brawl](/wiki/Skyrim:Brawl "Skyrim:Brawl") is like any other, and the usual rules apply: no weapons, and no offensive magic. Beware, as he is much tougher than most other brawlers.

### Claiming your reward

After winning the brawl, talk to Hofgrir and he will give you your 100 gold back, as well as another 100 gold for winning the bet.

## Notes

- Hofgrir brawls like other NPCs, though the one difference is that he does a lot more damage per hit than other characters. This isn't quite as notable on the lesser difficulties (Novice, Apprentice, Adept), but it is very notable on the higher ones (Expert, Master and especially Legendary). If you are a lower level/health or are wearing clothes instead of armor when doing this quest on those higher difficulties, it would be viable to heal during the encounter or you'll be swiftly beaten.

## Bugs

- If you don't have 200 gold when you attempt the brawl the quest may be uncompletable.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.
  -  This can be fixed using `setstage FreeformRiften19 200` followed by `resetquest FreeformRiften19`.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformRiften19 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformRiften19`.

# Skyrim:Blue God

## Overview

The "Blue God"

The Blue God is an [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") masquerading as a deity of the same name, specifically the [Goblin](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblin "Skyrim:Goblin") interpretation of [Malacath](/wiki/Lore:Malacath "Lore:Malacath"). He is hostile and you will need to kill him during the related quest.

He carries the *[Blue God's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_God%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Blue God's Journal")* and wields a [Goblin Totem Staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblin_Totem_Staff "Skyrim:Goblin Totem Staff") in battle.

His journal reveals that he was originally from the [Orc stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") [Largashbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur "Skyrim:Largashbur"), where he was considered a black sheep. He unintentionally became the leader of a goblin tribe after visiting Gromm's Pass with full blue body paint, which made the goblins mistake him for the Blue God. His secret was almost discovered when the goblin [Gogh](/wiki/Skyrim:Gogh "Skyrim:Gogh") caught him applying the blue dye to keep up the act. The imposter sentenced Gogh to death in the goblin's fighting pit. With enough goblin troops gathered, he planned to assault Largashbur for his ill treatment from its inhabitants.

## Related Quests

- **[Blue in the Face](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_in_the_Face "Skyrim:Blue in the Face")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblins "Skyrim:Goblins"): Investigate rumors of the Blue God's return.

## Notes

- He is referred as "blorc" in the files.

# Skyrim:Blue in the Face

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Legoless](/wiki/User:Legoless "User:Legoless"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Legoless](/wiki/User:Legoless "User:Legoless"), *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Automatically added after purchasing the [Goblins](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblins "Skyrim:Goblins") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") |
| Location(s): | [The Bee and Barb](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bee_and_Barb "Skyrim:The Bee and Barb"), [Gromm's Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Gromm%27s_Pass "Skyrim:Gromm's Pass") |
| Reward: | [Goblin Totem Staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblin_Totem_Staff "Skyrim:Goblin Totem Staff"), a [Goblin](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblin "Skyrim:Goblin") [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") named [Gogh](/wiki/Skyrim:Gogh "Skyrim:Gogh") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE040\_Quest |
| Added by: | [Goblins](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblins "Skyrim:Goblins") |

The "Blue God"

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read *[Letter to Clexius](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_to_Clexius "Skyrim:Letter to Clexius")* at [the Bee and Barb](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bee_and_Barb "Skyrim:The Bee and Barb").
2. Enter [Gromm's Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Gromm%27s_Pass "Skyrim:Gromm's Pass") and kill the [Blue God](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_God "Skyrim:Blue God").
3. Read his [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_God%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Blue God's Journal") and free [Gogh](/wiki/Skyrim:Gogh "Skyrim:Gogh") from the fighting pit.

### Creatures from the South

Upon installing the [Goblins](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblins "Skyrim:Goblins") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"), you can go to [the Bee and Barb](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bee_and_Barb "Skyrim:The Bee and Barb") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), where in a room upstairs you will find a *[Letter to Clexius](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_to_Clexius "Skyrim:Letter to Clexius")*. This piece of personal correspondence describes a tribe of Cyrodilic [Goblins](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblin "Skyrim:Goblin") who have invaded a cave known as [Gromm's Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Gromm%27s_Pass "Skyrim:Gromm's Pass"). By all accounts, they seem to be led by the "Blue God", an aspect of [Malacath](/wiki/Skyrim:Malacath "Skyrim:Malacath") worshipped by Goblins. You'll have to head there to investigate.

### Cave Crawling

A Goblin heretic fighting back

Gromm's Pass is a new cave added by this Creation. The entrance can be found in the valley directly south of [Forelhost](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost "Skyrim:Forelhost"). It is notable for being filled with hostile Goblins as well as a unique type of mushroom called [Steel-Blue Entoloma‎‎](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel-Blue_Entoloma "Skyrim:Steel-Blue Entoloma"). This plant is added by the Creation and cannot be found elsewhere, although it can be grown in [Fertile Soil](/wiki/Skyrim:Fertile_Soil "Skyrim:Fertile Soil") so it would be advisable to harvest a few samples while you're there. While exploring the cave, you will soon come across the body of [Avanessa Calladius](/wiki/Skyrim:Avanessa_Calladius "Skyrim:Avanessa Calladius"), the mage whose letter you found. On her corpse you will find a copy of *[The Posting of the Hunt](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Posting_of_the_Hunt "Skyrim:The Posting of the Hunt")*, a book which describes the legendary [Spear of Bitter Mercy](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_of_Bitter_Mercy "Skyrim:Spear of Bitter Mercy"). The relevance of this will soon become apparent, once you step foot inside the cave's central chamber where a Goblin wielding this legendary Spear is currently battling for his life inside an enclosed fighting pit.

You likely won't have time to watch the fight, as the chamber also serves as a throne room for the [Blue God](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_God "Skyrim:Blue God"). Kill him and his Goblin minions in order to loot the powerful [Goblin Totem Staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblin_Totem_Staff "Skyrim:Goblin Totem Staff") from his corpse. You will also have to read his [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_God%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Blue God's Journal"), which reveals that this supposed manifestation of the Blue God was actually just a hapless tribal [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") who covered himself in Steel-Blue Entoloma‎‎ paste to trick the invading Goblins into following him. Unfortunately, the underground passage to Cyrodiil has since collapsed.

### A Grateful Goblin

Once you've had a chance to read the journal, you will be directed to free the surviving Goblin in the fighting pit, where he was thrown after figuring out the Orc's trickery. His name is [Gogh](/wiki/Skyrim:Gogh "Skyrim:Gogh"), and he will be more than happy to join you as a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") for saving him from the pit. He acts similarly to the [Riekling Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling_Warrior "Skyrim:Riekling Warrior") follower from [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") and can be spoken to at length despite his rather lacking vocabulary. You have the option to change his outfit visually, but you cannot take the Spear of Bitter Mercy. It is left unclear as to why exactly a Goblin is in possession of a powerful Daedric artifact, but he will use it to great effect as a follower, using it to perform attacks and summon [storm atronachs](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Atronach "Skyrim:Storm Atronach").

Gogh cannot be commanded to stay at any of your [houses](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses"). If he leaves your service, he will return to the throne area in Gromm's Pass.

## Bugs

- The *Letter to Clexius* frequently falls through the top of the shelf below, making it difficult to find. The letter will also be permanently inaccessible when it falls through the shelf, no shouts or use of Telekinesis will get it out.
  - You can circumvent this step by going straight to Gromm's Pass, which is just south of Forelhost.

## Quest Stages

| Blue in the Face (ccBGSSSE040\_Quest) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 8 |  | I traveled to Gromm's Pass and proceeded to investigate the cave's interior. Inside I found an arena pit and several goblins, as well as an Orc who served as their shaman. I killed the Orc and read the journal on his person. *Objective :* Speak to the Goblin |
| 10 |  | There are often rumors in Riften of strange creatures coming across the border from Cyrodiil. I should head to the inn and see what information I can find. *Objective :* Look for information at the Bee and Barb |
| 20 |  | I found a note at the Bee and Barb that implied goblins were spotted in Skyrim near the border to Cyrodiil. The writer of the note claimed she was on her way to Gromm's Pass to investigate. *Objective :* Head to Gromm's Pass |
| 30 |  | I traveled to Gromm's Pass and proceeded to investigate the cave's interior. *Objective :* Investigate the cave |
| 80 |  | I traveled to Gromm's Pass and proceeded to investigate the cave's interior. Inside I found an arena pit and several goblins, as well as an Orc who served as their shaman. *Objective :* Kill the Blue God |
| 100 |  | I traveled to Gromm's Pass and proceeded to investigate the cave's interior. Inside I found an arena pit and several goblins, as well as an Orc who served as their shaman. I killed the Orc while a lone goblin fought for his life in the pit. *Objective :* Read the Blue God's journal  *Objective :* Free the Goblin from the pit |
| 200 | ☑ | I traveled to Gromm's Pass and proceeded to investigate the cave's interior. Inside I found an arena pit and several goblins, as well as an Orc who served as their shaman. I killed the Orc and read the journal on his person, then recruited the goblin in the pit. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 1, 5, 6, 7, 9, 40, 70, 75.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE040_Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE040_Quest`.

# Skyrim:Blue Palace

## Overview

> *Been up to the Blue Palace? It's a sight to see. Even if it is filled with fops.* ―[Solitude Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Guard "Skyrim:Solitude Guard")

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-SolitudePalace.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-SolitudePalace.png) | Castle: Blue Palace ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Blue+Palace)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Blue_Palace "Lore:Blue Palace")) | | |

| Special Features | |

The Blue Palace

The **Blue Palace** is the current seat of power for [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar"), and [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"); and home to the [High King of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:High_King_Torygg "Skyrim:High King Torygg"). The palace is split into two zones, the *[Blue Palace](#Blue_Palace)*, and the *[Pelagius Wing](#Pelagius_Wing)*. The Blue Palace is divided into ten rooms, and the Pelagius Wing has three rooms.

The Blue Palace holds a prominent position over Haafingar.

The palace sits on the tip of the arch that Solitude is built on, and commands attention once [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour") has been passed. It is the last port of call in Solitude, as the walls of the palace are a part of the walls of Solitude, which themselves are built on the edge of the arch.

To explore the full extent of the palace, and to retrieve one of the hidden treasures, you must complete [The Mind of Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mind_of_Madness "Skyrim:The Mind of Madness").

### Bards College

- **[Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames")**: Unveil the truth about a deceitful [King](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_One-Eye "Skyrim:Olaf One-Eye") and become a member of the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College").

### Daedric Quests

- **[The Mind of Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mind_of_Madness "Skyrim:The Mind of Madness")**: Gain access to and solve the mystery of the [Pelagius Wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_Wing "Skyrim:Pelagius Wing").

### Thieves Guild

- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.
- **[Scoundrel's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Scoundrel%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Scoundrel's Folly")**: Squeeze a [reluctant informer](/wiki/Skyrim:Gulum-Ei "Skyrim:Gulum-Ei") for information.

### Other

- **[Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery_(Sorex) "Skyrim:Delivery (Sorex)")**: Deliver a bottle of Rum to [Falk Firebeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Falk_Firebeard "Skyrim:Falk Firebeard").
- **[Elisif's Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif%27s_Tribute "Skyrim:Elisif's Tribute")**: Take Torygg's war horn to the Shrine of Talos.
- **[Fit for a Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Fit_for_a_Jarl "Skyrim:Fit for a Jarl")**: Model some clothes for [Elisif the Fair](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair").
- **[Kill the Vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Vampire "Skyrim:Kill the Vampire")**: Do menial work for [Sybille Stentor](/wiki/Skyrim:Sybille_Stentor "Skyrim:Sybille Stentor") by assaulting [a vampire lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinemoon_Cave "Skyrim:Pinemoon Cave").
- **[The Man Who Cried Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Man_Who_Cried_Wolf "Skyrim:The Man Who Cried Wolf")**: Investigate reports of strange happenings in [Wolfskull Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave").
  - **[The Wolf Queen Awakened](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen_Awakened "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen Awakened")**: Potema must be stopped.
- **[Thane of Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Haafingar "Skyrim:Thane of Haafingar")**: Gain the title of [Thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") of [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Incomplete Quests

- **[Boethiah's Bidding](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Bidding "Skyrim:Boethiah's Bidding")**: Slay the Jarl of Solitude. ([unfinished](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfinished_Quests "Skyrim:Unfinished Quests"))

### Courtyard

The Palace's entrance is guarded day and night by a [Solitude Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Guard "Skyrim:Solitude Guard"). He stands watching the courtyard, and his gaze cannot be evaded when entering it. It is divided into quarters by cobbled paths, and there are covered paths to both sides of the courtyard. There are six thistle branches here, one in each of the left-hand quarters, and two in each of the right-hand quarters. There is a single door here, past the guard and to the left, which leads to the Palace interior.

#### Waiting Room

Melaran talks with the guard while waiting for his employer

Everything in the palace is originally marked as owned and taking it is considered stealing. The door opens to a waiting room. During the day [Melaran](/wiki/Skyrim:Melaran "Skyrim:Melaran"), a [mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Mage "Skyrim:Mage") who works for [Erikur](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur "Skyrim:Erikur"), can be found here, waiting patiently for his employer to finish his day's work at court. There are two guards stationed inside the entrance, one in the waiting room, and another beyond the arch and in the next room, between two sweeping flights of stairs that lead up to where [Elisif](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif "Skyrim:Elisif") holds court daily. There are two chairs, a bench, a table, and a small cupboard to the left, and a small cupboard, a bench, and two tables to the right. There are some standard fine crockery items on the tables, and a copy of the book, *[The Real Barenziah, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Real_Barenziah,_v3 "Skyrim:The Real Barenziah, v3")*. On the two low tables there is an assortment of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") items, including [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and cheese, and [apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"). On the higher table there are a few [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"); namely a [chaurus egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs"), a sample of [hagraven feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Feathers "Skyrim:Hagraven Feathers"), two [hagraven claws](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Claw "Skyrim:Hagraven Claw") and a stone bowl containing some more; a sprig of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulb, a [purple](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") and a [blue mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") and a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), with a second bunch of lavender in a tall vase behind. There are also three [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") growing from the walls around the room.

#### Hallways

The hallway below the court, with the small garden

Beyond this there is a hallway, with the second guards and twin staircases leading up to the Jarl's court. To the right is the door to the [Pelagius wing](#Pelagius_Wing). To the left there is the [kitchen](#Kitchen), which includes the kitchen and a door through to the [staff quarters](#Staff_Quarters). Alongside the kitchen is a hallway, which leads to the [guest quarters](#Guest_Quarters) on the left, and a flight of stairs, which lead to the [basement](#Basement) which contains additional guest quarters, and more bedrooms upstairs. Up the stairs are Sybille's, Bolgeir's and Elisif's bedrooms, along the (now) right-hand side, in that order, with a guest bedroom between Sybille's and Falk's rooms. The hallway opens to the Jarl's court on the left.

There is a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing leveled items beside the door to the [Pelagius wing](#Pelagius_Wing), three [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") plants in planters, and behind the guard between the staircases, a small garden, containing a snowberry bush, a lavender plant, and two [thistles](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle "Skyrim:Thistle"). There is a cupboard, a bench and three tables along the lower hallway. On the right-hand table after the bench, a [case of Firebrand Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Firebrand_Wine_Case "Skyrim:Firebrand Wine Case") will appear during the quest [Scoundrel's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Scoundrel%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Scoundrel's Folly").

There are four benches along the main part of upper hallway and two offshoots from this hallway, leading to Sybille and Elisif's bedrooms respectively. The offshoot to Sybille's room contains a bench, a table, and two sets of shelves, one of which is full of books. The offshoot to Elisif's room contains a cupboard containing clutter, a small wardrobe containing a selection of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots "Skyrim:Fine Boots"), and a table.

#### Jarl's Court

The court in full session

The Jarl's court, the focus of the palace's architecture, is in the center of the second floor. High up to the left are two windows, they are designed to filter light from outside in such a way that it engulfs the throne. The throne itself is off-centered to the left of the far wall. It is on a double-raised platform designed so that while the [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") is sitting, they are still at the same head-height as the subjects in attendance. A [Staff of Magelight](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Magelight "Skyrim:Staff of Magelight") can be found to the right of the Jarl's throne. There are two tables with a few items of fine crockery and candlesticks by the northeast wall, and to the southeast, there is a table separating a sitting area from the court. There are three chairs, a bench, a table, and a cupboard in this part. To the west is a short hallway, with a cupboard and a bench. The cupboards mostly contain clutter.

As you get close to the court for the first time, you will hear the court in session; [Varnius Junius](/wiki/Skyrim:Varnius_Junius "Skyrim:Varnius Junius") is petitioning for troops to be sent to investigate strange occurrences near [Wolfskull Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave"). [Jarl Elisif the Fair](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl_Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Jarl Elisif the Fair") occupies the throne, straight ahead and to the left. [Sybille Stentor](/wiki/Skyrim:Sybille_Stentor "Skyrim:Sybille Stentor") and [Falk Firebeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Falk_Firebeard "Skyrim:Falk Firebeard") are in attendance to Elisif's left all day. [Bolgeir Bearclaw](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolgeir_Bearclaw "Skyrim:Bolgeir Bearclaw") splits his day between standing to Elisif's right, and eating meals on a bench in the hallway behind him. [Erikur](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur "Skyrim:Erikur") and [Bryling](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling "Skyrim:Bryling") spend their time either standing beside Falk, or sitting on the chairs behind him.

| Varnius' Petition | |
| --- | --- |
| **Varnius Junius**: | *"I swear to you, unnatural magics are coming from that cave! There are strange noises and lights! We need someone to investigate!"* |
| **Elisif the Fair**: | *"Then we will immediately send out a legion to scour the cave and secure the town. Haafingar's people will always be safe under my rule."* |
| **Sybille Stentor**: | *"Your eminence, my scrying has suggested nothing in the area. Dragon Bridge is under imperial control. This is likely superstitious nonsense."* |
| **Falk Firebeard**: | *"Perhaps a more... tempered reaction... might be called for?"* |
| **Elisif the Fair**: | *"Oh. Yes, of course you are right. Falk, tell Captain Aldis I said to assign a few extra soldiers to Dragon Bridge."* |
| **Varnius Junius**: | *"Thank you, Jarl Elisif. But about the cave..."* |
| **Falk Firebeard**: | *"I will have someone take care of the cave as well Varnius, you can rest easy. You're dismissed."* |

#### Sybille Stentor's Room

Lots of potions, pity they're all owned...

Sybille's bedroom is the first room along the hallway from the court. It contains a large four-poster bed, that is marked as owned, two end tables, a long unlocked chest containing random items, an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"), a small and a tall wardrobe containing a selection of fine clothes and boots, a narrow table with two wall shelves over it, a low table and chair, a total of five sets of shelves and four open crates. There are many [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") and miscellaneous items found around the room as per the list below;

Outside Sybille's bedroom there is a bookcase holding a further eight common books, a small unit holding the usual assortment of fine crockery and at the end of the corridor is a low table with a copy of *[Lost Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends")* on top.

| Ingredients | | Potions | | Other |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| - 1 Blue Mountain Flower - 1 [Bone Meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal") - 1 Chaurus Eggs - 1 [Deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") - 2 [Void Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts") - 7 Lavender - 1 [Juniper Berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") | - 1 [Tundra Cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") - 1 Hagraven Feathers - 2 Hagraven Claws - 1 [Potion of Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health") - 1 [Potion of Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Magicka") - 3 [Potions of Minor Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") - 1 [Potion of Minor Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") - 1 [Potion of Plentiful Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Magicka") | - 2 [Potions of Strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength") - 1 [Weak Aversion to Shock](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Aversion_to_Shock "Skyrim:Weak Aversion to Shock") - 1 [Weak Paralysis Poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Paralysis_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Paralysis Poison") - 1 [Weak Poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Poison") - 1 [Weak Stamina Poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Stamina_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Stamina Poison") | - 2 [Black-Briar Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead") - 10 Common [Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books") - 1 [Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") - 3 Empty [Lesser Soul Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem") - 2 Empty [Petty Soul Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem") - 6 [Spiced Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiced_Wine "Skyrim:Spiced Wine") - 4 [Soul Gem Fragments](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gem_Fragment "Skyrim:Soul Gem Fragment") |

#### Falk Firebeard's Room

Falk's room

Falk's room is the second room along the hallway from the court, and it is extended right out to the corridor, unlike the others. It is fairly spartan compared to the other members of the court. The room contains an owned single bed with an open crate at the foot of the bed containing a random [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). There are a total of four sets of shelves holding twenty-one common books, a copy of *[Charwich-Koniinge Letters, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:Charwich-Koniinge_Letters,_v1 "Skyrim:Charwich-Koniinge Letters, v1")* and a [potion of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"). There are also a low table and chair, with bread and cheese on the table, a wooden bench, a small wardrobe holding fine clothes, and an expert-locked display case containing a leveled dagger and leveled [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"). Two wall shelves above the bed hold a [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword") and a [giants club](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Club "Skyrim:Giant Club"), that you cannot interact with.

#### Bolgeir Bearclaw's Room

Bolgeir Bearclaw's room

Bolgeir's room is the third room along the hallway from the court. In comparison to the other bedrooms, it is both compact and full. There is one wardrobe containing the usual assortment of fine clothes and with a common book on top, two wall shelves, Two tables, a desk, a chair, and an owned single bed. Despite having his own room and bed, Bolgeir prefers to sleep downstairs in the [guest quarters](#Guest_Quarters), because the bed there is closer to him at all times (of the ones that he is allowed to sleep in). On the table to the right of the door is a bowl with three pieces of bread, and a [sliced eider cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese") on a plate. On the desk are three potions; a potion of strength, a [draught of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Health "Skyrim:Draught of Health"), and a [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), a bunch of tundra cotton, and a copy of *[Wabbajack](/wiki/Skyrim:Wabbajack_(book) "Skyrim:Wabbajack (book)")* as one of three common books. There is a bunch of tundra cotton and [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum") on the wall shelf above. The other wall shelf has two rolls of paper on it and is above the table to the right of the door. There is a set of shelves beside the chair. On these you will find an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet") and [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield"), a common book, a copy of *[Short History of Morrowind](/wiki/Skyrim:Short_History_of_Morrowind "Skyrim:Short History of Morrowind")*, a [candlestick](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlestick "Skyrim:Candlestick") and another bunch of tundra cotton. There is a final bunch of tundra cotton on the table by the window and a set of shelves to the right holds eight more books and a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute").

#### Elisif the Fair's Room

Elisif's room, with an unusual gem by the bed

The corridor leading to Elisif's room has a cupboard containing clutter, a small wardrobe containing fine clothes and an empty table along it. It is the last room along the hallway from the court. The room is rather spacious, and focused nominally on the owned four posted double bed. There are five small and two tall wardrobes around the room, all of which contain a selection of fine clothes and boots, an end table containing clutter, a long chest containing random items, five tables, and two chairs. There are only two things of real interest in the room, an [unusual gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") beside the bed, and a copy of the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Biography of the Wolf Queen](/wiki/Skyrim:Biography_of_the_Wolf_Queen "Skyrim:Biography of the Wolf Queen")*, on one of the small wardrobes, in a sectioned off part of the room opposite the bed. Two of the tables beside each other have a selection of bread and cheese, two [baked potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll") and red and [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") on them. A third table has a bowl containing a purple and a blue mountain flower. The largest table is the one she seems to sit at, it has a drum, a bunch of tundra cotton, a potion of health, a candlestick and a quill and ink pot on top, and an open crate containing three rolls of paper, a potion of minor stamina and a bunch of lavender underneath. Beside this table is a set of shelves holding nine common books and a flute. beside the small wardrobe beside the bed is a basket with a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") hidden inside. There is also a small coin purse on top of the wardrobe by the door, two wash basins around the room and a large vase holding a bunch of tundra cotton.

#### Kitchen

Odar watches as Erikur and Bryling have a meal

The kitchen is [Odar](/wiki/Skyrim:Odar "Skyrim:Odar")'s realm. He runs the kitchen with the general help of the two servant girls, [Erdi](/wiki/Skyrim:Erdi "Skyrim:Erdi") and [Una](/wiki/Skyrim:Una "Skyrim:Una"). Unsurprisingly there is a vast amount of food around the room, but no barrels or sacks of the same found in the kitchen. There are three dining tables with four baked potatoes, a sweet roll, six [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), several pieces of cheese and two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") on top. A table used for food preparation has three fillets of [salmon meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Meat "Skyrim:Salmon Meat"), two [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), a [carrot](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"), a [leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), three [tomatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato"), two bulbs of garlic and a sheaf of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") on top and there is a narrow table with a bowl of bread, a plate of cheese and an iron dagger against the southwest wall. There is a bottle of [spiced wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiced_Wine "Skyrim:Spiced Wine") on the small unit, with another bottle in an open crate that both become marked as unowned once you have completed [Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames"), even if nothing else in the kitchen may be taken.

A total of eight wall shelves around the room holding; two haunches of [horse meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Meat "Skyrim:Horse Meat"), a rack of [dog meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog_Meat "Skyrim:Dog Meat"), a haunch of raw [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison"), a bunch of lavender, a baked potato, a potato, many more pieces of bread and cheese as well as many items of clutter. There are four bunches of dried [elves ears](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braid, a bunch of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), and two whole [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") hanging from racks around the room and two sets of shelves in the northern corner holding a [leg of goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat "Skyrim:Leg of Goat"), a rack of dog meat, a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish") steak, a fillet of salmon meat, a [slaughterfish egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg"), a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"), a salmon steak, a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a potato, five bulbs of garlic and plenty of bread and cheese on the shelves. There is an oven shelf in the northeast wall with another baked potato and portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks") next to an empty metal pot. To the right of this is an unusable woodcutters block with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") on top. In the western corner is a door which leads to the [staff quarters](#Staff_Quarters).

#### Staff Quarters

The staff quarters are used by Una, Erdi, and Odar for sleeping, and are also partially used as a storeroom. There are a few baskets with some brooms along the corridor leading to the main chamber. Opposite the entrance is a small storage area with two barrels, two mead barrels, and a set of shelves with eighteen [empty wine bottles](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle"). The main chamber has four beds, one in each corner, with two wardrobes between each them back-to-back. There is a table with a bench, and the room is well lit by numerous candles. There is hardly anything of value here, except for one thing; a potion of regeneration on the shelves above the table. The beds here become available for sleeping after completing [The Man Who Cried Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Man_Who_Cried_Wolf "Skyrim:The Man Who Cried Wolf").

#### Guest Quarters

The room is located along the hallway from the kitchen. It contains two double-beds, four wardrobes containing a selection of fine clothes and boots, three tables, and three chairs. The room is bare besides the furniture, containing only a bowl, a pot, and a bunch of tundra cotton, all on the table in the far right-hand corner of the room.

#### Basement

The basement

The basement is at the bottom of the stairs, which themselves are at the end of both the upper and lower hallways. The basement is actually designed as more guest quarters, containing three beds, a table surrounded by four chairs, and six benches around the edges of the room. The table holds two pieces of bread, sliced eider cheese, and some fine crockery.

If the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") gain any [holds](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") during the [civil war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"), the displaced jarls will relocate to the basement of the Blue Palace.

### Pelagius Wing

The Pelagius Wing needs a cleaning

The Pelagius Wing, named for [Pelagius the Mad](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_the_Mad "Skyrim:Pelagius the Mad"), is locked. You will need the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_Wing_Key "Skyrim:Pelagius Wing Key") to open the door, which is only available from either Erdi or Una during the quest [The Mind of Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mind_of_Madness "Skyrim:The Mind of Madness"). Despite assertions from Falk that the wing has been *"sealed for hundreds of years"*, the servants reveal that they enter once a year to get rid of any spiders.

The wing is in a decrepit state, with chairs overturned, fine crockery on the floor, and cobwebs everywhere. It certainly lives up to Erdi's claim that *"...it's scary in there!"'*, and the possibility of the ghost that Una claims is there does not seem far-fetched. There are three tables with their chairs placed on top of them in the first room. There are thirteen bottles of alto wine, seven bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and seven bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") in the first two rooms before the hidden portal upstairs, scattered on the crates, floor, tables, barrels, and the oven shelf opposite the entrance. The doorway to the right is boarded up, and the open doorway on the other side leads upstairs. Under the stairs and in the first room are several barrels of food, while beside the stairs is a set of shelves with a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots") on the bottom shelf. Growing from the ceiling at the top of the stairwell is a hanging moss.

The room upstairs is laid out as a bar. There are four bar stools placed on the counter, and five tables with their chairs placed on them. There is a hidden portal to [The Mind of a Madman](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mind_of_a_Madman "Skyrim:The Mind of a Madman") in the hallway, which cannot be avoided if you wish to access the rest of the wing.

It looks like someone has been here recently

Once you return from The Mind of a Madman, you can follow the hallway (which has three hanging moss growing from the walls) to another stairwell with another hanging moss growing down the wall; the stairwell leads down past the boarded-up doorway to a basement. The basement shows signs of being lived in, with a bedroll in the far corner, a lit lantern and a copy of *[Thief of Virtue](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_of_Virtue "Skyrim:Thief of Virtue")* beside it, and an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword") on the bottom lip of the wall near the bedroll. In the middle of the room are two crates supporting an unusable chain mechanism, and on the crate to the left is a copy of the [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") skill book *[Surfeit of Thieves](/wiki/Skyrim:Surfeit_of_Thieves "Skyrim:Surfeit of Thieves")*. Between the bedroll and the skill book are four sets of shelves back-to-back filled with mead and wine. There are in total nine bottles of alto wine, seven bottles of wine, and nine bottles of Nord mead in the basement. There is a single potato in a metal pot hanging from the ceiling near the skill book, and a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") on one of the many food barrels around the room. By the entrance are three stacked boxes holding over fifty [burned books](/wiki/Skyrim:Burned_Book "Skyrim:Burned Book").

## Notes

- The Blue Palace is mentioned in the books *[Walking the World, Vol XI](/wiki/Skyrim:Walking_the_World,_Vol_XI "Skyrim:Walking the World, Vol XI")*, and volumes [v3](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen,_v3 "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen, v3") and [v6](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen,_v6 "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen, v6") of *[The Wolf Queen](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen")* series of books. Walking the World also claims that the Pelagius wing *"has been locked and left alone since shortly after Pelagius's death."* which is proven untrue by the statements of the servants.
- Elisif keeps her position as Jarl if the Stormcloaks win the civil war. If any of the four other Jarls who initially support the Empire are deposed by the Stormcloaks, they will move to the basement of the palace.
- If you are in Solitude, and above level 4, the guards may suggest that you head to the palace, although they aren't complimentary about the people there, *"Been up to the Blue Palace? It's a sight to see. Even if it is filled with fops..."*
- The Pelagius Wing was named after [Emperor Pelagius III](/wiki/Lore:Pelagius_Septim_III "Lore:Pelagius Septim III").
  - Despite being part of the palace, the music that plays in the Pelagius Wing is the same that plays in cities like [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") and Solitude.
    - Also despite being part of the palace, none of the items in the Pelagius Wing are considered owned by the latter, making everything there free to take anytime.
- Once you have completed [The Man Who Cried Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Man_Who_Cried_Wolf "Skyrim:The Man Who Cried Wolf") most of the low value items and ingredients are free to take, with the exception of the bunch of lavender found in the large vase within the waiting room.
  - Completing Sybille Stentor's [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Vampire "Skyrim:Kill the Vampire") will also allow you to take the Staff of Magelight near the Jarl's throne for free without it being considered theft.
- Although several [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") plants can be found outside the building, a good majority of them are unreachable by normal means. This includes the courtyard.
- Except for most barrels and sacks, all containers in the location are [non-respawning](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") and safe to store items in if you wish to.
- Interestingly, Elisif's throne is marked in the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit") as being owned by [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak").

## Bugs

- Several scenes at the Blue Palace make no sense when played after General Tullius is dead because they talk about him as though he's still alive.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.2, addresses this issue. These scenes have now been blocked from running if Tullius is dead.
- One scene between Falk Firebeard and Bryling takes place at the Blue Palace but makes no sense when being run here due to dialogue indicating they should be handling it secretly instead of in front of the entire royal court.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, fixes this bug.
- The activators for the doors to both Elisif's and Sybille's bedrooms are not fully connected to the doors themselves. There is an invisible barrier in the middle of the doors that can be walked around on either side. If you close the doors after entering the rooms, you can walk through the doors, but will be totally blocked from exiting the rooms by an invisible barrier, which is about a foot away from the doors, until the doors are opened. The bug doesn't appear until the doors have been closed for the first time.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.
- The Staff of Magelight here may clip through the pot next to the Jarl's throne.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.8, fixes this bug.
- Two bottles of Spiced Wine are marked as owned by the ServiceSolitudeFruitEvette faction. The wine, however, has already been shipped to the palace and is stored in the kitchen with the rest of the food, so the ownership doesn't make sense anymore.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.2, fixes this bug.
- Exiting the Pelagius Wing during and after The Mind of Madness can cause the game to crash on PS5 and Xbox Series X.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.342, fixes this bug.
- One sample of Lavender and one sample of Deathbell are marked as owned by the MarkarthHagsCureFaction, making them free to take if you help [Bothela](/wiki/Skyrim:Bothela "Skyrim:Bothela"). One single bed is owned by the TownWhiterunFaction, two single beds are owned by the TownMarkarthFaction, and one random instance of farm clothes is marked as owned by [Keerava](/wiki/Skyrim:Keerava "Skyrim:Keerava").
- Unarmed NPCs who are looking for a weapon can access the merchant chest of Sybille Stentor through the floor. They will walk up to the bench to the left of the stairwell down in the basement and seemingly equip the weapon out of nowhere, as the chest is located just underneath, slightly out of the normally accessible area. **?**

# Skyrim:Bodies of Water

## Overview

Lake Honrich

This page lists all the named **bodies of water** (lakes, ponds, rivers, and seas) in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").

## Lakes

:   **[Lake Fjalding](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Fjalding "Skyrim:Lake Fjalding")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A frozen lake near Thirsk Mead Hall. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&x=66298&y=62779)[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")
:   **[Lake Geir](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Geir "Skyrim:Lake Geir")** — A lake in the western Rift. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lake+Geir)
:   **[Lake Honrich](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Honrich "Skyrim:Lake Honrich")** — A lake in the eastern Rift, immediately southwest of Riften. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lake+Honrich)
:   **[Lake Ilinalta](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Ilinalta "Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta")** — A lake in west-central Falkreath Hold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lake+Ilinalta)
:   **[Lake Yorgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Yorgrim "Skyrim:Lake Yorgrim")** — A lake in the eastern part of the Pale. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lake+Yorgrim)

## Ponds

:    **[Clearpine Pond](/wiki/Skyrim:Clearpine_Pond "Skyrim:Clearpine Pond")** — A pond with a small island, located west-southwest of Solitude, just to the northeast of Pinemoon Cave. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Clearpine+Pond)
:    **[Clearspring Tarn](/wiki/Skyrim:Clearspring_Tarn "Skyrim:Clearspring Tarn")** — A small mountain pool on the cliff overlooking Eastmarch, due east of Snapleg Cave and west of Shor's Stone. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Clearspring+Tarn)
:    **[Evergreen Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Evergreen_Grove "Skyrim:Evergreen Grove")** — A grove of trees concealing a small pond fed by a rocky stream, just southwest of Half-Moon Mill. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Evergreen+Grove)
:    **[Mara's Eye Pond](/wiki/Skyrim:Mara%27s_Eye_Pond "Skyrim:Mara's Eye Pond")** — A small lake due east of Gallows Rock. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mara%27s+Eye+Pond)

## Rivers

:   **[Darkwater River](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_River "Skyrim:Darkwater River")** — A river connecting Lake Geir to the White River. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Darkwater+River)
:   **[Harstrad River](/wiki/Skyrim:Harstrad_River "Skyrim:Harstrad River")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A river in northern Solstheim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Harstrad+River)[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")
:   **[Iggnir River](/wiki/Skyrim:Iggnir_River "Skyrim:Iggnir River")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A river in southern Solstheim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Iggnir+River)[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")
:   **[Isild River](/wiki/Skyrim:Isild_River "Skyrim:Isild River")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A river in northern Solstheim on the Felsaad Coast. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Isild+River)[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")
:   **[Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River")** — A river flowing from Markarth to Solitude. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Karth+River)
:   **[River Hjaal](/wiki/Skyrim:River_Hjaal "Skyrim:River Hjaal")** — The main river that flows through the center of Hjaalmarch. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=River+Hjaal)
:   **[River Yorgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:River_Yorgrim "Skyrim:River Yorgrim")** — A river flowing from Lake Yorgrim to Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=River+Yorgrim)
:   **[Treva River](/wiki/Skyrim:Treva_River "Skyrim:Treva River")** — A river in the center of the Rift. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Treva+River)
:   **[White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River")** — The longest river in Skyrim, stretching from the south of the province to the northeast corner. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=White+River)

## Seas

:   **[Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sea_of_Ghosts "Skyrim:Sea of Ghosts")** — A vast ocean to the north of Skyrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sea+of+Ghosts)

## Notes

- The [Special Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition "Skyrim:Special Edition") adds water shaders, giving each one a more realistic look.
- If you ride your [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses "Skyrim:Horses") into a body of water, it will navigate the water very slowly. However, if you take your horse into the water, dismount once it starts swimming and quickly get back on, you'll still be submerged halfway, but your horse will now be able to sprint across the water.

## Bugs

- Water may appear blurry when loading a saved game after creating a save underwater.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.6, fixes this bug.
- The water flow may fail to render properly.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.

Bodil

**Bodil** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [miner](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner_(class) "Skyrim:Miner (class)") who works under [Beitild](/wiki/Skyrim:Beitild "Skyrim:Beitild") at [Iron-Breaker Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron-Breaker_Mine "Skyrim:Iron-Breaker Mine") in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar").

Like her colleague, [Gjak](/wiki/Skyrim:Gjak "Skyrim:Gjak"), she never surfaces from the mine and spends her entire life working, relaxing, or eating.

She wears a pair of [ragged trousers](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragged_Trousers "Skyrim:Ragged Trousers") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#00080699 "Skyrim:Clothing"). She wields a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") and carries [lower-class loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Dialogue

When approached she can say:

:   *"Here to dig. That's all."*
:   *"Dawnstar's got its problems, but as long as the ore is good, I'll stay."*

## Notes

- Bodil actually owns a bedroll located in the mine. However, due to her not having any kind of sleep package set up, she will never been seen using it.

# Skyrim:Bodyguard (Carvains)

## Overview

| Bodyguard | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Race | [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") | Gender | Male |
| Level | PC×0.25 (max=50) | Class | [Soldier](/wiki/Skyrim:Soldier_(class) "Skyrim:Soldier (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | N/A | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000B91A6 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 50-442 | | |
| [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50 | | |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 50-393 | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") |  |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [WEDL03Faction](/wiki/Skyrim:WEDL03Faction "Skyrim:WEDL03Faction"); [WIGenericCrimeFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:WIGenericCrimeFaction "Skyrim:WIGenericCrimeFaction") | | |

.jpg)

The Carvains' bodyguard

This **Bodyguard** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") [soldier](/wiki/Skyrim:Soldier_(class) "Skyrim:Soldier (class)") who can be found guarding [Plautis](/wiki/Skyrim:Plautis_Carvain "Skyrim:Plautis Carvain") and [Salonia](/wiki/Skyrim:Salonia_Carvain "Skyrim:Salonia Carvain") Carvain during a [random encounter](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#On_the_way_to_the_Wedding "Skyrim:World Interactions") in the wilderness. They have traveled from [Cyrodiil](/wiki/Lore:Cyrodiil "Lore:Cyrodiil") to Skyrim in order to participate in the wedding between [Vittoria Vici](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici") and [Asgeir Snow-Shod](/wiki/Skyrim:Asgeir_Snow-Shod "Skyrim:Asgeir Snow-Shod"), but never make it there. According to Plautis the second time you meet him, he is ultimately eaten by a dragon. The bodyguard wears either [Imperial light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Armor "Skyrim:Imperial Light Armor") or [studded Imperial armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Studded_Imperial_Armor "Skyrim:Studded Imperial Armor"), along with [Imperial light boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Boots "Skyrim:Imperial Light Boots") and matching [bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Bracers "Skyrim:Imperial Light Bracers"), and [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Helmet "Skyrim:Imperial Light Helmet"). He carries a matching [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Shield "Skyrim:Imperial Light Shield"), [Imperial sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Sword "Skyrim:Imperial Sword"), and a [torch](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch").

## Notes

- Despite seemingly being an Imperial soldier, Stormcloaks will not attack him on sight. This is due to him not belonging to the normal Civil War-related factions which would normally provoke members of the other side to attack him.
